mynysshe adde augmet shall fynde cause requysyte theyr doynge shall praye god vayne transytory lyfe may brynge vnto perdurable ioye heuen amen thus endeth translatours prologue phere foloweth table hyght noble prowesse large comprised bokes makynge mencyon chyualrye duke name iohan endued wyth sappence yt kynge gouerned fraunce loued honoured hym aboue soo moche sayde euer wente beholde yonder wyse man britaine sworne kynges preuye streayte counsayle kynge onely gouerned noble aduise gret ou stedfastnesse yt euer foude hym duke hadd ryghte noble lady wyfe good holy life doughter erle leycester englande loued togyder ryght feruently cordyall loue al theyr lyfe accomplyshing betwene werkes maryage ordeyned nature fynaltye pleased good lorde sende theym fayre sonne remembraunce good kyng arthur hye renowne named arthur chylde goodly ful greate beaute afterward grew mooste fayre creature founde crystendome duke duches loued hym well entended nothynge onely prouffyte theyr chylde specyally enhaunce honour rych sse phow duke brytayne delyuered sonne arthur gouernaunce prudent knyghte named syr gouernar dyd ensigne goodlye maners dedes armes afterwarde non lyke vnto ca ii wha chyld arthur nyne yere age duke fader delyuered kepte vnder gouernaunce noble gentyl mayster named gouernar ryght prudent puyssaut hardy vertuous vygorous bodye well proued amonge thynges dydde teach noble chylde arthur play chesse table yt non coninge lyke vnto wha xx yere mayster taught hym man skyrmyshe wtin lytle season ther none able copared wt hym thus amended chylde frome daye daye grew goodly yt al worlde none sene lyke nether fayre gracyous ne cou reyse muche yt kynge fraunce desyred oftetymes yt sholde haue noryshed brought vp wyth one chyldren ye duchesse moder coude wyse suffer ne scant let oute presence neuer day loued enterly longe thys chyld soiourned wt moder yt gretlye noyful hert moche therby became ryght pensyfe sore troubled mind gouernar hys mayster demaunded hi cause sorowe good fayth mayster sayd arthur long soiorning abyding home greatly noyeth wolde gladly go play yoder fayre forest hunt chase grete harte hath ben grete season sythe went ony foorthe se ynly sayde gouerner fayre arthur pleaseth ryght wel noble mid go ford pour fader desyre hys lycece ye may go chase ye forest th n arthur went forth duk fader demaunded hym lycence wha duke hard tydyng wyl son grete ioy ryght swete dyd graute hym request commaunded desyred gouernar shold take good hede hym suffre hym enne ne folowe faste dysport gouernar answered wolde take good hede arthur caused ye huters warned make redy greyhoudes houndes raches wo de go nexte daye tymes chase forest nexte mornynge arthur gouernar mouted theyr horse wt grete ioye x gentylmen kepe company arthur mounted grete courser hat hangynge backe lace sylke bonet head hunter wente ledinge greyhoundes houndes thus ryde forthe toward forest grete ioye phow arthur founde forest noble lady wtout socour wt fayre yonge mayde doughter named iehannet lytle lodge whyche made ye brauches tree arthur amorus sayd iehannet cap iii tyme real desert knyght grete power right riche hauiour frendes lord castell called toure knyght named vyciers vertue douted nothige x knyghtes armed valiat corage sin time coude fyrst beare armes neuer knew fayte armes occupyed employed hiselfe euer iustes tornayes dedes armes dyd alowed yt spekige noblest knight world finally led life speded wastest goodes largely theter get hym laude prayse end became therby port tha faynt fell make shyfte owne good lady wyfe dyed grete pouerte whan buryed suche persones detter vnto toke londes goodes perteyned hym lady wyfe good lady wife fledde departed pryuely ye coutree non frendes wyste become thoughte hadde rather lyue poorely straunge countrye ferre fro fredes aqueyntaunce tha endure pouerte owne countrye ben nobly broughte vp lady went doughter age xiiii yeare ryght beautefull porely arayed name hannet trauayled loge theyr iorneys aduenture came forest arthur gouernar vsed chase hunte desolate place forest ferre ony hye way ther two ladyes dyd reste made theym lodge abyde boughes suche thinges coude gette thus contynued space moneth lady went eueri day right porely nexte vylage gete suthe thinges doughter neded fortuned yt day arthur gouernar departed fro courte fader entred sayde foreste anone houndes founde grete harte noble knyghte yt copany named lorde olyuer c folowed harte gret courser huters hym yonge arthur began folowe gou r ar toke hede sholde folowe fast sayde lorde olyuer past f rth hym gon ferre thicke ye foreste arthur gouernar clene loste sight heringe theyr houdes ge folowed fayre esyly log folowed aduenture came place lodge made lady doughter bothe tyme syttynge wythout lodge dore soone arthur sawe lyghted downe hors gouernar wt hym wha lady sawe arthur gretly abashed thought well sholde grete man wt rose arthur right swetely saluted lady like wise agayne tyme aboute thre clocke whan ladye sawe arthur gouernar dyscende theyr horse remembred state fader ge lmen seene owne countree norysshed vp u wherof herte gretely ashamed troubled arthur toke hande moder also set ne togyder arthur demauded yonge mayde sayd fayre swete damoysell name lord helpe syr called iehannet iehane good loue ye borne certayne syr born cou tre moder sayd syr truely doughter sayth sothe truely borne lod desarte castel called tour truly sayd arthur whome doughter god helpe syr knyght right stronge puyssaut tyme loued euer dedes armes acqueted wt many noble men fortune dyed yt lost away wasted londes goodes myne poore wyfe broughte ferre vnder lytell nothing left v death suche persones owed ony thynge peraduenture yt owed nothing tha importune fayne sel al yt whan saw ferre broughte vnder yt nothyng lefte wherby lyue occasion therof caused steale awaye nyght thought leuer go lyke poore woman beggynge straunge countre tha lady gouernour therwith ryght pyteously wept sayd gentyl knyghte nowe come coutre lonely accompanyed wt yog mayde dere doughter wot brought vp fayre place ryche halle chambres lye th bed incorteyned wyth sylke nowe ho eth lye mosse lodge couered wyth grene boughes arthur answered sayde fayre lady dide ye requyre youre frendes helpe socour necessite leste gyue mete drynke clothing mid honorable tha th desolate come strauge coutrye god helpe syr sayd lady pore folkes hath fewe frendes howe ought haue many betwene riche poore wanteth frendes ryche maketh frendes money pore euer put euery place sorowfull creature hath bene grete lady moche honoured haue moche people vnder obeysauce thoughte grete shame requyre ony creature owne cutre helpe soccoure specyally yonge mayde doughter come goodly lygnage ala olde alwayes hath serued ryghte well lyke wt lese tyme ther wt began agayne wepe whan iehanet sawe moder wepe coude abstayne selfe wepyng tenderly whan arthur sawe th full sorowe grete pyte sayd lady right dere lady wepe ye sette youre harte rest fro hesforth wyll stede youre olde lorde good honoure lu e cherish best power whyle iehanet made styll grete la entaco arthur toke yonge mayde armes ryght swetely sayd right dere adye loue abandon youre herte ioye leue sorowe god socoure shall cause haue honoure welth yet eu rcame shal owne good loue wyll take handes delyuer fro pouertye faythfully assuryng kepe honour youre bodye moche youre owne p opre broder wolde myght phowe arthur caused delyuered iehanet moder reuenues yt belonged stang ponde forest wherby stode fayre goodly place pleasure afterward arthur didde often tym resorte thyder passe tyme capit iiii season yt arthur comunycacio wt ladyes ther came mayster forester named pyere also receyuer reuenewes forest al ye day ghte mayster arthur aduenture foud talking wt ladyes incotynent yt arthur sawe hi called hym name demaundyd hi yf receyued yt mawdeleyn tyde ye reuenewes forest pier answered said syr haue alredy comaudement fyue c pounde well quod arthur co maude incontynente delyuer lady doughter also maner place pertayning stang forest wherein thou hast dwelt tyme stage water wylde beastes foreste dyd euer thyder resorte drynke ioynynge water house maners duke gyuen arthur son playe hi forest pyers keper thereof arthur behoue sayde arthur pyers delyuer ii ladyes charge truly kepe honour brig maner deliuer apertenaute goood ladyes man haue taken hades kepyng therfore kepe well truely fayth yt owe lord fader yf knowe yu entende ymagen agaynst lady doughter dyspleasure shall cause suffre foule death warne loke yt lacke thyng syr sayd pyers trust shall demane yt shall wt contente wha arthur ben grete season toke leue lady doughter pyers dyd conduyte said maner bought abylementes iewelles mete drynke best yt coude goten thynges yt couenyent noble lady haue garnysshed euery offyce ye house wt plate syluer wt necessary thynges whan arthur gouernar wer departed fro ladyes rode tracke syr olyuer iryac companye laste mete togyder ferre forest grete depe valey syr olyuer hadde kylled thre grete harte brekynge therwith arthur came hym laughed ryght swetely resorted hunter fro partyes arthur commaunded seruaunt belongynge sayd pyers take one harte bere fro sayd lady doughter seconde arthur dyd gyue abbotte come theym aduenture thirde commaunded sholde conueyed duke fader hadde greate ioye therof phow within viii dayes arthur gouernar wente stange se ladye iehannet doughter capitulo v eyght daye arthur come fro foreste rose erly fayre morninge sayd gouernar frende lette v go leape vppon horse goo se oure damoysell forest two alone gladly syr sayd gouernar arthur toke sparhawke honde gouernar gerfawcon arthur aparayled hym selfe grene silke hatte auayled fresshe chaplet floures heade rode longe sonne rysynge came stang foud lady iehannet ready aparayled ryght nobly pyers forester purueyed thinges necessarye suche ladyes iehannet dronken good wynes taken sustenaunce good mete forgote sorowe wherby beaute newly renewed whan arthur sawe pleased hym moche better tha dyd whan sawe fyrst toke fayre hande sette downe togyder parte meane seaso lady moder gouernar talkynge togyder mornynge fayre clere earth bedewed wyth clere syluer droppes byrddes sange lodiously euery braunche ii yonge lusty louers gretly reioysed great myrthe theyr harte bicause swete season metely suche yonge people playe laughe loued togyder good herte without thinkinge vylany shame eche arthur sayd al laughyng swete damoysell haue ye ony maner louer halfe smilig beholdynge arthur ryghte swetely answered fayth owe owen dere lorde haue one ryghte fayre gracyous swete iehannet fayth yr coutre wherof lorde fayre loue howe called syr dyspleased haue sayde suffycyent presente teme syr wolde ye knew king arthur noble knyght grete vertu syr wolde louer good yf better redy one thig syr assure resembleth ony vnder sonne lyuynge bothe goynge comynge bodye thynges one persone may lykened owne swete fayre damoysell sayd arthur wolde fayne se hym fayth ye ow vylony praye shewe hym promyse faythfully shall loue cherysshe hym ryght derely loue yf yt wyll shalbe one house yf greater lygnage ne rychesse ight dere lorde sayd damoysel hubly thanke howe grea ter gentylman ye thynketh well haue grete honour frendes ye haue ye may se may well ye shall haue knowlege hym soo thus comoned togyder manye thinges tyll tyme arthur sholde retorne courte aboute pryme arthur toke leue lady iehannet gouernar mounted theyr horse rode forth alwayes deuisyng maner damoysell iehannet last arthur sayd mayster howe saye swetnesse damoysell frenes herte sagely gracyo slye answereth euerye demaunde remembrynge also gentyll maner noble countenaunce beawtefull facyon body vysage god helpe mayster thynges manye saemeth vertue causeth loue hyrtely syr sayde gouernar god helpe ye saye trouth myne owne dere lorde take good hede honour remembre grete lorde ye lygnage honoure frendes thinke poore gentylwoman knowlege ye ony vylony body takynge render agayne syr grete synne ye ought therein blamed nother meanes persone mayster sayd arthur praye god neuer helpe yf thynke go aboute dysshonoure wyll loue kepe honoure faythfully lyke case myne owen proper sister without euer desyringe onye velany body rode forthe talkyng til came courte went dyner time nere vpon two clocke phow duke duchesse toke counsell mary theyr sone arthur sente theyr stewarde lady luke ostrige demaunde doughter arthur cap vi wyse arthur soiurned great longe space yt e twyse thri e gouernar wolde ryde stange copany fortuned one day taried lenger tha customed wherfore sought aboute comaundement duke father tydinges coude herde hym gouernar gone togider sporte man wyste whyther duchesse sayd duke syr wote meaneth soone thus goth forth pryuely euery day man tell whyther taketh none gouernar veraylye doubte chylde least sholde set herte loue perso wherby shold haue velony syr yeres sufficient perc iue know fayre perteyning loue wherfore wolde nobly maried tyme xxii yeres age madame quod duke ye haue ryght wysely sayd acorde well thereto whome thinke ye best giue mariage syr sayd ladye minde wel doon demaude fayre perron o ryge trust lady luke moder wyl therof right glad veryly madame sayd duke haue harde saye lady perron hath wyselye demeaned self hath greate blame nyse kepyng company w knight countrey wolde good yt demaunde person hath deserued blame syr sayd lady beleue ye reportes lusteth say god helpe slaundred wrongfully sure eis better maide lyuyng wherfore greate sin reporteth ot erwyse dame sayd duke yf right ioyfull let v send thyder al hast called syr olyuer yt senesshall duke sayde hym syr olyuer wyll ye go ost yge ladye luke desyre b ha e pe ron doughter giue matrymony thur sone syr olyuer prepayred ride forthe x knightes company departed rode forth longe wednesdaye mawdeleyntyde came ostryge whan sir oliuer great hall lady luke acompanyed many great baron ladyes damoysels dyd right reuerently salute lordes baron messenger sent fro duke duchesse britayne lady luke right honourablye dyd receyue hym hys company demaunded cause occasyon comynge phow senesshall demaunded daughter ostryge arthur brytayne request great ioy graunted hym cap vii syr olyuer began hys proposicion sayde righte hye myg ty prynces lorde ladye brytayne hath sed v hither publishe vnto theyr entente ryght desyrous haue loue affinitie well appereth haue harde suche bruce fame lad per doughter wherfore thei haue sent hither presece requyre theyr behalfe gyue doughter perron mariage arthur theyr sone ryght gentyl noble valiaunt madame effecte request name god sayde lady luke humbly thake duke lorde yt wyl please haue wyth v acquentaunce wherof haue right g eat ioye wi h good hert gyue freely doughter perron holly comaudemet madame sayd oliuer dede ought greatly thanked say fayre lady perron acorde mariage syr sayd perron shall euer fulfyl pleasure lady moder certaynly fayre lady doo wysely ensure ye shall coupled yt fayre goodly ladi luke doughter giue syr oliuer hys companye manye noble iewels thinges theyr apoyntment nauntes within viii dayes middell next august phow yt arthur sore dyspleased yt father wold mayr hi ye doughter ostryge bycause sayde yll gouernaunce ca viii senesshal toke le e lady luke fayre perron retorned brytayne whiche tyme founde duke risen fro diner duchesse hi arthur gouernar playing chesse sone duke saw syr oliuer made good cher knight right humblye saluted thanked greatly greate loue gyftes duchesse ostrige done sake shewed lady luke wolde nauntes bring perron redy ap ayled giuen ar hur aboute middell august next insuyng wha arthur herde fader wolde mary stepped forth left playe sayd right dere fader wyll ye marie ye fayre sone sayde duke right nobly good fader vnto wyll ye gyue fayre sone vnto gentil perron ostryge syr noysed hath trespased wt nother knight set ye litle ye wyll gyue perro yl name fame certainly worshyp ne honour none frendes therfore maner wyse wyl take fayre sone sayde moder displesed ne beleue euil reportes yt sayd lad great sin say thinges cannot proued certayne clene mayden therfore wil ye shal haue hir damoisell neuerthelesse pleaseth syr know case found true tha let arthur leue forsake yf dyd neuer suche trespas tha let arthur kepe ought doo hys wyfe hall thys knowen sayd duke wysedome suche thinges lightly done couertly harde know syr sayd gouernar let enquyred wysely presume know matter also let damoysell self wysely examyned yf good wyll kepe selfe yf otherwyse perauenture espied content sayd arthur time left theyr commig matter duke sent comau dementes baron knightes damoysels sholde al redy nauntes bi middes august tha wolde kepe open courte make arthur sone knight marye hym dyspleasure demauded cause displeasure certaynly loue said arthur greater displeasure coulde neuer haue fallen lorde father wil mary forthinke wt al mi herte loue yt haue thinke veryly ye wyl contet therwt displeasure perseth myn herte min owne swete lord sayd iehanet god sake trouble selfe cause certayne like case fallen treatie maried good loue sayd arthur prai whome syr god helpe whome haue clothyng sute ye shall day wedding name god sayd arthur haue great meruayle ye haue sayde great lignage gretly endued wyth hauyour frendes resembleth pointes also howe hath ryche puissaunt vncle wote lordes euery man place serued ryght rychely wyth gre e ioye souper played sported uery n b ste l ed tyll se son go rest past mydnighte duke entred chambre arthur hector gouernar wet se iehannet whan came nere place ange herde greate noyse myrthe instrumentes ound house newly hanged ladyes arayed wt vesture pleasure founde grea e apparayle thoughe kyng sh lde haue come thyder iehann apparayled though sh e haue ryed incotynet wha harde arthur come thyder e came goodly vn meruayle beholde fayre sone arthur saw h r coming herte smyl sa de vnto hymselfe iesu gentyll gracyous metynge god h lpe rather haue company e encombred wyth muste haue therw clepped arm sayd swete loue god fou med worlde nd bett daye h ue nygh syr sa de iehannet god gyue good daye hath done sam nyg shall wyth louer god lykewyse wyth certayn ly sayde arthur repute loue shall ye yt ye saye wyth louer shalbe nerer herte shall praye swete hanet shew louer syr haue redy promysed ou yt ye shall se within thre ayes therfore beseche abyde tyll seaso good wyll sayd arthur taryed longe tyll fayre daye behoued hym departe phowe arthur wedded fayre perron doughter lady luke ostryge protestacion made barony capitulo xi sheweth history howe yt wha arthur hector gouernar parted frome iehannet came courte tyme lordes knyghtes al risen fro theyr rest archebyshop toures ready synge masse solempny se matrymony duke duchesse lordes knyghtes ladyes damoysels dyd conuey ar hur ladye perron chyrche sight people open audyence arthur sayd wyll knowen yt euer fynde trewe suche wordes haue heroe saye lady thoughte wedded houdred thousande tymes yet wyll leue vtterly forsake condycio contente take wyfe none wyse therto wel acorded moder theyre frendes wyth greate solemnyte e wedded togyder grete feaste add ioye made al cyte lady damoyselles dydde daunce made gret ioye myrthe made chaplettes token dyd gyue lordes knyghtes sygne loue phow ladye luke o ryge sente iehannet caused secretly fyrst nyght lye arthur bycause perron mayde ntente yt arthur shold perceyue ca xii must knowe howe dame luke duryng seaso greate ioye myrth made grete thoughte herte bycause knew wel yt doughter perron mayde therfore doubted greatly haue vylonye therfore wyste beste laste called one owne knyghtes whome trusted beste besynesse shewed vnto demenoure perron desyred hym gyue behalfe beste counsayle yt knewe sawe wel howe arthur wolde fayne fynde cause ntente myghte departed fro company syr quod yf arthur fynde mayde doubte vy therfore requyre goddes loue counsayle case knyghte name syr aunsell answered sayd madame syth thus case muste suffered easely may whan dede done tyme take cousayle sage secret shall tell shall dwellynge stange forest poore damoysell ryght fayre yonge hath moder ryght good aucient lady thinke verely good mayde sende vnto moder parte syluer golde promyse doo many thynges wyll ende doughter fyrste nyghte lye wyth arthur mydnyght paste thynke verely ye shall haue yf wysely entreted secretly yf ye haue wha perron sholde layde bedde shal stede tyl arthur slepe shall ryse perron shall lye downe arthur syr sayd lady god sake thynke brynge mater aboute take charyot fyue hondred poundes golde bere vnto moder shewe shall gyue large lo de rente shal mary doughter ryght hyghly soo maye haue nyght tha incon inent knight clepte horse tooke wyth hym golde cha yot caused couered robe vnto stange founde fayre lady doughter dyde salute th ryght swetely drewe theym aparte sayde lady dame come hyther fro ladye luke ostryge ryght enderly sendeth gretynge vnto fro hesforth wyl enspecyall louer frende aboue wyll loue honour sygne loue hathe sente fyue hondreth poundes golde ferthermore promyseth gyue greate londes goodes mary ryght hyely iehanet doughter ye wyll bounte pleasure tyme sende doughter entente lye thys fyrst night arthur brytayne tyll mydnyght case soo perron doughter insoo good poynte wolde e hath trespaced wyth another knyght therfore good lady humbly requyre speciall louer frende mater greate charyte one lady saue ye worshyp honoure another sayde lady thanke lady luke greate loue honour preseteth yf theyr eyther loue honoure case syr knyghte thynketh lacketh loue whan requyreth shame dyshonoure wolde shold sell doughter moneye certaynly shall neuer dye therfore praye bere agayne money god gyue good aduenture iehannet sayd vnto moder madame goddes sake ye dyspleased wyth wordes sauyng grace desyre knyghte keth sellynge lady luke greate noble pryncesse therfore velony sholde spoken yf meeuneestate woman oughte put theyr payne couer hyde suche mater also euery woman helpe sustayn blame defame lady requyreth youre vylonye dooth hyde owne dyshonoure truely dought r quod lady moder yt demeneth wysely chylde blamed yf lady luke haue kept lady perron doughter curyouslye wysely haue doone neclygence renne foly daunger let take worth thanke body selfe madame sayde iehannet harde thynge ouercome youthe yf thys lady perron haue doone amysse yet remebre hath easely swetly noryshed euery creature desyrous de sake madame beholde myghte loue whome ouercome serur floryshyng yougth god loued loued agayne remembre also greate case wherin hath yougth bene noryshed whyche one cam pur e herte amorous loue madame yf trepas mercy fayth yt ow wyll fullfyll yt pleasure lady luke sauyng honour shall put myne ieopardy syr knight take agayne money yf shold take money shoulde sell bodye whych wyll yt freely f r l ue lady luke shall good whan shal please best moder sayd syth ye wyll nedes ye lyst yf foly take aduenture wyll fall therof moche better worth woman poore true folysshe riche ye shall go wyll honour surmouteth al thiges madame yt ye saye trouth requyre suffer let alone syr knyght let v departe tary longe myne owne fayre quod arthur righte good wyll wente bedde phowe iehanne e arthur stede wyfe per wolde suffer hym touche demauded endowrye capitulo xiii wha arthur thus bedde beganne draw nere wyfe knowlege iehannet shall haue fayre endowry draweth nere x thousande pounde dydde put rynge vpon one fyngers ryghte dere lorde sayde iehannet humbly thanke toke charter rynge layde theym vp priuely vnder beddes syde thus iehanet moost parte nyghte wyth arthur grete ioye myrthe vntyll tyme arthur fell slepe slepte al nyghte whyle thus pte iehannet pryuely rose tooke wyth charter perrons endowrye came lady luke ncontinent w co ueyd agayne pryuely theistange moder perron put softly bedde arthur woke tyll fayre daye whan waken sawe perron laye faste slepe hym slepte nyght tyll phowe arthur hector gouernar palays oute theyr beddes thre ye clocke saue onelye hector gouernar whan arthur sawe goodlye gaue good morowe sayd syrs praye l v lepe vpon horse go iehannet wherwyth said well content soo rode forthe semeth ye halfe slepynge cause ye rysen soo early thus slepe clothed n youre bedde syr sayd hanet behoueth doo nere lorde louer whan conuenyente ryse fayre lady yt youre lorde louer dydde retayne true al worlde fayre loue iehanet ye haue sayde shoulde marye certaynly syr ye nyght hath lyen wyth wel fayre lady pray hath gyuen endowrye syr god helpe hathe endowed ryght rychelye hathe gyuen well thys mater tyll came nauntes went palays whych tyme ordes knightes redye apparayled gr ioy feast maruayle think theron whan duke saw arthur son began smyle demaunded hym whether wyfe ded nay syr quod broughte forthe redde openly presence mine vncles arche ysshop yf ought amended beseche let reformed wel sayd sone quod duke syr perron hath delyuered thys nyght past let sente fayre neuew sayd erle bloys lady luke perron broughte forth duke sayd perro fayre doughter arthur husbande thinketh wel profit therefore bring charter dowry arthur gaue night ought refourmed hal amended syr sayd perron suffyseth ryght well therwith ryght well content well doughter sayde duke yet pleaseth shal seene rede syr quod good truth haue whye duke syr surely haue sente trusty enger owne coutrey well fayre doughter quod duke ha dly haue ye doubte fere therof none wolde begyle therfore hardly boldly bring forth therwith gouernar stepped forth herte great mightie velonye doone arthur maister coude ought defende right therwith cast downe gloue said gentil honourable knight duke receyue guage right lord son say damoysell iehannet sayth truth euery thinge knight falsly lieth wyl proue body agaynst payne people yt saw sayd euyll coutenaunce semyng shold wronge wha mou ted theyr horse cried haraude armes yt eche theyr best sayde arthur gouernar myn owne good frede quite lyke valiaunt knight two drewe aparte fro dressed speres restes da e theyr sportes horse sydes met togider rudely yt frusshed theyr speres theyr fi te like hardye knightes ful great valure howbeit syr aunselles valure compared wt gouernar fo gouernar ben man greatly redoubted breking theyr speres past retorninge set theyr hades theyr swerdes gouernar stroke syr aunsell rudely dyd ryu shelde bocle brake great parte harneys swerde entred depe flesshe syr aunsel stroke agayne gouernar helme brake stroke many arces therof stroke glented downe lifte syde ate way great parte harneys ba e sadell god kept entred fleshe gouernar florysshed agayne swearde st oke syr aunsell heyght helme cut ha de sercle stele stroke glenced downe shelde rudely claue middes wt stroke swerde lighte necke horse wher wyth horse sore wounded fell downe e whan syr aunsell felte h rse fallen vnder hym lep foot erde hys hande wherfore gr atly praysed dyd greatlye prayse stroke gouernar wha gouernar saw erthe thou got yt wolde renne enemy horse fote therfore incontinent dyd yght downe fote putte shelde hym wen e sekynge enemy gaue hym hast strake wa e parre cheke stroke dyscended sholder wouded harde bone wherwt syr aunsel constrayned knele right ne e haue fallen al lordes sayd yt theyr coude longe endure stroke gouernar arthur laughed good herte gouernar harde hym wherby te douwbled courage whan syr aunsel felt hymself thus hardly bestad sware mynde wolde au nged stroke therwith lyfte vp hys swerd haue st ken gouernar whan sawe stroke coming put shelde hym aduysed wel syr aunsell arme vp loft wt nawke stroke stroke chief father arthur dere te wyll ye thus loue wha duke saw make great lamentac opened herte rendred many saite ere wi h hi ey n thi season goue nar ap rayled suche necessary thinges metely theyr departyng arthur tooke leue father moder ight sorowful party ge went ieh nnet take leue soone sawe sh ranne toke armes sayd ryght pyteously right swere syr ende herte loue fynde youre herte leue poore orphelme whan arthur harde speke swetely touched nere herte sorow fader moder kynne fynally commaunded god sayd fayre swete loue requyre praye god promysse yf lyue wyll good honour yet euer ye kyste swetely departed mounted horse garmente couered al grene gyrte wt rede lase bothe hector gouernar al sute scarlet hosen eche chaplet theyr hedes lyke yonge lusty louers roode longe tyll oute towne arthur entred grete thought rode musynge greate space whan hector sawe case called gouernar hym sayd frende se ye howe arthur rideth musyng holde beste breke hym thoughte therwith hector called arthur demaunded hym ayled ryde sadly whan arthur harde hym tourned heade hym warde sayde fayre cosyn praye come ryde syde gouernar syde whan arthur betwene sayde frendes haue mused season dreame laste night whan ye woke olde parte surely chefe cause wherefore haue take iorneye herken shal shewe hole dreme thynge hyde fro laste nyght whan fyrste slepe thought moost fayrest place worlde sawe fresshe fountayne thought beau te therof caused syt downe brym therof fayr clere water therof washed face handes fynally cast vp myne eye alofte ryght hand thought sawe richeste pauilion pyghte euer sene hyght pauylyon egle golde richest fayreste coude deuysed properly thoughte sawe egle come downe lyght bosome shewed greate sygne loue pleased muche coudle satysfyed wt beholdynge therof thought flykered aboute wyth wynges sygne grete loue last thought sawe came warde grete griffon foule horrible broughte wyth hym great multytude serpentes wherwt earth aboute couered thought wolde haue taken fro myn egle ryght ferde couered euer loked swetely maner thoughe wolde haue sayde arthur kepe thoughte toke swerde hande fought gryffon al serpentes whome thought suffered moche payne great peryll laste thoughte came turtyll helpe brought many douues parte sawe came sparhawke accopanied wt many faucons dyde suche socoure slewe yt gryffon serpentes sodaynely thoughte egle turtyll hye toure bothe hector gouernar v thoughte came people wtout nombre thoughte lyon foure grete leopardes didde enclyne theym selfe warde didde grete honour al crowned wt golde thought gaue egle frely pleased soo well woulde neuer haue departed wyll fro company euer syth woke herte loue hath ben set ye egle draw herte fro loue entyerly aalonge lyue shall neuer cease trauell laboure tyll haue found verye cause wherfore departed myn owne countree uer ly syr sayd gouernar okeneth ye greate honour shall come syr ye knowe wel lyon ye thoughte dyd gyue egle beest tyail lyon kyng beestes egle kynge foules soo sygnyfycacyon therof kynge shall gyue quene grete payne shall ye fyrst suffer griffo yt woulde haue taken fro youre egle betokeneth grete man wolde haue shall gyuen therfore shall behoue conquere swerde syr gouernar seruaut yt neuer shall fayle whyle lyue shall fayre cosyn sayd hector fayth awe vnto lor e father frendes sayd arthur hartely thanke rode forth theyr waye ye shall vnderstande sygnyfycacyon egle lyon therfor shall leaue season spekyng arthur company rydyng theyr iorney ye shall heare egle tyll tyme shall retourne agayn arthur phow myghty kynge sorolois called emendus helde open courte realme foure puyssa te kynges subiectes ye shall thynges meruaylous capitulo xvii seaso arthur thus rode ye haue herde realme soroloys kyng whiche realme ind ioyning greate see called betee also rede see betwene mesopotanye perse kynge name emendus ryght puyssaunt hauydur frendes vnder four kynges myghty puyssaunt vnder obeysauce helde theyr realmes hym wherof fyrste kynge orquany syde babilon realme extendeth rede see lande full gyauntes second kyng realme mormall whiche lond sodome gomorre extendeth lorde ioynynge dead see kyng myght well brynge batayl better tha hodred fyghtynge men thyrde hathe gouernance realme valefounde obscure darke londe people therof blacke sote extedeth oryent son ryseth whiche people greatly doubted battayle warre without pyte dydde eate raw fleshe lyke dogges fourthe kynge realme ismaelyte extendeth eghypt vnto land femene iiii kinges subiectes mighty kig doroloys emendus hadde w se noble lady named fenyce reason countre yt borne named fenyx bycause coun ree bredde byrde yt called fenyx worlde neuer one sayde whan olde auncyent maketh neste drye thornes heyghte hye mountayne nere sonne hete sonne nest quickeneth flameth fyre bre neth herselfe asshes another fenyx ngendred sayde lady fenyce wyfe kynge emendus quene enherytaunce clere toure whiche noble ryche cyte greate force subdued cytye comeyne costantinople cornite macedonye phesale bo coutre ef denmarche ryght hye mighty pryncesse right good vertuous yt harde haue founde ony ladye comperable fortyned freshe mery moneth maye feast pentecost ye kyng emendus helde open courte cyte cornyte whiche feaste foure foresayd kynges al seuen perres realme thys feast great courte ful peple fyrst day feaste kyng emendus palays lenyng rodde golde yt helde hand aboute hym stode four kynges vii perres accompanyed also wyth hye myghty duke alatre xxiiii erles noble quene fenyce satte hym greate chylde nere tyme delyueraunce kynge orguany behelde well ne e cosyn sayde madam thynke sholde metelye youre grace fro hensforth drawe place kynge wyll ye shall take cha bre thynke youre tyme approcheth fast dede fayre cosyn said quene ye saye ryght truely knowe yet lorde wyll shall lye therto kig answered sayd dede yet determyned place shall lye sayd kynge mormall sage prynce syr wyll cousayle let quene lye porte noyr whan delyuered let chylde borne hyll aduentures syr yf ye thus thinke ye shall wysely fayth quod kyng ualefounde wo e say mater whether better bere chylde thyther youre fyrst chylde harde tell destynye chylde hall yf shall good well one yt borne thyder peraduenture ye aduentures chylde maye suche better hydde kepte secrete openly knowen aduenture lyeth often tymes well yll good well quod kynge emendus madame wyll ye go porte noyre whan ye delyuered wyll chyld borne vp mount perylons knowe destyny chylde shall pthe dyscrypcion facyon sytuacyon mount perylous whiche conquered prowes arthur capitulo xviii moute perylous castell named porte noyre castell ryght stronge grete suyrte made ordeyned proserpyne ye quenes fayry cytuacyon castel suche x legges length ranne gre e ryuer cyrcuyse castell whiche soo epe fro erth bakes hye sca last founde grete stange water fayre grene medowe ioynyng therto conteyned space two myles halfe rode styll syde medowe fynally botome grete valey thee espyed stronge oure closed wt myghty wailes arthur sawe wel howe gate place open soo lyghted horse entred toure wente vp hall way founde creature wherof grete meruayle last arthur harde voyce woman lytle chambre besyde hym cryed ryghte pyteously sayd lady vyrgyn mary helpe send som maner therwith arthur lept chambre found right fayre lady ben drawen aboute chambre yelowe heere drawen cutte head sore b ten yt power helpe selfe chambre stode table redy couered wherreon stode wyne met gret plete wherof arthur grete meruayle demaunded ladye done moch trouble shame whan lady saw arthur herde hym speake sore abasshed afrayde sayd gentyll knyght requyre doo hurte haue harme ynoughe ready fayre lady sayd arthur nothinge afrayde wyll warraunt defede fro enemyes therfore shewe vnto hath thus entreted wyth moche payne lady rose vpo feete sayde syr god helpe departed fro hen ryghte nowe xii knyghtes armed haue thus pyteously arayed ye se thynke haue slayne lorde husbonde haue away wt dere doughter defoule virgynyte yf god doo pouruey remedy well fayre lady quod arthur lord place syr cannot saye whether alyue dead beseche ke aboute thike shall finde hi quycke dead arthur soughte l aboute place last lytle house founde hym handes bound behynde backe sore wounded head sholders hector dydde lose handes gouernar dy serche wounde arthur demaunded hym delt wt syr good fayth quod knyghte knowe none cause laste day straunger dyd ouerthrowe mayster sayd xii knyghtes whe fore thus haue arayed withoute cause haue ledde away doughter shame velany thus talked togyder lorde placr sawe squyer clerke lay dead wherof grete ruth well quod arthur grete outrage come frendes get v harneys whan armed folowed knyghtes rode longe tyll laste found chyef mayster enterynge fayre forest besy damoysell haue fyled arthur escred sayd yll shameful knight hardy yt thou one touche ensure thou shalte come fader sp te th herteto th ntente yt shall take vegeaunce thy trespa therfore defye therwt company lept theyr horse capytayne theym broched horse agenst arthur stroke rudely brake spere fyste thur stroke hym pussauntly speare head en red clene th oughe body wherewt fell downe deade earthe arthur drewe hys swerde smote seconde feruentely p r ed hys third stroke cut hym e sadel fro roke hed fro sholders hector parte stroke one udely entred hys spere hys body fot toke sworde stroke amonge rudely made al knele also gouernar made ii theyr heades ee feldes whan maunt sawe companye thus delate wythall toke flyght drede dethe fledde sayde eche let v saue oure selfe fro deuylls l none erthelye creature soo arthur folowed theym ferther came damoysell shee fast bounden tree dyd owse caused mounte horse one knyghtes sla ne brought agayne fader whan sawe hys doughter herte reuyued kneled downe arthur rendred many gret kyngs arthur toke vp hande remayned ye daye nyghte nexte mornynge hys company toke leue theyre hoost damoysel loued arthur wyth herte departed entered theyr iorney ro e fo th longe tyll cam countree uienne met ssenger hauynge semynge grete haste wyth nelyn hande scochen arm breste boget wyth leteers hang ng sadel bow arthur curte sly dydde salute hym syr sayde verlet god g ue entred foreste varlet shewed theym rode daye coulde fynde house mete drynke theyr horse began waxe late forest acostomable dydde repayre xxx theues dyd robbe aboute coude gette ony praye creature durst stere passe countree specially throughe forest ony thynge late fortune theues encountred stuffe caryages perteynynge arthur hys company incontynent toke al stuffe dyd bette intrete theym conductours therof tyll laste iaket arthur squyre drewe swerde hys power dydde helpe ayed defende maysters stuffe many hym sore wounded therwyth arthur hys company came whan arthur espied seruaunt iacket sore wounded great leoperdy drew swerde stroke fyrste claue h h downe chynne fro seconde stroke head fro thyr e share clene awaye sholders wt arme hector gouernar ryght strongly layd euery syde amonge theues helpe arthur slewe kylled euer theym dead arthur commaunded serche people wont resort vnto thus prowes th e knightes xxx theues brought deth confusion last founde fayre ancient man vnder trelienge naked bounde faste two theynes could help arthur dyd louse gaue hym abylmentes dead bodyes sayde xxx theues whe foreth good man humbly th ked arthur specially sauyng h lyfe arthur copany rode forth trauayled long last founde stronge house knocked longe gate tyll came varlet bare l gged redy go bed place gone theyr restes foresay e varlet demaunded theym knocked fast gate time night good f eende gouernar knight wold fai night haue lodgyng hym h c pany syr sayd varlet please tary wyll go speake lorde mayster shew hym mynde thinke est olde anc ient hath ben dayes good knight yet hie pace quod lor con en thou hast made tary without long wh ent ed come agayne bring worde maner e yt har y armes bere varlet went ayne gate set wide open su arthur copany entre whereof great nede ter varlet beh lde arthur saw w l e gentl man b ing lo g wel fornysshed uaylously fayre e company next sawe hector tyght fayre hie well made also behelde gouernar al poyntes like bigge browne coloure also p rc yued wel theyr ha ney fayre ryche tha r e brought forth var e aune r eyr horse f st va let rne agayne lorde sayd syr th yt borne neuer sawe goodlye knightes specially chief theyr mour bothe fayre ye e ensure seme right great men men noble lygnage wel quod lorde loke thou al haste appa ayle theyr lodginge e serued right honourably well syr quod varlet shal done incontinent lorde sayd lady yt might yse hurt self therfore madame myne sen e pray go make best chere ye canne syr sayde lady right good wil h please shall ladye ose apparayled selfe rygh orsship ryght fayre yonge lady age xi yere whan arthur hector saw rose cu teysly eche dyd salute sat downe betwene theym arthur sayde madame ye haue taken great payne leue co pany lorde come se v syr pleaseth lorde shal therfore come stede hym wold wyth right good wyl haue come hym selfe yf myght haue doone syres ansient wolde sore anoye haue broken reste thus talked dyuerse thinges meane season mete prouided table spred couered washed sat downe arthur lady together hector gouernar hector eyen lady neyther eate drynke whiche arthur gouernar wel espied tha arthur sayd hym frende al yt ye se syr sayd hector haue seen thinges yt yf might wolde fayne mayster hector quod gouernar mane ought euer folow ordre reason beleue ought therwith lefte wordes howe lytle nothinge refrayned hector looke alwayes styll behelde lady tyll tyme go theyr restes toke leues lady thanked great ch made theym nexte day ymes departed entred forest morninge fayre clere warme aboute ende apryl lordes rode forth gret ioy tyll last gouernar sayde hector syr wyl accoplysshed last night ye sayd ye wold gladlye fulfilled youre wyll saye trouth thinke wyll hostes fayre yonge fayth quod hector wold haue ben ight glad haue fulfylled wyl vndoubted fayre gracyous loue herte syr wil quod gouernar fayth sayde hector yt haue ben night myn armes truly syr sayd gouernar yt wil neyther good honest reaso ye good lorde husbad cause rise fro entente honour v kepe v company remebring also honestly receyued v good syr wolde haue done velanye ye good lorde haue hadde hys wyfe vnto dishonoure hys owne house fayth owe vnto god hadde ben well doone yet none honest thoughte syr gouernar quod hector sure ye sage scyence yt ye wyl foly wysdome greate ca neuer touched myl e much say wha loue toucheth wysedome oftentymes ou rcome well al gouernar maketh mater bu yet say sayde yt haue ben wel done gentylma haue doone ye saye rather treason wherwt hector began sore chafed sayde gouernar sayst thou traytour thou liest falsely neu r none drew nere gouernou layd hand swe de sayd gouernar stryke saye ye traytoure ye great man youre noblenesse thynketh wolde ye greater ye yet yt say dede accordinge youre wysshe ben treason remembryng trust confidence good lorde v coloure thereof haue taken wyfe hys dishonour surely say thought noble wyth wordes hector chafed drewe swerde stroke gouernar helme rudely therwyth sore stonyed w th arthur sore dyspleased blamed greatli hector therfore tha gouernar sayde syr stryke fayth owe lorde yf ye doo wyll pardon ye shall haue good ye brynge ye haue done wyl suffre honoure lord arthur great lygnage ye good syr quod hector wolde ye elles great hu te shall soone seene stroke gouernar agayne helme great blowe wt gouernar drew swerde rudelye stroke hector helme good knight began great sore ba ayle betwene two knightes arthur dyd payne wyth fayrenesse depart sore dyspleased chafed eche wyth arthur coud wyse cause leue wha arthur saw drewe swerde stroke hector rudely made stoupe ye necke horse stroke stroke gouernar sore sore aston ed therewith e fallen fro horse arthur wolde haue recouered nother stroke gouernar went hym arthur came hector wolde haue stryken agayne hector sayd cosyn wyll ye doo e ye dyspleased ye veryly sayd arthur ryght sore gouernar shewed folye ye therfore haue stryken hym presence wherof content syr sayde hector repente dyspleased sore yt coude refrayne selfe tyme well quod arthur nowe fro hensforth peace faythe owe lorde father fyrst beginneth shal lese copany also good wyll euer therfore come gouernar make ame de vnto cosyn hector ye haue stryken syr v dyd also helme eche kyssed e entred forthe iorney rode forthe longe tyl passed forest sodaynly encountred knight syr delalaunde messenger met day eche salute syr delalaunde demaunded arthur party madame quod lorde thus comm unde ye loue ye beare vnto ye god apparayle fresshest maner ye come agayne hyther lady dyd comaundement came agayne hym sayd madame wyll also desyre derely ye thynke kepe would great vylany bothe tofore god worlde madame sayd lorde wyll take al synne swere faythfully trouth wil loue kepe derely euer therfore wyll ye thus contynent well syr sayd lady behoueth thus syth madame lord certainly said castelle madame sayde howe doeth know ye come hyder ye syr sayd god helpe ha caused apparayled fresshest maner entent shold please better hath sent hyther entent fu fyll wyl greate courtesy lord loued well hym elfe sent thyng loued best world fulfyll desyre therwith woulde suffre vylany sake therwyth fel away clene foly vnresonable desyre thoughte better leue sensuall wel praysed moche theyr heartes lady rossylon sayd ye marshalles syster fayre ladye trowe yonder knyght hath espyed youre broder ye may se howe faste flyeth course marshall hytte arthur myddes hys ladye blaunche saye ye straunge knyghtes ryghte valyaunte th refore madame goddes sake cause marshal broder absente hym selfe syghtes soo doyng thynke verely shall gret almes dede arthur rusht gretest prease strake ryght hande left gret stroke heauy maruayle none euer abode hym auoyded arson hys sadel fell earth last arthur espyed squy holdyng hys hande spoke great pece olde broken charyot whyche stroke touched wente flatte earth condycyon hadde grewe hys strength vertue vnbarred helmes claue soun der sheldes maruaylously bet downe knightes whome someuer touched astonyed eyther auoyded sadell agayne thyckest prese began agayne fyght fresshely though done nothynge daye soo dradde euery place none durst abyde hym al fledde fro hym soo last came chiefe standarde found marshall dyd hys payne bete downe afore hym whyche time stryken fro gouernar shyelde therwyth arthur strake hym helme rudely draue earthe astonyed arthur toke hys horse gaue hector hys horse fayled hym sore wou ded hector rossylon sayd vnto marshalles syster madame youre broder yll myscheuous ye spake ye may behold straunge knyghtes howe hym yet dooth hynge theym thynke slepeth ye maye se yonder howe styll lyeth grounde al season lay styl earthe sore astonyed greate traunce whan knyghtes hys partye saw hym lye styll vpon grounde feared least bene dead sayde one vnto yonder deuyll thynke wyll confounde v therefore let v depart thys fyelde therwyth al went theyr wayes remayned styll arthur hector gouernar whan yong kynge dolphyn manye saw arthur alone fielde came hym alewed hym sayd syr god kepe best well syr sayde kynge haue ne ryght well therfore myne owne sw te frende requyre ye wyll b one house ye shall companyon syr sayde arthur ryght well euer howe haue lorde already hath nourysshed lyke hys pastaunce sownynge noblenes phowe arthur crownacyon toke leue yonge kynge lordes knightes ladyes damoyselles conuayed hym hys iournay warde great sorow leue company capit xxxii end xv dayes arthur wolde god mooste puyssaunt might ye desyre grete ioye abyde noble company one thynge haue enterprysed yet wote well fynde mine aduenture happenneth haue taryed longe therfore time departe whan herde bawdewyn squyer wyll delyuer hym good true wyll vndertake woulde rather dye mayster sholde take ony hurte domage defaute also knoweth vertues herbes souerayne surgyon name god sayd arthur contente togider arthur betwene rode comoned grete valure yonge kynge malogres erles knyghtes ladyes damoyselles gre e honour amonge maner rode euery daye space thre wekes wtout fyndynge ony aduenture wherof mencyon made phow arthur company aryued erledome brewle marchynge agenst londe sorolois entred cyte brewle whiche besyeg duke orgoule named malaqu bycause ye erle wold let haue doughter maryage wherfore false treson slewe erle cap xxx ii ende iii wekes arthur hys company entred erldome brewle agenst londe soroloys erledome erle noble hauoyre frendes reputed ryghte wyse wyfe noble ladye vertuous hadde name gentyll isabell betwene two fayre gracyous doughter named alyce ioynynge thys erledome marched duchy wherin duke whiche named malaquys cruel man enuyons thys duchy called orgoule thys duke often manye tymes demaunded erle doughter dame alyce haue maryage erle good lady wyfe wolde maner wyse graunte therto bycause euyll condycyons wythin duke whan duke sawe coulde gette fayre lady alyce bare herte grete heate enuy erle father soo muche last thys duke knowlege vpon daye howe erle gone chase forest therby hys prepenced malyce caused earle shamefully slayne murdered whan erle thus myscheuously slayne brought home wyfe whiche ryght sorowful deth made hym honourably buryed sorowfull la noo wyse coulde yly tell slayne grete suspecte duke soo within halfe yere duke came vnto counte e demaunded dame alyce doughter countes e bycause e hym suspecte er e husbonde wolde maner wyse graunte therto also fayre mayden alyce wolde noo wyse haue hym dye therfore whan duke perceiued might haue pleasure g te esp te therof soo defyed coun esse assembled grete hoost yeg cyte brewle wasted al countre rounde aboute greate ci cuy e made hys auowe woulde departe then tyll wonne force thys meane season arthur company arryued countre duke layen syege space yeare cyte accompanyed wyth foure hondred knyghtes besydes seruantes thus rthur company rode thro ghe thys countrye whyche founde exyled put wast mette wyth much people leyng lande whereof gretly ameruayled demaunded two vytaylers mette ledynge vytayle hoost cause exile wasting count e answered hym duke orgoule hadde wasted suche wyse ye fredes sayd arthur pray cause syr sayd wil tell haue nede sel vytayle wyn thereby sustenauce therfore behoueth v saye yll accuse ony per one yf ye wyl knowe ye may e people ye se helpe socour v good lorde sayd arthur wel sayd wyl shall enter cyte syth duke ath besyeged rounde aboute well quod gouerner muste enter one waye thus rode forth tyll laste espyed cyte brewle ryght hye stronge hyghe walles myghty toures rounde aboute cyte sawe tentes pauylyons pyght glysterige standardes streme wauerynge wyth wynde moche people wel atayed warre sayde arthur frendes duke besemynge hath moche people wyll gooe speke wyth hym entre cyte ye saye ryght well sayd hector thentente ye may hym better tyme yf fortune encounter wyth hym felde rode forth streyght vnto great tent duke founde hym standynge wythout sayd tente commau dynge hys senesshall nexte daye betymes make assaute cyte wyth thre hundred halbardes wyth wordes arthur company lyghted theyr horse salewed duke full goodly whan duke sawe theym praysed theym gretly h rte courteysly dydde salewe agayne syr sayde arthur departed countrye herde spekynge warre ye haue moued thre knyghtes fraunce wolde gladly serue noble man retayned wage name god sayde duke ye hyder ryghte hertely welcome thoughe haue people suffycyente yet wyll ryghte gladde retayne house haue wage mete drynke hors harneys ye conquere youre trouth al yt ye say thynke none counsayle sheweth moche reason elles wyll shew syr syth ye haue sayde moche ye haue done wyll desyre praye doo soo moche shewe muche ye haue done ye yet indifferet ye neyther partye therfore ye maye speke boldlyer wyll agree let e incertayne wyll take force brenne syghte syr ye haue ryghte soo sayd arthur syth pleaseth shall goo thys message ryght well content doo whereof thanked greatly uer herde arthur wordes praysed moche loued hym therefore better wente mete arthur syr clarembault sate bothe togider thus arthur hole army toiourned styll without doinge anye thynge space moneth tyme suche hurte recouered helth duke hys hoost lyke wyse laye styll abode company soo fortuned wednesday arthur rysen betymes herde masse stode leanynge wyndowe loked duke hoost se demenynge enemy company hector gouernar syr othes clarembault laste arthur behelde ouer foreste espyed came moche people harneys downe grete mountayne sawe shyeldes helmes shyne agaynst sonne sawe great baner waueryng wyth winde arthur ewed company laste syr clarembault knew baner sayde syr people yonder cometh profyte peter cornu duke broder come helpe hym well sayde arthur welcome may fortune cometh soone therefor hector freende yf abyde suffre hym assemble hys company duke hoost shall haue moche doo therefore counsayle let v go mete theim forest let v shewe maner people syr god helpe sayd syr othes ye haue ryght wel deny ed therfore let v go arme v shortely syr sayd arthur cause people arme pryuely thentent without maye know nothinge therof let v enter priuely forest espyed comynge soo shall hande wyth wa e uysed ordeyned done rode forth ryghte pryuely forest departed theyr companyes busshementes tyll laste theyr enemyes amonge espyed syr othes duke horse assyle ledde ha keper shewed arthur sayde syr beholde yonder best horse al worlde neuer yet werye labour euer sytt th hym take hurte myghty stronge name god sayd arthur duke hath done ryghte well kepe hym soo well longe hath done fayth owe god go seke hym incontynent arthur dressed hym towarde varier ledde horse toke hede arthur toke hym sholdres cast hym f atte grounde toke hors brydell lyghily dyde lepe hym arthur assayed hym fielde foude hym ryght stronge lyght wherof wondersly gladde wolde forge hym moche golde syluer arthur thus proued horse peter cornu duke broder espyed hym anne strake hym behinde vpon ba ke ware whan hector sawe pricked forth towarde hym eche ran mette rudely peter cornu brake spere hector marked hym well put sp thrughout body soo fell downe deed yn place whan p ter yt cornues men sawe assail hector sydes enclosed hym amonge wounded hys horse fell downe vnder hym anone lepte vpon hys fete nobly defended hym soo none durst approche nere hym dyde cast hym knyues swerdes wepens soo wounded hym dyuerse place last gouernar espyed hym sayd arthur syr goddes sake go socour hector cosyn nye g ete mysch f whan arthur herde spurred noble horse assyle lepte fu th xv fo e playne grounde soo rusht amonge theym hande wyth hector encountred fyrst claue hym e chy ne carued heed tethe made hede armes handes flye fyelde therwith hole company da te togyder whereas teryble batayle last gouernar gate good hors brought streyght hector mouted shor ly theron dashte prese dyd meruayles armes confounded euer attayned vnto arthur gouernar marueyles theyr parte syr othes companye behynde dyd full nobly fynally arthur company bate theym well theyre enemyes dyscomfyted taken prysoners beyonde iii score whiche ledde cyte r wle many fledde awaye sore wounded grete nombre theym slayne arthur felowshyp retourned cyte countesse receyued ryght conrteysly grete ioye tryumphe whan e knewe howe duke broder slayne assyle good horse wonne greate ioye erof sayd arthur swete frende ye ouercome myne enemyes one another syr clar bault right sorowful knew death syr peter cornu sayd duke ye haue yll acquayntauce lyt e therby sere ye lyke lese good peter cornu god haue mercy thy soule thus dem aned grea e sorowe arthur dydde moche coulde comforte hym suche escaped batayle fledde duke shewed broder peter cornu slayne men slayne taken good horse assyle taken ledde cyte b ewle wherwyth duke sorowfull coude sustayne hym selfe fe downe traunce whan reuyued sayde swetee broder dere haue ye bought sekynge thys countesse syth ye haue lost lyfe comaunded body broder sholde fette caryed cyte orgoule done solempny buryed duke bewepte deth brother space viii dayes contynually phowe arthur company vtterly dyscomfited duke strake head dydde sende gouernar fayre lady alyce moder promised cap lxxxvii ende viii dayes duke comannded hys people shoulde armed ready apparayled fygher thentente make assaute cyte wherat sayd wolde selfe whan art ur de noyse without duke hoost saw euery man barneys kn rygh well therby entended auale cyte called hi gouernar syr othes sayd frendes let v arme v al let v go encounter e luke comynge assayle cyte lord arthur sayd syr othes goddes sake well aduys ye great multytud people great part oure men sore wounded ye thrugh ho e therfore syr myne aduyse shall yssue let v defende cyte wit syr sayd arthur yt god pl ed wyll haue none proche therfore let v yssue go grea e woode ioynynge he oute towne ty l oure enemyes come wal e let v assemble fyght wyth theym whan shall se oure tyme may yf nede w draw v ayne eyee spite syr sayd hector relay ryght well soo let done souned greate horne noyse therof euery man cyte ranne th yr hernayes suche able soo yssued passed nombre two hondre haubd whan yssued ut wente betwene foreste dyches espyed none du e hoost anone arthur appert ed came foure hondred haub de well arayed warre xxiiii crosbowes also sa e meruaylous grete baner wauerynge wyth wynde dyde shewe syr othes whan sawe knewe ryght well sayde gentyl knyghtes mery baner pertaynynge syr g ce broder lady countesse come londe neorlande sucour lady well good frende sayd arthur ryde afore knowe trouthe whether syr othes rode agreate pace approched nere vnto syr g ce made token pea whan sawe eche put theyr helmes made eche grete feest ioye syr gace demaunded wente warre hys syster duke th b ter god helpe sayd syr othes yet haue better ouer hande thank god reason ayde thre knyghtes god trowe hath sente vnto v aboue al knightes full stroge myghty yonder knyght ye may se sytting assyle whyche duke good horse chefe soueraigne knyght worlde hys chyualry surmounteth thys one day dyd dyscomfyte duke also hath taken syr claremb u prysoner dyscomfyted hys route also hath wonne duke horse assyle ye may se mounted hys backe knyght hym hys cosyn slewe day peter cornu duke broder also knight lytteth assyle good horse hathe promysed lady syster doughter head duke bycause slewe false treason lorde husbonde god thynge formed sayde syr gace gyue hym power accomplishe pronesse let v tyde rode forth route whan arthur sawe dde helme spured forth assyle horse came syr gace eche made grete ioye feast syr gace thauned departe company twayne therefore syr yf please ye shall haue company cosin hector gouernar syr othes ye shall goo along vpon dyches encounter enemyes face face company shal come behynde thyr tentes soo whan ye hande wyll theyr backes wherby ye shall se abashed therby shal lese best halfe theyr hardines syr ye haue ryght well deuysed mater sayd syr gace departed eche fro syr gace hector gouernar goster great offycer duke strake hym soo rudely perced hys herte soo fell downe dead earth duke hector set hande sweede gaue duke suche stroke fayne stoupe downe vnto ye neeke horse duke men fell arthur sydes defended hym lyke noble man gouernar hys parte bette downe knightes sydes whan syr gace saw hym doo well praysed greatly herte hys company freshly ranne vpon duke hooste howe duke company fer aboue wherfore endured muche payne whan hector sawe ryght sorowfull spurred hys horse habandoned hymselfe amonge enemyes gouernar lyke wyse gaue stroke co fo unded euer attayned vnto tyl last horse fayled vnderneth hym fell grounde enemyes fell vpon hym sydes fought fyersly none durst approche hym confounded euer attayned vnto syr gace folowed hym nere euer coude gouernar ouermatched taken prysoner x knightes pertaynynge company syr gace ledde towarde duke tent tyme arthur among tentes cuttynge rope betynge downe pauylyons laste espyed gouernar ledde forth lyke prysoner wherwyth arthur ryght sore dyspleased rushte amonge fyrst encountred wyth departed lyfe body asonder smote heed soo helpe syr gace brought deth al ledde forth syr gouernar soo remounted hym agayne vpon another horse arthur strake soo prese draue asonder sheldes frushed death euer touched soo fledde hym none whiche durst abyde hym without wolde receyue deth syr gace sawe ryght well sayd good lorde knyght thynke pere worlde syr othes gouernar theyr company layde wyth grete heny stroke myght well harde grete space duke people fore afrayed whan perceyued assayled al partes bothe behynde hector fortune dyde entre fleshe greate batayle betwene greate prese bothe party dyd departe theym arthur went serchinge gret thycke preses founde syr gace fote defendynge hym selfe right valyauntlye goue nar doynge hys payne rescowe hym prese grete endured moche payne arthur strake yn thyckest amonge fyers ouerthrewe knyghtes hepas dyde suche noblenesse armes wonder consyder remounted agayne syr gace yn spyte enemyes duke company began wexe feble whan duke perceyued yt ryght sorowful fortuned hym encouter syr hector bete downe syght two knyghtes ther strake hector fyersly ni wyth stroke sore astonyed
