gouernar departed fro arth r rode ii day without fynding ony aduenture thirde daye entred grete forest ryden two leges founde knyght lyeng erath one handes stryken sore wouded backe gr nynge ryght pyteously whan gouernar sawe hym demaunhed ayled hurte hym syr sayd thus hath arayed two armed knightes brethe ne yere paste syth ewe fader broder false treson bycause syster myn yt wolde haue force conueyeng ro vncles place hath bene euer sythe deth father thought haue brought place syr ii knightes vnhappely knowlege thereof lay wayte thus ye se haue arayed armed without harneys also haue lede awaye syster ente defoule dyrgynit whereof sorofull myne owne hurte therfore gentyll knyghte requyre yf ye may kepe vilany goddes sake whiche waye gon sayd gouernar ferre lykelyhode past syr sayd knyght ry en yonder way yet past mountenaunce lege iaket good frende sayd gouernar stop woundes thys knyght tary styl tyl come agayne rode forth fast coude tyl laste espyed fayre valey herde well damoysell cryed helpe made grete lamentacyon one knyghtes helde encene haue pleasure whan gouernar herde crye sayd fa se knyghte charge touche wyll defend ede brother one knightes lepte horse wythoute speking ony word fye sly goue nar brake spere gouernar hyt hym egerly dasht spere body fote fell downe dead wha knyght yt helde damoysell saw broder slayne perceyued wel gouernar cominge toward wyth swerde drawen hand g ete fere yt kneled erth cryed mercy certaynly said gouarnar thou ge st mercy damoysell wil co maude shal tha syr sayd damosel shal lose hed slewe fader thus talked togider came wou ded knight iaket knight sayd vnto gouernar gentyll knyght requyre ou giue fals knight traytour murtherer hath slayne fader broder hath maymed take sayde gouernar ple eth ryght well wounded knyght sayd seruau te come hym fro hous charge take thys traytour lede hym toure e shal rightful iudgemente hym gou rnar toke leue comaunded god wouded knyght wold fayne haue haue taryed night hous wyse coud make hym abyde departed eche wounded knyght wente place dydde rightfull iudgemente prysoner accordyng deseruynge phow gouernar came strog castell called brosse vanquyshed knyght kept howe afterwarde kepte castel agenst wyl grete daunger deth tyll last arthur delyuered ye shall hereafter ca xlii thus whan gouernar departed wounded knyght fro damoysell rode forthe daye longe tyll full none yssued wylde forest founde fayre mddowe sawe hym merueylous fayre castell rounde aboute whiche well pe ceyued pyght freshe tentes goodly pauylyons also sawe many bright helmes shynyng agaynste sonne also well behelde yt pyght en myddes felde grete per wheron hanginge riche goodly shelde gouernar rested hymselfe good space regarde al forsayde thynges wha knyghtes within tentes pauylyons sawe hym standynge muse xii well armed mouted theyr horse wente hym stode right goodly dyd salute hym sayde sir behoueth rendre truage whiche due accostomed place syrs sayde gouerner syr said ther knight passeth place departe must strike fayre shelde also must iust agaynst owner therof syr maner suche place yf knight within ouercome withoute ouercomen shall lese horse harneys shall led fote iuge lymyted case shal cause openlye proclamed sayde behold knyghte vaynquished yf knyght straunger ouercome within shalbe done hym haue deuysed knyghte strauger hath ouercome hym shal lorde castell fayre lady within shall seruauntes loue kepe hym chefe lorde name god sayd gouernar sayde iustyce wyl refuse signorye castel abidynge therin ese frely yf god sende vyctory pauylions mounted theyr horse armed wel nombre two hundred al thei came aboute gouernar said sir ye must iuste sh lde gouernar spurred horse gaue sh lde suche stroke myght well herde grete dystaunce therwith knyght within castel yssued al armed wha gouernar sawe hym come ranne eche knyght gaue gouernar grete stroke brake spere gouernar strake hym soo rudely ba e hym erth ouer horse tayle brused sore fall lyfte arme coude remounte agayne horse without helpe whan knyghtes sawe toke vnarmed hym ledde hym forth fote cyte rendred iustyce aud incontynent proclaymed thrughout al stretes towne behold knight vanquysshed toke gouernar brouhht grete ioye castell encountred hym fayre damoysell lady castell sayd syr ye welcome place requyre nothinge dysmayed syr shall serued byloued lorde place syr one thynge ensure ye shall good surety body euer shall myn owne body syr ye mu abyde styll wyth space two yeres wyt oute soo knyghte ouercome ye haue done hy whiche lorde laste fayre lady sayd gouernar yf godwyl shall abyde space fyue dayes well syr sayde lady wyll none otherwyse ther ore content therwyth well madame saide gouernar trust better al accordynge wyll soone entred castell brydges drawen vp kepte xl knyghtes thentent sholde escape alwayes serued rychely many goodly squyers dyd nothing elles pleasauntely serued hym alwayes coude doo noo wyse coude please hym syth myght goo seke hys lorde arthur wolde sh suffre knyght vaynquysh hym yet many knyghtes came thyder euer ouercame theym thus gouernar abode long space tyll last arthur delyuered hym let v leue speke gouernar etourne agayne arthur phow arthur conquered castell porte noyre prowes slewe kepte entred halle palays wher assayled two grete horr ble lyon grete graunt ouercame wyth grete payne ac eu merua llous aduentures castel right wonderous reherse cap xliii whan arthur departed fro gouernar toke waye erghte hande rode forth iii dayes without findinge ony aduenture ony maner hous place counseyle hoost toke hym sustenaunce hym selfe horse space thre foure dayes thus passed many valeys mo ntaynes horse right wery ye fourth daye founde hydeous ryuer depe perfound bankes hye fro water yt coude se ren yt whiche water rored brayed r n swyf ely none myghte passe wtoute drowning certayne place full grete myghty rockes whiche suche heyght fro valey bynethe toppe myght vnnethes sene whiche rockes soo full vermyn ryuer thereby stanke abhomynably last arthur found lytle way alonge ryue syde lyfte hande whyche rode long tyl hye none espyed lytel streyght waye b twene two mountaynes wh che w meruaylous heyght founde lytell narowe brydge ouer ryuer whiche wt moche payne passed ouer entred streyght causy made stone wherin rode forth euery hade hym grete es foule stynkynge water whiche waye brought h streyght vnto porte noyre whiche strong st castell worlde whan came brydge gate therof founde xii knyghtes armed ho back vi one ende brydge v ende gate xii knyghtes fote holdyng hatch ma st le theyr handes ment kepe none sho de entre castell aboue n bowleweckes stode men warre cro ow w pen defend place al season mout peryllous mayster steuen clerke fay e florence doughter vnto myghty kynge soroloys emendus lien nye space yere abyde comynge knyght sholde acheue al aduentures castel company c stable kepte palayses halle wt castell porte noyre mayster steuen knewe bo e connynge astronomy ye knyght sholde come daye therfore company mounted walles palays se knygh e sholde tha come gate castel porte noyre whan fyest vi knyghtes sawe arth r toke theyr sheldes speces arthur sayd bawdewyn frende haue nede take good hede therfore tari h withou le alone vi knightes ran one n arthur brydge strake speres swerdes felte hurte encountred soo firste spere dyd glyde thrugh body fell owne dead spere breake ronch n thereof strake seconde curteisly oue threwe horse man fell b de brydge water whan thought haue releu se fe ag yne water baw wyn cast downe agayne riuer drow ed tha bawdewy toke spere brought arthur wherwith st ake knyght rudely heade spere perced herte f downe head whan vi ther k ghtes saw yt theyr iii felowes ay e edde backe agayne ouer bry ge went theyr fel wes bri ge fo e arthur folowed sw de hade strake one claue hym sholdres al remena ran one defended hym selfe valyaun ly noo thynge fered f r suche maner hadde g ater g ewe strength courage put hym selfe betwene gate alles dyd hym muche rouble assayled hym sydes euer r ght noblye defended hym selfe gaue stroke made flye f l e heades armes handes euer felled erth neuer rose agayne bawdwyn toke legges dyd caste ouer brydge downe ryuer whe drowned arthur begane chafe waxe angry layde soo faste rounde hym finally slewe saue two fledde gate thought haue e aped arthur hasted hym soo fast theym str ke one theyr heades uped haue entred gate arthur strake h fyerslye backe c aue hym nye asonder w bowle erk wailes dyd caste hym many grete stone ot er pen coude hym n ne hu te bycause hat nere gate w xii knightes whic e n fo e within gate sawe dyscomfyture theyr xii felowes horsbacke done al onely one man ryght sorowful ran one hym grete hatch theyr handes whan arthur sawe fered gretly as le good horse therefore alygh ed delyuered hym bawdewyn badde hym go tye hym wythout brige fore arthur encoutred fyrst made head flye fyeld seconde gaue suche stroke claue head nye teth whan mayster steu walles p lay sawe noble prowes arthur great strok gaue sayd company verely behold yon der noblest knyght worlde shall acheue aduentures place knyghte haue taryed e longe euer thur fyersly fought amonge people bette downe one among one gre e byg thoughe bene g nt ran arthur war ke hym legges pulled h fy ly fell downe togyd r erth arthur fel vnderneth grete churle one ye knightes wha sawe arthur lye erth lyfte vp axe thoughte haue striken arthur hed th hurte ing togider stroke lyght grete deuyll soo hys hugged soule heed flewe earth arthur lepte fete sayde syr thanke thee thou haste delyuered fro muche payne ieopardye syth thou hast delyuered thys gret foule dwe e shal paye anone th mages th rwith lyfte vppe h swerde gaue suche stroke claue head asonder arthur abandoned hym selfe amonge remenaunt fyersly made great plente edes armes fal groud make shorte processe dydde soo moche none xii lefte liue al slayne christened wa er bawdewyn good go fader arthur stepte w ket gate al walles shot caste euer bare wyth shelde well myght tyl la te came fyrste mette wyth loste lyfe dyde meruayles wounder thynke ther threwe ouer walles lept water ynally slayne drowned none lefte loue castell coude find bawdewin right sore trauayled wyth castynge water slayne arthur sayde bawdwyn frende wyll go entre grete palays aduentures sawe hym castel therfore bawdewyn wyll ye abyde h court kepe well horse assyle tyll come agayne syr said bawdewyn goddes sake put youre selfe noo ony place ye thynke ony grea e peryll well said arthur care praye say loke wyse ye come wythout cal tha arthur mouted vp certane greces entre hall palays yt way ye mount peryllous found moost fayre hous euer sene set e aboute ymages f ne go de wyddowes fyne mbre wyth many hys clere wyndowes hall entred chambre moste rychest euer seen forsyth god first made mankynde maner hystorie bataile chambre po trayed golde asure f esshe coloures quyckely aourned wonder behold portrayed god dyde create sonne mone rofe al vii planettes wrought fyne golde syluer sytuacyons heuens wherin pyght many carbuncle precyous stone whiche dyde cast grete clerenes bothe daye nyght saye trouthe moost rychest chambre wonderfullest euer seen worlde proserpyne quene fayry caused thus made also dyuerse beddes wonderfull ryche specyally one whiche stode myddes chambre surmounted beaute vtterbrasses therof grene iasper wyth grete barres golde set full precyous stone crapons fyne syluer enbordered wyth golde postes yuery pomelles corall staues closed bokeram couered wyth crymesyn satyn shetes sylke ryche couerynge e myns clothes cloth golde foure square pyllowes wrought amonge sarasyns curtaynes grene ndall vyroned wyth golde asure rounde aboute bedde laye four carpettes sylke poynted enbrowdred ymages golde foure corner bedde foure condytes meruaylously wrought subtyll entayle whiche yssued swet odour delectable yt al swetenesse world nothynge regarde therof head thy bedde stode ymage golde hys lyfte hande bowe yuery right hande arowe fyne syluer myddes brest lettres sayd thus whan thys ymage shoreth palais shall tourne like whele euer lyeth bedde shall dye without knyghte whome bedde destenyed vnto whan arthur saw noblenesse thys chambre specyally bedde great plesure behold sayd selfe aduentures wold lye downe bedde ferre anye drede death lyeng downe bedde espyed euerye corner chambre gret ymage fine golde standynge eche theym holdynge theyr handes great horne syluer theyr countenance redy blow arthur herde great voyce whyche loude horryble master steue playes wtout castell myght ryght wel voyce sayd behold ende mayster steuen sayd hys company sure ye knyght entred ye palays wt castell god defend hym yll encobraunce al palays bega tremble shake wondersly moche last one iii ymages bega blow horne loud might wel herde space myle palays trembled sore shold haue fallen peces dores windowes ofte tymes dyd open close agayne theyre owne accord arthur hearde aboute gret noyse people though bene thousandemen togyder coulde se creature last perceyued greate lyghte torch euer herde styll noyse people comynge goynge aboute ye bedde also herde brayenge hydeous ryuer yt hym ben oringe wylde see ther felte suche terryble wynde moche payne sustayne hym fete arthur assayed agayne haue layne downe bedde voyce began crye agayne sayd beholde ende seconde ymage began blowe came chambre suche noyse tourment arthur nye defe wyth ye terryble dynne palays began sorer tremble dyde arthur thought surely yt ye palays sholde haue fallen arthur drewe hym towarde bedde wold haue layne hym downe sawe hys ryght hande grete lyon fyers fell comy ge hymwarde ga ige ramp ge deuour hym assayled hy ght rudely wyth hys pawes toke sholder harneys coulde kepe yt sharpe clawes entred fleshe lyon wolde haue taken hi ye heed helde hym lyon sht wyth pawes peces nye ouerthrowen hym ye erth arthur toke strength hym lyon rampige hym put sworde clene thrugh body lyon fell downe deed er arthur yght fore hurte sholder bledde faste approched aga ne bedde haue layde hym downe ye thyrde ymage fyersly dyd blowe h hor e ende therof semy ge arthur yssued lyon greter stronger whan arthur sawe hym cryed god blessyd lady helpe socour hym yll deth soule encombrauce lyon dressed hym towarde arthur strake hym wyth brode pawes arthur helde hym remenaut left shelde lyon shortly brake peces though bene glasse one fete toke arthur ye lyfte syde rased fro gre parte harneys doublet shert gret pece flesh bare rybbes god helped hi tendred mortall lyfe arthur wyth swerde strake lion fote vnder yde therwith lyon fell e th ose agayne arthur recouered another st oke st ake heade shuldres arthur toke fayre cloth sendall laye bedde therwyth wrapped woudes staunched frome bi tdynge approched agayne bedde lye downe test hym sodenly fourth ymage began terrybly blowe horne therwith thu loked behind hi espyed great g aune com ng hi warde xv fote l ngth betynge togeder tethe though bene hamers stri inge stythy hand great axe wherof blade wel th e fote lon whiche longe sharpe would cutte clene sonder euery thynge touched whan thys gyaunt sawe lyon dede sore dyspleased arage rowled vp eyen dashte togyder tethe ran fyerselye arthur thynkynge haue stryken hys head arthur feared moche stroke lepte asyde whereby stroke wente besyde hym dasht panement udely yt blade weapen entred therin iuste heade arthur strake swe de stroke mounted vp agayne wold wyse enter harneysed skynne serpent whiche hard wepen coud empoyre whan arthur saw yt ryght sore displeased lyfte vp swaerde agayne strake giaunt heade rudely didde aualed semed stra e stethy stele arthur fered selfe gretely gyant strake many stroke arthur alwayes watched stroke dydde let theim passe hym wi hout ny hurte domage perceyued ryght well gyaunte dyd light wi h full stroke none way death thus gyant euer pursued arthur haue striken alwayes arthur watched stroke voyded wysely oftentymes strake gyaunt agayne coulde doo hym hurte thus fought grete space ferre fro ryche bedde myddes chambre giaunt grete yre lyfte vp fauchon haue stryken ar hur vpon head stroke came brayeng dasht erth lyke thonder arthur auoyded craftely stroke entred cut asonder greate brase ch stode bedde white yuery stroke desceded downe rth thrughout pauemen gyaunt sore dyspleased weapen en red thrugh bothe wode stone r h hard head therwith b ade fauchon brast clene asonder myddes whan giannt sawe fared lyke fende hell toke handlynge therof cast arthur wysely dyde auoyde lyghted wall chambre wherin stroke entred well fote halfe gyaunte lepte thee brase benche cut asonder wold haue rasshed benche sore bounde cramp n stele ye benche coude remeue stouped pull therat arthur espyed hym serpentes skynne shorte behynde backe vnder skynne dasht swerde bely crosse gyaunt fell downe made terryble braynge whiche myght well herde grete waye arthur recouered hym oth r stroke dasht swerde herte made greter rye ther soule passed awaie deuil hell ye noyse hearde agayne tha sayde beholde thende arthur sore trauayled woudes bledde fast yt much payne sustaine himselfe fete wel might repayred downe ryche bed alwayes swerde hand therwith layd bed ymage gold beddes head bow arowe dyd shote hy te one wyndowes sore yt flewe wide open stroke whiche window yssued suche smoke fume blacke yt made hous darke arthur coude se nothing fume stake abominably arthur nye dead rose suche wynd grete feruent brast glasse windowes lates tyles stone flew hous lyke hayle thodred terrybly al erth shoke pal y trembled like haue gone peces last perceyued brenynge spere al fyre whiche comynge hym warde therwith l pte fro bedde fiedde fro stroke sawe yt w nte lytell chambre fell knyght lay bedde brente hym clene thrugh fyre desceded thrughout bedde chambre al sanke depe erth sodeynly brast asonder two pyllets whiche susteyne couerynge ouer bedde al hole palays began tourne aboute lyke whele arthur ranne ymage golde stode beddes heed enbraced armes ymage remoued noo thinge tourneng palays endured grete space bawdewyn arthur squyer wythout courte pyteously wepte demened tyght grete sorow ye fete mayster thought veryly deed sayd lorde arthur best kni ht moost noble ha moost sage curteyse crea ture euer fourmed nature dyde ye entre vnhappy castell thynke surely ye de nd ye last yt tournynge palays began sece derkenes began auoyde waxe fayre cl ayre peasyble thau arthur sate hym downe vpon ryche beddes syde ryght feble faynt bycause gret oble endured ferefull hor yblenes yt een herde han whan thus wa ed fay e clere voyce sayd agayne twyse y ended y ended wha may ter steuen herde voyce sayd vnto compani veryly aduentures palays ye castell porte noyr acheued therefore sure none otherwyse ye knight eyther dead elles ryght sore wounded wet gadred herbes suche knewe ryght precyous maner wou de made theim gyue vnto arthur fortune fynde hym alyue baudewyn al herde voyce thoughte verely arthur ben dead sayde selfe neyther ye dyspleasure lorde ye feare ony thynge wolde abyde longer yt wo mount vp palays se coude knowe howe lor e dydde vp ye stayres wt swearde hande passed thrugh hall entred cha bre arthur sittynge beddes side bawdewyn glad whan sawe mayster alyue demaunded didde arthur answered said ryght wery sore wounded badewyn ryght sorowfull herte fered gretly leste mortall wounde sayde syr may please shew woudes pleaseth right well sayd ar hur bawdewyn vnarmed hi serched woundes ryght good surgyen wasshed staunched woundes softly dyd anoynt whiche right grete ease ar hur armed hym agayne sayd wolde go se che ferder ouer palays knowe yf ony mo aduent r therwith entred ye chambre yonge varlet acc stomab bef apparayled mete drike rued knightes w dead gate castel whan came arthur kneled downe sayde gentyll knight crye mercy goddes sake saue lyfe pore verlet serued lyuing knightes ye haue slayne thou shalte haue noo hurte sayde arthur condycyon thou wylt tell trouthe whether castell moo men woman syr sayd verlet place noo moo creature onelye two prysoners delyuered maysters whome ye haue slayue kepte hire prison entente shoulde neuer knowen become sente hyther comaundemen duke vygor well good frende sayd arthur brynge varlet conuayed streyght prison closed varlet didde vnlocke al dores whiche w meruaylously wrought laste came grete cofer yren whiche surely made fast wall wt gret bondes barres stele arthur didd muche strength brast open cofer toke prysoners much payne sore charged boltes yren coude stere maner waye wha loused one sayde dere lorde wote ye whether ye haue taken v prison welthe hurte goddes sake rather ye shold put v agayne cofer fyrst strike hedes certaynly sayde arthur haue non entent maner hurt therfore tel whens ye ye borne syr sayde nye ouercome lack mete sore brused withal yt scant speake ony worde therfore syr goddes sake gyue v mete fredes sayd arthur tel whether ony mete drinke hous yes syr sayd varlet hous suffycyent receyue myghty emendus kynge soroloys well sayd arthur go fetche theym parte thereof varlet set vp table dyd set brede wyne mete sufficient dyd eate drynke muche dyd please whan done varlet demauded prysoners wolde shauen answered yes right good wyl varlet apparayled thinge redy good arbour whan shauen varlet brought gownes knyghtes slayne wha apparayled semed wel extraught noble lygnage thee dede ye shall phow arthur yt acheued ye aduetures palays delyuered prysoners yt acheued aduenture yt galary goyng gardin mout perillous might grete barre bet downe ii massyue ymages coper eche holding flayle yt wyght x men myght scant lyfte one fro e th wherwith euer beting wyth greate stroke made enchauntment thentent none sholde passe gardyns mout peryllous fayled ended enchauntementes place cap xliiii arthur delyuered prysoners acheued foresayd aduentures varlet came hym sayd syr trouth ye haue fordone ouercome aduentures place sauynge one ye galery goynge ye gardyn syr yf done euery body myght goo come castell surely ony place well good frende arthur praie bryng thyder syr ryght good wyll sayd ye varlet syr must haue fyrst fyre v ye galery derke se thynge lyghted torch wente forth ferre laste lytell strayte way arthur foude two ymages coper one one syde ye syde eche grete flayle theyr handes wherwith contynually bete downe ryght ye whiche made enchauntement creature coude passe without deth whan arthur sawe toke swerde hande layde myght macomettes wyse stroke might wel herd great waye coude enpayre tha perceyued wel hys swerde coude hym lytel helpe wherfore toke agree bar dore foude laid fast finally bet downe macomettes encha tmet began faile myght seclerely al wyth strayning selfe bataile woundes braste agayne bledyng wherfore fayne vna hi place bawdewin dyde stauch al wouds againe dressed newly wi h swete soft oyntementes wold haue armed hym agayne varlet sayde syr harneys shall hurt wou de hardely leue styll arme surely syr ye nowe good sauegarde though ye wer fader engendred frende sayd arthur loke treson syr waraut payne syr boldly ye may enter gardyn ye shall fynde noble clerke son king pertayning ryghte hye mighty pryncesse th noble florence doughter cyre puyssant king emedus hath bene halfe yere abyde cominge sayde arthur thou wotest thou saist shold haue ony knowlege syr sayd ye varlet tell surely saye therfore let v go thyder wente forth entred gardyn wherin plesure coud thought went forth therin playenge came arthur fayre yoange varlet goodly dyd salute hym sayd syr ye ryght hertelye welcome londe soroloys moost desyred knygh euer gyrde wt swerde good frende sayde arthur place sore desyred syr sayd lode argence fayre frende sayd sore desyred syr yt ca prysoners ye haue delyuered shewe full well arthur know syr god helpe ye better knowen tha ye ware gardyn noble clerke son kyng hath taryed grete season knoweth wel demenour hath ben betwene fayre damoysel iehannet ye departed owne coutre also knoweth ryght well howe ye dyd vyen tournay also wat ye dyd brewle ye made youre cosyn hector duke orgoule name god sayd arthur haue great meruayle howe ye tel thus talkynge came grete flocke knyghtes ye varlet sayd syr yonder sayde lorde coming nay said arthur shall go vnto whiche tyme sayd maister steuen apparyaled matell vyolet chamlet sircote grene satyn furred ermyns soone sawe arthur auayled hys bonet dyd salute hym arthur sayd gentyll mayster grete rebuke noble man ye sholde greate reuerence mayster dyde smyle toke hym hande sayd syr haue olnge trusted welth honour nowe come therfore nowe ye welcome chefe souerayne knyght wyde worlde syr thinke go se palays neuer man entred saue onelye ye fyrste euer entered therto noble valure syr know wel ye sore wouded therfore haue made lytle drynke sente incontynent whan come sayd syr drynke therof hardelye feare nothyng name god desyre youre health honor tha ony creature liuyng arthur toke dranke wel thereof soone spredde abrode vaynes thereby sodeynly hole lustyer euer thought yt strength bled truelye maner vertue herbes ye grace yt ro then forth neuer man yt coude drawe body ony blode onely foule monster brosse wt whome fought great ieopardye ye shall afterwarde phow mayster steuen went arthur palays wtin castell ye entet see wonderfull aduentures arthur acheued cap xlv whan arthur receyued sayde drynke recouered helth mayster steuen toke hym hande sayde syr haue grete desyre go se palays praye let v go thyder went forth togyder folowed wolde last came na owe entre whe e arthur bete downe ii mages coper theyr greate flayles grete season stode behelde euery man assayed remeu one theyr flayles wolde heuye euery man grete meruayle yt might muche myghte one knyght beate downe mighty heuy thing tha entred palays whyche moost fayrest rychest euer sene mannes eye laste entred ryche chambre wher goodly bedde mayster steuen grete meruayle ye inestymable rychesse chambre bedde came theym ii prysoners salute mayster steuen whan mayster sawe knewe one ryght wel made hi good chere sayd syr markes haue ye bene pryner ye syr said truly yt neuew duke bygor wha slayne lorde murdered bretherne false treason tooke thys ether knyght sende v thys place pryuely coude dyd delyuer v knyght kepe thys place al dead prowes knyghte hath delyuered v pryson thraldome thanked god noblenesse escaped f dauger name god sayde mayster g ete nede yt shulde com countre sayd arthur syr draweth fast night warde wherfore hye tyme go souper syr wyll soupe wt chambre syr thanke sayd arthur tell wheder ony thing coueni nte receyue suche pe n ye syr sayd mayster fayth owe pertayn ng hye p yssant rych lady hath sufficient v ye mayster comaunded make redy souper anon table layd maysters seruautes ran h tent mounte peryllous one brought maner thynge nec ssary vessell plate gold syluer grete plente clothes layde wa er brought forth arthur refused w sshe ye mayster son vnto kynge wel syr sayde mayster praye fulfyll desyre truly k ow better estate honour ha ye wene arthur dyd requyred mayster sat wne arthur hym markes b fore sate downe syde table rych ly rued though ben hous noble flores thogh yet payed th yr expences thus arthur sat soupe seamed theym se hym ryghte fayre gracyous aboue euer sawe praysed hym moche theyr hertes wha souped good leysure table taken awaye set downe cosshyns sylke ye mayster sayd arthur syr behold lorde markes shal youre knyght ye haue delyuered oute pryson trouth sayde markes therfore thanke hym well syr sayd foresayde turnay brother duke neuew gret enuy bycause great noblenesse herde repu ed hym oke counsayle affinite det rmined iust lorde brother thetent abate renowne toke company x knightes wha tournay begon company ran one broder ware malicious purpose mo hys company squier wherfore suffred muche payne finally broder deliuered v fro bette downe duke neuew e th brother gentylnesse wold haue done right sore dyspleased bycause beten downe hym day herfoe openly duke pure malice appeled broder treason sayd beten downe tournay crafte false eso broder coulde lenger endure wordes bu sayd fayth syr ye say vntruly neuer thought treson lyfe neyther non creature therwith quarell dyd caste downe gloue fote duke whan duke neuew saw cast gloue nie en aged anger spite stept fete toke grete mace stele likewyse wherby likely haue ben great fray wysely duke appesed bothe partyes right sore dyspleased outrage neuew tha brother sayd duke syr neuewe hath appeled treason therfore beholde lieth gloue defend self qua el treason wtout defiaunce ware hath striken like alse traytour wyl proue body agaynst therfore syr duke lette haue ryght according law armes tha duke neuew greatli blamed euery knight fote sitting vnder oke bycause shadowe therof weder hote wha iiii knightes horsbacke saw arthur one dystranged hym selfe wythout speakyng ony worde ran arthur strake hym shelde grete stroke passed agenst grete toure passed forth ed agayne wyth theyr swerdes hades assayled fyersly arthur al sydes arthur waxed angry toke hand good swerde clarence strake therwith fyrst claue head downe sholdres whan fel w sawe fledde elawes yt n fote sir iseharte neuewe duke bigor fye se fell captayne al copany whan saw one hys knightes slayne cosyn germayn uffed nose bette togyder teth bended browes though ben wode called helme horse wold suffer none copany go sayd wold alone reuenge death hys cosyn therewith mouted horse toke grete speare myghty arthur espied spere stod leuing agaynst tre toke hys hand rode agaynst knyght came rennynge hym mette udely al sheueted theyr speres passed forth without ony hurte yt course whan syr isembarte sawe beten downe felawe wente arthur strake hym shelde swerde stroke bounded agayne whan knyght sawe ryght sorowful sore displeased agayne al myght strake arthur ye myddes shelde rudely swerde brake asonder myddes whan arthur sawe sayd syr knyght ye haue made one two ye haue made shorte swerde longe ye shall se werke arthur strake hi clarece good swerde helme rudely stroke dyde glent downe cut asonde harneys entred fless stroke bare away agrete pece brawne arme whiche stroke heuy descended downe crope horse cut asonder arson sadel gaue horse grete wounde therwith horse man fell downe erth ye knyghtes seruauntes ran helpe hym laye grete whyle traunce whan reuyued sayd arthur syr knyght ye haue wounded slayne cosyn germayne syr promyse faythfully soone shall hole agayne shal render bounte wyll stryke hed sholdres euer mete eyther chyrche ony place longeteth whiche sharp stele wha arthur saw mouth wyde open toke swerde lady rosse gaue hym dasht mouth whan monster felte swerde mouth let go hold helme toke swerd bitwene teth al brake though ben glasse whan arthur saw knew well yf clarence good swerde dyd help lif lost toke good swerde hand monster toke helme one handes sheld hande al nayles perced hys helme lightly though felte nothing dasht arthur sore hand shelde nye fallen stroke coude perce shelde arthur lyfte vp clarence good swerde strake monster therwith head rudely swerde entred therin tha handefull whan monster felte selfe wounded anger bette teth together rouled hys eyen glemed like brondes fy e bette togider fistes made terrible noyse phow kinge emendus sente knight named brysebar acompanied thousand men warre buryed gone al ye people towne sauynge tho yt lodged aboute toure yt left sayd place creature onely coke yt kechyn dressynge theyre mete none yt ware arthur brekinge vp doore toure wythin th arthur companye dyd much brake vp dore entred gardyn tha arthur sayd company syrs go quycklye gate drawe vp brydge wyl go meane season kechyn coke ha ha sayd bawdwin sure yster hathe felte sauour smoke thinketh ryght good whereby hath gette good appetyte wel sayd arthur haue shewed ye shal right wel went togyder gate dyde shytte faste lyfte vp brydges sure tha doubted man mean season arthur entred kech n began crye auaunt hous ye foule rybaude knaues ye shall dye whan coke sawe arthur knewe well vaynquyshed syr fyrmont wyth sore abasshed yt fledde away cri sayd deuyll h brought hym hous iosseran brysebar dore receyued gaue dyscyplyne oughte cotrowled gouernar ba ewyn k pt gate tourned agayne abode one lyue brisebar gouernar toke dead bodyes dydde cast wyndowes batylmentes hye wall syr fyrmont lyenge bere caryed menes shold r passed walle hous arthur hys company passed vnder ye wall arthur company didde cast downe deed bodyes bere whan syr isembartes se uaun e sawe yt knew ryght well duke fortres tak n soo w nt shewed theyr mayster wher withall gretely enraged comaunded haste assayle place thur companye wall defended th mselfe valya tly theyr enemyes dyd l tell pr uayle agaynst arthur oftentymes wyll haue yssued haue fought enemy brisebar wolde suffer hym v rely bene feare company hym selfe wold haue sette open gate whan wi hout saw coude preuayle seased theyr assaute wythdrewe emselfe arthur company w nte vnarmed baw wyn iaket couered e table serued thur felawshyp ryght r c ely hous bothe wyne vytayle suffycyent hole yere thus ryghte well theyr ease remayned xv dayes wtout fere theyre enemyes wythoute ony grete hurte thus wyll leue speake arthur company shewe somewhat mayster steuen phowe mayster steuen vertue arte ygromancy delyuered arthur copany fro peryll dauger duke bygor neuewe ca liii dvryng time arthur knightes wer thus besyeged duke bygors fortresse mayster steuen clerke noble lady florence soroloys noble markes reaso port noyre loking windowes palayes talkynge togyder arthur thinkynge longe hym viii dayes sythe promesse made retour wherfore greate sorowe grete fere leaste slayne foule monster brosse wel sayd mayster steuen felawshyp howe e besyeged castel duke bigor xl thou sande man come castell roche helpe neuew wher ore sayd nothynge study theyr delyueraunce whiche sayd harde without counseyle aduyse gentyll mayster sayd markes whan nede cometh frende knowen fyr goddes sake make hast theyr delyueraunce syr sayd mayster ye shall kepe castel wyll go theym put payne delyuer departed fro markes entered chaumbre toke bokes dyde moche last al thynge demaunded hys connyng caused hym selfe borne hall arthur copany lenyng lokynge oute wyndowes beholdynge duke hoost come lodged hym selfe company aboute palays tyme syr isembart hole able ryde wolde armed soo came duke hys vncle recounted hym al aduenture well fayre neuewe sayde duke take noo thought therfore fayth owe vnto shal dere bought meane season mayster steuen come palays stode behynde arthur ware thereof layde hande sholdre therwyth arthur tourned aboute whan sawe mayster steuen cleped hym armes dydde brysebar iosseran gouernar made hym right greate demaunded howe entered peace well said mayster soeuer ye haue kepte place yet haue doone moche nowe entred mary trouth sayd gouernar elles sore abused thus made greete feaste ioye nyghte ne te mornyng rose betymes loked wyndowes beheld du e host arthur sayde wolde issue g fyght wi h enemyes brisebar wolde su fre hym tyme wende mayster steuen stil abed slepe come chaumbre aboute studye theyr delyueraunce sone bed toke bokes made coniuracions wherby caused tempest winde rayne ryse fal duke host without brast downe tentes ouerthrew pau lion rusht downe standerdes tare downe lodgynges haled asonder rope asht downe al erth wynde blowe vp ayre stremers towel clothes hie syght clene lost arthur compani whan perceyued host hey great meruayle fayre clere mornynge whan storme somewhat seased endured longe al duke host also within castell towne fulfylled fauoure laste seased wether began w xe cleare fayre fortuned suche hadde felte sauour foule mist theyr hertes began fayle full cowardyse fere though th ben chased hondred thousande men armes oftentimes helde towarde fortresse arthur company waye feryng lest wolde haue yssued loked towarde mountaynes theyr heryng de x thousand horne hym selfe ranne oute fielde founde nothynge doo tyme arthur made ende soo retournynge home warde squyer sawe arthur ouercomen al hys enemy thought verely hye prowesse thanked moche sayde syr ye tolde outhe whan ye sayd ye would make pea betwene myne aduersaries nowe amonge yet saye nothynge soo arthur squyer entred place closed fast gate drewe vp bridge wente restes morning squier wente se whyche countrey knyght white shielde slayne ouercome xv knyghtes whych wordes came hearynge mayster steuen brysebar uerely sayde mayster steuen arthur hathe righte gerat valure hym god helpe said brysebar se well ryghte valyaunt knyghte best worlde thus arthur rode forth tyll thre clock foud betwene twoo mountaynes great vylayne huge mightye blacke hery measure bare sholdre great croked leuer whan sawe arthur ranne hym ke horse brydel rayne demaunded hym saying thus fayre syr maner man ye frende sayde arthur knyght straunger ye syr sayd vylayne ye knyght se e ye e pasture haue kepyng good felow sayde arthur go myne aduenture w e g wil bring vnto syr sayde vylaine go ye seeke aduentures yf ye well harted ye da e folowe mee shall brynge vnto straunge aduenture thynke ye dare folowe thynke ye one knightes wyl menace threten whan ye stand chymney warmyng aft souper mornynge forgoten whan bawdwyn herd vyla nt say hys mayster began laughe greatly saide well good owe leade hym whether euer wylt warrant wyl folowe syr sayde vyllayne speake se well oughe ye force myght ye drawe wyne drinke pay shot ye go speake mayster therfore let hym answere yf da e frende sayd arthur bawde squier f le take ye hede whatsoeuer sayth hardely bring w ether euer ye wyll truely shall folowe longe life wyll laste ye syr sayd vylayne yf ye folowe whan cometh nede fere least ye wyl leue runne away lyke cowarde naye sayd arthur promyse faythfully wyll forsake longe may well sayd vylayne come waye forthe promise yf ten suche ye shall bryng thycher none shoulde escape deth lyke wise haue caused mani vylayne wente furth arthur folowed hym laste entred great valley betwene two greate mountaynes foud ly el lodge meat drynk er aualling men vylayne sayd arthur syr knyghte nowe good season ye gyue youre horse repast ye shal fynde mo h us tyl nyghte tyme shall brynge vnto suche longyng whiche shall good shall ye lese lyfe arthur alyghted gaue hys horse meate dyd eate drynke selfe vilayn said syr knight eate drinke great ioye alwayes ensure thys shall laste euer ye shall take whan bawdewyn de vylayn thus alwaye manaced mayster greued right sort sayde thou oule thurle holde thy tonge fro thretenynge thus mayster est thou make abashed thy wordes naye wa ra e taketh lytell e thereto worst thou canst thy malice began oule hys eyen bende browes toke leu r handes wold haue steyken bawdewyn arthur helde sayd frende take hede sq yer sayeth tell fole therfore speke ye wil let hym alone whan good wife lodge herde speake swetely vylayne loth dysplease hym whan vnarmed saw goodly creature loued herte praysed hym moche demaunded hym wheder wente arthur answered sayde good loue folowe good felawe certaynly syr sayd wyfe good felawe moost foul st traytoure lyuynge therfore gentyll knyght haue grete pi ye v terly lost dede yf ye go hym ony ferder foule vylayne othe nothynge watche suche knightes passeth coutre hentent brynge thyther full purpose bringe vnto fro thence neuer none euer returned agayne without deth therfore gentyll knyght returne agayne great losse suche knyght ye seme thus destroyed bawdewyn sayd syr howe fele ye herte wyll ye recule backe agayn el wyll ye goo forth frende sayd arthur euer ony lady damoysell enploye theyr loue yf sayd haue fledde away menacynge foule churlys vylayne nay god helpe rather suffre deth well syr sayd bawdewyn ye thynke loue se wel touched oth wolde thynke lady loue poynt wolde loue myne owne lyfe better tha trust theyr prayse rewarde wyth wordes vylayne came sayd syrs noyse thys cowardy se syr knyght se well herte fayleth ye aboute make couenaunte retourne agayne therfore thynke well ye wyll leue whan nede frende sayde arthur truly shall forsake well sayd vylayne arme shortely let v goo hense last dayes draweth faste onwarde truely therfore make haste phowe great vylayne brought arthur foughte wyth great terryble lyon fynally arthur slewe hym howe foughte wyth greate gyauntesse horryble gyaunt hys prowesse conq ered theym bothe foughte wyth greate gryffon thys begynnynge aduentures towre tenebrous wherein ye shall manye tryble maruaylous thynges whych acheued onelye prowesse valyaunte arthur capi lvii whan arthur well repasted hym selfe hys horse armed hym mounted hys horse folowed sayde vyllayne tyll laste came intoo great valey darke depe say vylayne arthur syr knighte tyde ye ye dare shal folowe arthur rode rode theyr ryght hande hewer woode soone saw arthur vylaine knewe wel brought thyther soule churle tha cryed alowde sayde gentyll knyght goddes sake retourne agayne ye goo ferther ye deed thou foule vylayne praye god thou mayest dye euyl death many noble hast thou caused dye whan bawdewyn herde wordes sayde hys mayster lo ye may remembre loue ye may heare people sayth certaynlye woulde thynke fayrest creature worlde poynt whan arthur herde bawdewyn saye laughed hym saynge thus frende faythe owe vnto lorde fader tell whether goo peryll therin peryll soo euer shall fynde wolde double mouche condicion certayne sawe neuer loued well loue whan foule vylayne herde hym saye herte praysed hym moche knewe well therby valyaunt herte thus rode forth longe tyl last foule churle cryed sayd syr knyght wyll appere ye doo ye shall haue nede defende selfe worde arthur loked lyfte hande sawe comynge hymwarde grete myghty lyon arthur ered horse lest lyon sholde haue slayne hym therfore lyghted downe grounde deliuered horse vnto bawdewyn dressed hym towarde lyon whan lyon perceyued hym lepte strake hym wythe pa e thinkinge confounde arthur put shel e hym lyon stroke dash e theron sore arthur astonyed stroke arthur strake hym clarence good swerde passed hym strake clene tayle whan lyon felte hymselfe hurte habandoned power body agaynst arthur sharpe tethe toke arthur helme entred bokles harneys god wolde touched flesshe fote strake arthur suche stroke vpon shelde ben better shelde hadde bene clouen petes hys fote toke arthur ryghte sholdre arthur swarued hym elles bene torne asonder swaruynge awaye lost greate quarter harneis therwith arthur lift vp good swer dasht vp harde crosse throte lyon therewyth lyon dyd cast greate crye hydeous fel groud starke dead therewith incontynent espyed agayne co myng warde greate gyauntesse wyth great faw hon hande soo well steled nothinge would cut asonder therewith came vntoo arthur strake hym right egerly whan arthur sawe stroke comyng hym quickely caste shelde thys gyauntesse w terribly angry death h r lyon wherefore gaue arthur suche stro e vpon sholdre yt ryght sore astonyed therewithal god wolde fawchon brake asondre two yeres shelde therwith nothynge enpayred whan gyauan esse saw fawchon broken lyft vp gret spere standynge thoughte haue stryken arthur therwith vpon head arthur stepte vnder stroke closed wyth toke arthur head arasshed clene helme rudely braste asonder al buckelles wher withal tyed pull made stepte back warde helme arthur good swerde strake clene thrughout bely therwith fell backwarde soo hasty reuenge lyon came arthur vnarmed wher sole man may anone hasty come enemye whan fell gaue suche crye valey range noyse grete gyaunt make herde wel ranne grete leuer toke hande came rennynge rudely thoughe grete multytude men hadde come gyder made g ete noyse tyme arthur stryken heed giauntesse rouled middes waye dyde set agayne vpon heed whan gyaunte sawe wyfe deed lyon also fared lyke fende hell toke leuer dasht arthur thynkynge h ue stryken hym downe groude arthur stepte asyde yg ly stroke lyght gr te rocke soo rudely handes tynger sore therwith leuer fel hym grou de stouped downe haue taken vp agayne whyle stoupynge downe arthur toke clarence goo swerde gaue vnto hym suche stroke one boystous armes flewe clene felde gyaunte lepte forth toke arthur arme yf e helde ben hadde ben frus ed asonder gaue arthur grete stroke stubbe hurte ar e arthur aduysed hym well vnder arme da clarence good swerde vp hard crosse fell downe starke dead came greate gryffon stryuyned arthur horse cleane throughout al body thought haue borne awaye whan arthur sawe horse hurte hys heart right sorowfull strake gryffon wyth swerde strake asonder legges therwith gryffon flewe away great payne bothe hys legges remained styl vpon horse horse bledde ast fel deade place wherewith arthur ryght sore displeased vylayne came sayd thys maner wyse syr knight thynge whiche remedyed must nedes suffered best wyse man may horse slaine take ye care hym horse ynough ye haue slayn gyaunt g auntes theyr lyon gryffon burfor promise ende draweth fast warde thys nyghte let v go borowe v gyauntes house hereby whyche strong place shall fynd great plen ye good wynes meates ye shall se manye fayre bryghte harneyses also ye shall se heades armes legges fete muche people whyche gyaunte hath taken broughte place alyue gyauntesse woulde neuer wyl eate none meate mannes fles soo entred place daye gyaunt taken knyght brought hym deade place vpon owne horse horse yet lyue whan vylayne saw horse toke hym brydell broughte hym arthur sayde syr knyghte youre owne horse deade therfore gyue horse thanke hertely good felowe sayde arthur bawdewyn dyd shytte faste gate dydde rest theym nyghte next mornynge ensuyng betymes arthur rose armed hym mounted horse vylayne gyuen hym vylayne came forth sayd syr knyght folow wyl go forth go sayd arthur arthur rode forth hym longe daye tyll nere nyght last came myghtie strong toure whiche pertained knyght named sir roger scot vilayne sayd arthur syr knyght good tyme lodge v castel al thys night let v goo entre place one thynge ensure knyghte oweth place moost shamefullest traytoure lyuynge none entreth place shamefully dothe murdre whyle beddes also cosyn germayne duke bygor nouewe syr fyrmount nowe late slayne castell ye roch knyght straunger therefore nowe let se ye wyll whether ye wyll go lodge place well sayde arthur se well lye wythoute shall shrewdly lodged sythe thys knyght lignage ye speke mortall enemy howe yet complayne hym dyd neuer trespasse therefore certaynly wyl go thyther take lodgynge whan vylayne herd say thought wel great corage loued therefore muche herte howe sayde vnto hym syr goddes name soo let v go thyther anye yll come thereby blame maye wythall haue gyuen warnynge thereof entred courte place sone syr roger sawe arthur knew ryghte well certayne howe done soo muche prowesse castell roche slayne syr fyrmont hadde sor wounded syr sembarte hys cosyn neuewe duke bygor herte began tremble great anger notwithstandinge made great outward cleped ki ed arthur sayde syr ye ryghte hertely welcome house god helpe haue ioye commyng manne liuynge hymselfe inwardly sayde yet mydnight haue head cleane sholders vylayne came vnto cryed loude euer could god kep lorde place accordynge hertes desyre wordes sayde thre tymes arthur sayde yf hys hearte good w haue yf otherwyse good god amende arthur brought vp chaumbre dyd warme hym meane tyme knyght syr roger came hys squyer demaunded hym howe maner myght slea arthur make assaulte hym wyl slea v none lyke hym wyde worlde none soore doubted dyd meruaylous dedes armes castell roche syr sayde squyer knowe certaynlye endure hym shall tell shall doo shall make bed night aboue youre toure sette ouer trappe doore dongeon wyll take away bordes bottome bedde stede bordes sette small staues sustayne vp clothes soo whan shall lye downe bedde clothes shall tomble downe dongeon shall soone cast downe squyer slee foule vylayn whan pytte wyll take speres slee elles let v thre foure cawdrons hote scaldyngewater cast downe vpon theyr hedes shall slee wha syr roger herde squyer saye soo ryght well content hym cleped kyssed hym sayd mater ryght well deuysed ye haue sayd shall done therwith vylayne yssued chaumbre arthur grete leuer he necke soone sawe syr roger counseliynge squyer standynge togyd r rownynge corner began escrye sayd maner people ye mater ye thus counseyllynge togyder maryage ware yt noo treason amonge yf shall frusshe downe leuer arthur issued chaumbre whan syr roger sawe hym toke hym hand sayde syr time wasshe handes souper ready syr pleaseth sayde arthur wasshed sate downe table righte well serued vylayne set downe table behynde arthur gaue hym parte al meates drynkes hadde dyde ete drynke excedyngly moche could satysfye hys apetyde souper bawdewyn arthur squyer toke hede horse arthur bedde made place deuysed vyllayne layde hym downe foure quysshens fyre hall hadde wel eaten dronken fel fast slepe snorted ryght sore wherfore syr roger knighte place would haue wakened arthur would suffre caused hym couered grene couerlet let hym lye wha time hym go bedde torch lyghted vp knyght co uayed arthur chaumbre hys taking leue arthur offered wt hys mouthe hym selfe householde redy comaundemente herte inwardly thought redy cause hym lose lyfe whan departed arthur wente bedde layd hym downe bed fell great pytte knyght hys seruauntes readye watchyng doore whan heard russhe entred chaumbre toke bawdewyn dyd caste hym downe hys mayster arthur receyued hym hys armes hurt fallynge downe ose greate crye noyse throughoute place bare speres barres yron caste downe arthur slee pyt euer arthur watched well stroke dyd auoyde well myghte laste reason great noyse vylayne arose oute hys slepe whan hearde great brute wyst well arthur betrayed mounted vp chaumbre greate leuer handes saw wel aboute enforce selfe slea arthur toke leuer strake knyght syr roger ye necke caused tonge hange mouth nye half fote therwith fel pyt arthur vylayne sayd arthur syr knyght gnawe well morsell ye shall haue anone lyft vp leuer agayne st ake syr rogers squyer suche stroke ye hed yt head frusshed harde shulders fell also pyt hys mayster vylayne sayd bawdewyn good sq ter cut hys throte make su e name god sayde arthur shal nede hath ynoughe alreadye vylayn dressed e naunt tha held torch theyr handes gyue lighte dasht theym downe one another fled awaye folowed slew entred kechyn found coke boylyng gret caudron full water haue ben cast arthur tha toke coke armes caste hym cawdron boylynge dyd hold downe leuer sayd thou shalt sethe without salte tyl thou ynough thy flesshe harde den shall broyle cole ran ladder bare arthur pyt tha arthur bawdwin issued soone arthur without ran swerde demaundyd place god helpe syr sayd vylayne trowe light vp torch descended downe found olde house ful deade mennes bone traytours place slayne name god sayd arthur vylayne ye haue holpen lyke frende al vn urteis wordes wel sayd vylayne wyl ye scape morow aduentur whether shal bring whyche thynke ye shall promyse thynge suche shall desyre frende sayd arthur promise vttermost power shal thing ye desire yf knight may wythout reproche vylany well sayd vylayne beleue promise shall nede though ye maner made yro yet thinke ye shuld scape fro death nighte shall kepe fro daunger made arthur fayre bedde lay nyghte flore hym e night chamberlaine euer lyfe afterwarde arthur dyd muche good thus went bedde toke theyr rest tyll next mornyng arthur rose phowe next mornynge vylaine brought arthur another aduenture nye toure tenebrous firste assailed wyth terrible monstrous byrdes greate griffon without nombre yt assailed xxiiii knightes b prowes slew also bet e gret homet brasse whyche issued oute wynd tourned great myllstones lyke powder also entred castell tenebrous quenched fyre cause great darkenes conteyned circuite v leges compasse ye shal afterward capto lviii ye next morning betimes arthur rose armed mouted horse toke wateuer folowing vilayn rode forth tyl thre clock entred great valey euer rode lowe lower fayre seaso sonne shone clere tyme ryden twoo leges halfe much darknes clene lost sight sonne also day dark though aboute midnyght vilayne sayd arthur syr knight ye tel fro whens al thys darknes cometh ye make clere shal ye get thereby perpetual honour know certayn yet neuer none euer entred ferder euer retourned agayne therefore youre hert fayle enter ferder ye ye shall dye haue done frende sayd arthur howe darkenes thys place wyl tell sayd vylayne rede sage wise standeth wel hand therwith arthur departed fro entred derkenes vylayn bawdewyn abode styll beginninge derkenes lost syght arthur myght se shynynge sheld farre one myght shote arowe thus rode forth well space halfe lege last foud ryuer great depe black pitch bankes hye vnneth water mighte sene runnynge vnderneth full serpentes lydardes none could entre amonge without slayne aboue head flewe monstrous bl de diuers griffon wer able beare away armed knyght hors al great multitude though thei ben sta ling arthur dydde couer head sheld griffon dasht therat talentes anoyed bothe arthur horse righte sore euer arthur florysshed hym wyth hys good sword clarence euer touched dyd hym hurt also fly grea nu te blacke pytche stange hym horse ryghte sore bloud yssued af er bene clerenes shelde bene slayne men liues bryght shynyng therof mighte well rounde aboute hym perceyue well whan thinges came warde wherby made good de ence possible thus rode longe season yuer syde last found lytel strayte way must nedes passe without would haue tourned agayne last arthur dasht strayte way anon vermin ran hors shortly w ful though bene fly souked muche bloud hors began wax feble wha arthur sawe horse would fayl hasted fast might get oute strayte waye wyth moche payn egal hors therof incontinent horse fel wn dead tha arthur set fete ye erth well might tha came knyght arthur ware hit sheld whiche helde fast hande therfore stroke dyd g ent spere helde brake knyght passed forth arthur toke hym rayne brydell caught hym arme pulled hym rudely made auoyde horse soo fell downe water drowned deuoured foule vermyn therin arthur lepte knyghtes horse toke spere knyght cryed sayd syr knyght beware arthur tourned encoutred hym knyght brake spere arthur strake hym rudely yt spere went clene thrughout hys body fell downe deed ran hym x knyghtes al one strake al sydes great myghty stroke tha toke good swerde strake one soo rudely claue hym clene sholdres claue sholders downe backe bone delte amonge stroke confounded l attayned vnto tyme hadde great nede herbes mayster steuen gaue hym also whyte shelde good swerde dyd hym good seruyce suche knyghtes hadde slayne chosen ryght puyssaut arthur chyualrye surmounted dydde muche wyth handes slewe yt euer agaynst hym rusht forth horse wyst whether til last hearde gryndynge togyther two milstones one vpon another myll wherby earth arthur shake cause stone went thus aboute stode great fat brasse wherin great machomet syttynge vpon barre yren made enchauntement blewe hym soo greate wynde stone turned therby swyftly creature could passe wythout death arthur approched mylstones felte terryble wynde fayne alyght downe horse wente fote well myght sawe wel coude come nere stone without dye therfore went rounde aboute se wayes myght come last founde lytle brydge whiche narowe yt one man could passe another vnder thys brydge great pyt botom therof could perceyued also xii knyghtes kepte thys brydge vi one ende vi armed wt o owes hatch e stele theyr handes wha vi fyrst knyghtes sawe arthur ran hym one gaue hym many great stroke hys shelde neuer could enpayre toke good swerd strake fyrst yt claue heed asonder fro seconde stroke arme clene wt sholdre fro thyrde beraue head whan ye thre saw theyr felowes slayne nothinge coulde endure ayenst hym fledd towarde bridge arthur ouertoke hyndermest hys brayne lewe clene felde seconde haste lepte pyt brake h necke thyrde ouertoke brydge toke hym hys armes dyd cast hym ouer brydge downe pyt dyed myserablye therwyth hasted hym ouer brydge vi ranne one hym thought haue dasht downe pyt arthur lyke valiaunt knight lept amonge layde swerde round aboute hym suche wyse within shorte space departed life death asonder v theym syxt kneled downe arthur besought mercye prayed goddes sake would sle hym take fere sayde arthur thy lyfe saued soo yt thou wylt tell fro whence grete wynde cometh syr sayde cometh yonder great vessell brasse ye may se yonder therein macho met made lether syttyng gret barre yron made crafte enchauntmente soo coulde ouer tourne machomet wynd shold cease well sayde arthur abyde styll wyl go se phow arthur bette grete machomet syttynge vessell brasse therebye wynde ceased capitulo lix arthur wence forth thought haue gone boldly vessell brasse ye wynd byg fayn lie ye erth alonge crepe handes fe e tyll came vessell drewe hym shielde swerd longe spere dasht therwith machomet rudely many stroke ye last foule machomet ouerthrew vp vessell incontinent enchauntment ceased stone stode styll maner wynd arthur stode vp fete came agayn knight demaunded hym towre yt sawe stande derke season lyght reason shyning sheld tha knyght answered sayd sir duke bygor hath neuew named syr isembart lorde place hath suche enuy people caused tour made subtyll enchaunter grete darknes ye haue bene whiche endureth v leges circuite compas land ayred sowed space syxe yeres paste suche people wont dwell therin fledde away famisshed ho g e enchaunte craft also made riuer yt ye haue passed neuer man dyd thys tyme withoute death euer thys darknes hath contynua ly endured sauyng one day yere new yere day whyche daye vi knightes ye haue slayne est knightes coulde found th lande nowe haue found mayster whiche knightes dyd prouyde v ye sayd day th nges nedefull v haue al company wer al numbre xii person w kept alway passage betwene mylstones whyche turned euer rest sauyng saynt martyns da e might passe fore sayd vi knightes fetche thynges prouided v al hole yere toure beset roud knyghtes milstones wynd wt darkenes maner impossible entre toure wtoute death well sayde arthur shewe vnto cause whence co meth al darknes syr sayd co meth greate pi ce toure greate gryffons descendeth downe thys pyt bottome therof great hideous fyre made crafte man tell whych e ryseth blacke thicke fume smoke whych ryseth p certayne dores wyndowes wherby light son brighte skye quenched euer contynually darke derknes conteineth circuite v leges compasse haue shewed wherfore country clene wasted destroied people fledde therof sayd arthur cruelte certaynly said knight shal shewe trouth abbey white monkes wont reputed ryghte noble great possessyons comonly kynges prynces whan paste place would rest herbour well serued named abbey grace dieu abbot right wise man noble brother vnto lorde argenton falslye slayne treason duke neuew whych fortuned come sayde abbey vpon ester day fore none seaso abbot al hole couent solemne processyon couent fyrst comyng leue seruyce god haue layde table haue brought meate drynke haue fylled paunche therfore displesed incontynent lepte horse departyng false enchauter hym whan abbot knewe soone myghte came hym desyred atye wyse could make hym chaunge purpose shamefullest wyse could rebuked called foule rotten chur e promysynge greate dyspleasure could lye hys power doo hath done ye may se hath caused euer lyth lyue great darknes also hath taken theym theyr rente possessyons helde vnder hym rule al londe argenton al cyrcuyte labourer coulde laboure theyr lyuyng lacke lyghte wherefore many famisshed hunger saye trouth thys sayde abbey seruyce god hath minys red fyue yere well sayd arthur greate domage praye th tell howe may darkenes fordone syr sayd knyght enchaunter whan made fyre ryghte sore dysplesed sprang oute earthe euen terryble fyre fayre fountayne wherby right well knew fyre quenched anye knyghte myghte attayne come therto cast water therof fyre al darknes cease euermore phow arthur entred toure tenebrous quenched fyre wherby terryble enchauntemente ceased cap lx arthur sayd frend brynge sayd toure wente arthur folowed hym wente fast greate wyndowes dores toure xv speres length square whyche yssued soo great haboundaunce fume bryght shelde lost clene shynyng wherfore sore troubled could se maner thynge dyd muche gropyng laste came iuste toure founde walles pyght ful sharpe barres yren set thicke prickes vrchins skyn length halfe spere thentent creature approche nere walles none entre lytle wycket moche payne knyght dyd open whan opened yssued greate haboundaunce smoke derkenes therby doubled throughout countre neyther candell torche coulde brenne place neuerthelesse arthur entred wycket left knyght wythout smoke hete ryght greuous hym yf ben valure hym ony bene clene ouercome alwayes went downewarde stayres sawe nothyng felt manye greate stroke oftentymes thereby constrayned knele hys knee coulde tell whens came dydde gyue hym euer flourysshed aboute wyth swerd auayled hym nothynge strake wyst wherat fynally fayne couer head wyth hys shelde elles ben sshed thoughe ben yren alwayes thus wente euer downwarde stayres tyll laste came downe botom founde fayre greate fawte felt great hete swette therby nye ouercome felte aboute hym perceyued nye fyre went ferder founde fountayne reason colde ayre yt felte wherof ryght gladde soo toke shelde plunged water bare muche water therin coulde dyd caste fyre euer fetched water contynually dyde caste fyre euer fyre quenched darkenes began mynysshe water dydde caste fyre clerer lyght began waxe conclusion dydde caste soo muche water fyre clene quenched myght se clerely aboute hym perceyued bothe sydes stayres stode greate ymages brasse holdynge theyr handes greate mace stele whyche doone hym moche trouble wente downewarde theyr power ended whan fyre quenched enchauntement fynysshed arthur wha sawe done retourned vp agayne stayres ryghte wery hys trauayle e swetynge greate stroke receyued came agayne lytle wycket knyghte styll abydynge whan sawe arthur hole sounde lyue kneled downe hym sayd syr ye welcome chefe floure chyualry worlde arthur set hym downe vpon grene grasse take brethe helme shelde thus countre clene delyuered fro darkenes soo euery bodye myght se clerely aboute theym wherof abbot hys couent great ioye went rendred thankes almyghty god theyr churche abbot sayd bretherne syrs let v go se hym hath thus delyuered v fro thralldome yf god wyll gyue v grace fynde hym verely thynke gentyl knyght yt porte noyre abbot al couent yssued abbey wy h comyn processyon came sayd toure whyche ferre then founde arthur syttynge grounde knyght hym whan arthur sawe toke hym hys shelde helme hys spere hys hande whan couent wyth processyo came hym kneled downe crosse couente kneled downe hym woulde aryse tyll vpon fete came bawdewyn wyth hym foule greate vylayne hadde broughte arthur forsayd aduen ures whan bawdewyn sawe procession al monkes thought veryly arthur bene dead began cry braye make sorow world sayd na vnhappy creature thus haue lost lord mayster floure al worlde noble thyualry ala death doost thou take thus made thys great sorow last espyed arthur wheras stode hys heart came hym agayne abbot came arthur sayd ryght noble vertuous knight ye ryght hertely welcome hath delyuered v th countre suche tou mente pryson longe space pleasure god meanes seruyce god hen forth hall mynystred churche syr hole couent hartely de come take rest wythin oure abbey great trauayle arthur ryght good wyll dyd graut wery bawdewyn toke shelde great vylayn toke hys spere helme often tymes sayd vnto hym gentyll knyghte god gyue ioye encreace thyn honour bounte thou haste acheued neuer man could thys tyme therfore nowe pleasure god hye prowesse fayre damoysell argenton shall delyuered oute trouble e oute ha de duke bygors neuewe thou haste promysed goo euer shall brynge therfore desyre kepe thy promyse well sayde arthur ensure faythfully wyll breake promyse sir said abbot god gyue grace brynge lady thraldome knowe well ye haue prowesse suffycyent acheue enterpryse thoughe greater mater trouth sayd vylayne hath ben tight well proued haue broughte hym place harde aduenture hath ben proue therby chyualry noble vertue duke neuewe greately redoubted doubte shall well chastysed soo therwyth wente abbey abbot made theym ryght great honoure therfore belle church ronge continually thre dayes thre nightes greate ioye lytell space arthur bawdwyn gr vylaine sported great feast ioy tyme let v leue arthur abbey let v speke mighty kyng emendus faire florence doughter phow brisebar mayster steuen wer departed fro arthur fro ye porte noyre aryued cornite king emendus company emperoure ynde foure knyghtes holdynge time great sumptuous ope court mayster steuen brysebar recounted al open audyence noble chyualry arthur meane season came cour e knight armed broughte tydynges kynge howe aduentures toure tenebrous acheued onely prowes one noble knyght capitulo lxi whan mighty kyng emendus hadde holden gret solemne court afest ester gret citie called sabary xv daye ester th emperour would haue departed kyng would suffre entreted hym fayre con nt abyde soo determyned kepe theyr whytsontyde cornyte dyd time kynge kepte moost sumptuous open courte kepte syth kyng soo thus emperour abode st wyth kyng tyl time whytsontyde tyme kynge sente noble hys realme sayd feast citie cornite whan daye approched kynge wyth h noble company rode cornite mette noble doughter gentyll florence accompanyed ye archebys hop cornite vncle brother vnto kyng father citie r ally replentished kynges knightes whan kyng entred alighted downe peryo soo unted vp palays nexte day emperou e came thyther kynge florence doughter hys hole bar ay dyd encountre conuey hym lodgynge whych abbey saynt quintine kyng f orence retourned agayne vnto theyr palays thyrde daye feast came cour e kynge orqueney noble kyng mormall kynge valefoude kyng sabary also thyther came lord neuelon sene shal vnto fayre floren e syr ncean neuewe lorde poole syr steuen syr mile valef unde lord ma syr artaude lorde arsate syr moraut lorde fenisse syr olyuer lorde sabary also syr ultier lorde amaso syr mo li scot syr sanxton oste retinue noble florence many greate parte theym fayne lodged wythoute cytye court full ple teous neuer seene none suche kynge caused cried whosoeuer would take hym noble ordre knyghthode shoulde dubbed knighte hys handes nexte daye whych fyrst day feast began courte soo muche feast ioye neuer sene courte whytsondaye masse kynge made hys palays fyfty newe knyghtes vnto whome dydde gyue armes horse harneys florence dyd gyue gownes skarlet mantelles grene furred wyth ermynes soo new knyghtes standynge kinge dyd gyrde aboute theyr swerdes ryghte swetely laughyng dyd giue neck stroke knyghthode florence dydde lace theyr mantelles theyr neckes emperour dyd make lodgynge xl knyghtes four kinges eche made x x knightes emperour othe kynges dyd mount horsebacke new knightes wy h soo came palays began horne bussynnes blowe ta oures ebeckes instrume te sowne make moost melody world assemble together al iuglers tomblers al resorted palays whan assembled courte numbre two hundred x newe knightes kynge emperour sate downe fayre florence betwene al oth kinges set eche g e iuglers mynstrelles began make ioye feast ladyes damoyselles began daunce lordes knyghtes dyd iuste ournay trompe te clario othe instrumentes musyke began sown cyte hanged cloth golde ryche arays great myrth ioy alyghted peryon syr brysebar mayster steuen remaynynge castell eynarte two leges then made pea betwene burg y towne meane people ben longe discorde whan syr brisebar mouted vpon palays baron knyghtes ran welcomed hym made hys comyng great ioye feest specyally syr neuelon senesshall syr ancell syr myles valifounde made hym suche chere yt prese greate payne come kyng soone kynge sawe hym made great ioy toke hym hande caused hym syt downe hym al courte ryght ioyfull hys comyng none lacking al florence knyghtes arthur kynge sayd syr brisebar ye sent hyther heed foule great mo ster whyche slayne thanked god pray tell conquered syr sayd brysebar grace sent thyther wyth great company dyd nothynge founde fyghtyng wyth monster moost gentyl knyght yt lyueth moost freest herte moost curteyse swete amyable moost valyaut redoubted knyght euer gyrt wyth swerd l stroke monster heed syghte dyd suche prowesse armes manne like name god quod kynge great valure one man bryng deth suche foule beest syr sayd br sebar ye know valure hye prowesse whiche thys knyght onely hath acheued straunge aduentures th porte noyre wyth body dyd maruayles roche syr fyrmont v hondred mo dyd laye wayte hym lepte shyppe full hys enemyes whan perceyued company taken prysoners ledde forth castell sustayned onely medlynge amonge enemyes whyche ye comynalte towne roche countre aboute slewe syr fyrmont thre hondred hys companye rescowed v pryson also rescowed knyght plash hys enemyes wyll ye shall saye floure chyualry pere worlde hadde scant vttred wordes came palays knyght armed dressed hym knyge sayde ryght hye myghty puyssaut kynge haue brought vnto good true tydynges straunge aduentures tenebrous toure acheued enchauntementes clene fordon greate darkenes tourned lyght bryghtnes knyghtes kepte toure slayne great lion gyaunt gyauntesse slayne countre deliuered fro al harde aduentures longe endured fayre rend sayd kynge hathe done thys dede syr hath done knyght al onely wereth whyte shelde certayne sawe hym vnarmed abbey grace di neuer syth god borne hath bene seen soo fayre creature gentyll gracyous whan florence herde spekyng whyte shelde thought veryly yt shelde whiche pauylyon porte noyre thought veryly frende louer arthur bare whome herde muche good reported thus wyth owne thought herte trebled sodenly therby blusshed made semblaut se fe sayd swete frende noble true hert whan shall se may speke wyth good leyser king sayd name god thys knyght right valyaut cause syr brisebar ye brought ye court wyth thentent myght acquaynted wyth hym myght ou f ende hys god helpe sayde kynge orqueney greate rychesse haue suche shelde nere v veryly parte rather haue co panye hym rychest persone nowe lyuyng syr b ysebar ye dyd ryght yll youre uoyre whan ye dyd yo r payne bringe courte syr sayd brysebar fayth owe v omy lorde kynge dyd beste power haue brought hym hyther answered yt must nedes go fyrst toure tenebrous sayd god gyue hym grace thereto escape adueture wold mawdela ntyde argence make battayle ayenst syr isembarte ye duke bygors neuew fayre mayden argentons sake shewed yt promysed vncle markes mayster steuen wolde best hys power get agayne fayre ladyes herytage wolde shewe vnto duke neuewe falsly vntruly dysheryted f lse treason slayne lorde argenton father trouth sayd knight brought thyther tydynges fro n brous toure waraunt hym shall ryght well helpe lady ryght fayth yt owe vnto god sayd kyng orqueney yf suche batayle shall yf god wyll shall b wythout veryly wyll therat tyme syr sayd phylyp orqueney fayre vncle suffre go truly wyll also quod syr nephelo wyl behynd sayd brisebar yf god pleased ther shal se maruayles knight tha ye court ther bega grete parlyament amonge knyghtes faythful auowynge go sayd iourney one accord wel nobre vc knyghtes al promised faythfully open audience sayd batayle helpe ayde ye sayd damoysell florence sayd king orqueney fayre cosin shal ryght well go thyther help lady also acquaynt wt gentyll knyght goddes sake bring hyther promyse loue hym ryght derely giue suche gyftes londe shall ryght ryche puyssaunt well fayre nece said king shall best power phowe emperour aferde lee florence shulde cast loue thur wherfore demauded kynge father haue maryage wtout ony lenger delay herwyth kyng content florence wold agree therto wherwyth kynge father wyth ryght sore dyspl ased ye shall afterward cap lxii whan emperour herd great praise laude ye generally giue arthur perceiued wel yt loue al ye court herde wel good wordes yt florence spake h wherby strake hert ialousy tere lest yt shuld cast loue therfore toke kyng emendus e hand said syr would ayne speke counsayl pray syr let doughter present soo bothe ro e florence softely smyled vnto kyng orq eney sayde hym cou seyle god gyue grace counsaile good may come therby fe contrary tha thre entred chaumbre leaned downe ayre wyndowe emperour began speke kinge sayd syr routh great season past syth ye gaue good wyll shold haue mariage ye fayre lady florence doughter presente hath euer excused selfe late departyng worlde quene mother h thought pertayning haue bene maryed soone decese grete season syth blame reputed maried therefore syr nowe require ye wyl incontinent deliuer according promyse made tyme name god sayde kynge reason right wyll wherfore fayre swete doughter florence ye wer borne good hou e whan noble hye person emperour wyl haue maryage whe great honoure wele shall come v countryes let v incontinent sende brother archbysshop thentent ensure togyther right dere father sayd florence ye ryght ouer soone mary certayne purpose yet maryed yet non think first se ii yeres passed ye least sayd kyng damosell wyl ye agenst wyl refusynge emperour lord way mariage syr sayd haue care lorde onely god surely wyl consent maryage ye shall sayde kynge elles ye shal right sore displese syr qoud displesure shuld greue aboue al thinges faith yt owe wyl yet maried ayd kynge se well yt ye wyll nothinge comaunde therefore ye shal whether ye wyl take hande thentent haue delyuered themperour whan sh saw conten pulled hande agayne thentent emperour touche whan kyng aw ryght sore displeased sayde damoysel ye haue set min accorde assent therefore promise fro henceforth help counsayle ye shal fayle therfore fro henceforth wel ye straiely charge auoyd come lyght presence soeuer whan florence saw father sore dyspleased said righ dere father ye thus dysplesed wt ye well therin syth pleasure take themperous elles lese couseyle helpe also come syghte whiche ryghte sore sayenge fader chylde syth humbly requyre g ase respyte space moneth tyll suche tyme may speke counseyle behalfe la sayd emperour longe respyte wyll departe hense ryghte shortely trowe hye tyme haue ben longe season al hath loue caused wherfore wold faine epart knowe wyse loue shall rewarded saye nay good take auysement cotent ye daye two well yd kyng content shall haue respyte tyl morowe houre lenger well sayd florence counseyle ayenst herte wyll sholde take man ayenst herte seynge yt quene doughter moost puyssaut kynge ye worlde certaynly greueth ryght sore ther began ryght piteously wepe make right grete sorowe whan kinge sawe wepe sayd auoyde syght let se tyl morow agayne present houre answere wheder ye wyll take hym good wyll therwith elles leue hym lese mi good wyl fauour euer florence issued chaumbre wepynge iiii kinges st pte whan sawe wepynge lefte eest mynstrelles iesters left al theyr sporte playe kynge orqueney toke bi hande demau ded wepte sore dere cosyn said lord fader right sore dyspleased hath com mauded sholde auoyde presence saw vncle archebysshop sayd hym fayre vncle let go lodgynge wyth ryght good wyl sayd shame haue yt thus causeth wepe thus al kinges conuayed vncle lodgynge dyd moost parte baron courte also new knyghtes al abode stil florence courte whan thus lodgyng kynges retourned agayne kyng emendus court kyng orque ey philip neuew ab de styll wyth florence king orqueney demaunded wepte cosyn sayde lord father woulde mary gyue emperour would haue ensured v togither wtout counsayl takyng eyther frendes god helpe rather dy haue themperoure hate nothynge muche worlde doo hym longe lyue wyl haue therfore greate foly enforce therto fayre lady cosyn said kyng god helpe haue agaynst wyl shal persed thousand helmes ye sayd philyp duke sabary daye com shall brente hundreth townes therof ye sure therefore fayre ladye yt pea set hert rest well sayde archebysshop let v go court speke thys emperour thus rose went forth left florence peace thus mouted vp palays founde kyng emendus emperoure together yssued chambre archebysshop sayd ye kynge fayre broder meruayle gretely cousayle ye haue cause beleue wel loue amitye beteth yt neyther knowe se hath displeased beholde e lorde dere frende empe ynde hath done v great honour would haue way maryage come desyre haue hys owne propre person without
