dysplesure worde wherefore ioye est longe ye haue wyll towarde syr comen thynke h dysplesure doth wyl nothing shall contrarye pleasure wyll eue shall redy accomplysh noble commaundement accordyng e whiche good true agenst personnes ought syr syth lo de noble emperour present wyl much honour desyre haue maryage whereof humbly thanketh ut wel custome accordyng state euerye person e dyscretelye wyselye suche case therfore syr conuenyent dele prudently ter ye empe two greatest puissan est person hauour r ndes nowe lyuyng lady florence moste ye puissaunt pryncesse worlde touchynge hye solempne matter maryage hemperour ynde doughter hye mightye kynge emendas hye great solempniti ought done priuely chaumbres rest peace ought done open presence ba ons bothe landes realmes thentent yf god sende anye yssue betwene theym theyr mariage may knowen ope ly al people bothe realmes whe shall eschewed grudge murmura yon han yssue shall wel knowen ryght ul heyre throughout bo regyons also conuenient solempne feast thys day holy ghoste thys solempne feast noble matrymonye sh uld made al one feast day hye prin ypally feast ha euery christen man ought nothyng elles aude serue god syr daye noble mariage let e kinges duke baron noble knightes lady damois let suche seruyce aperteineth let ladyes damoyselles dauce synge gyue newe knyghtes chaplettes stremers set theyr spere poyntes let yonge lusty knyghtes frusshe togyther theyr speres dasshe togyther theyr swerdes let ordeyned rounde table assemble togyther company shal brought thither lord kyng also emperour shall se knyght valure prayse whyche tyme shal brought hither riche pauylion lady florece wherin ymage fayry holdynge ryche chaplet yt whan tournay hal done lord themperour shal go image haue chaplet yt right ryche bo hauour frendes moost nobl parsone yt shal assembled hym ymage wyl giue chaplet moost wor hy whan hath shalbe sure certayne shall haue lady florence wyth good wyll entyre loue maryag yt made go loue hert good contrary ayenst ryght yl op rdous body without herte e wt salt body without soule thus may lorde themperour haue lady florence wyth great loue ioy feest whan emperour well herde mayster saw yt spake herte laughed bodye sayd fayth owe vnto god mayster hath ryght well sayd yly wyth great good hert acco de hys deuise let io full daye set let c yed great iustes tournay ayenst tyme let ordeined rounde table ke feest io e syr kyng day take tournay ayenst loue fauour god helpe sayd kynge ryght wel agreed myne aduise let al cyte cornyce day shall thys syr sayd mayster please hall shewe mine aduise let bartylm tyde nexte comynge hal cornes auoyded oute feldes time al thing necessary may honourably prouyded content sayd kynge say lorde themperour sir sai right well content anone poyntementes ran ouer palays euery mannes mouth euery man prayed god might send mayster right good adueture wel goodly speakynge began agayne ight great feest ioy tha came forth iuglers wt heyr fals caste tomblers wyth th soubersawtes damoyselles wyth theyr gambawdes made greater sporte tryumphe kynge themperour laughed made great ioye togither tyl tyme set table water b ought forth florece toke lycence kyng father sayd syr beseche grace dyspleased though newe knyghtes go wyth lodgyng though etayne wt daye well sayd kynge ryght well content go way hardely make good chere ye florence departed went chaumbre king abode styll palays kynge orqueney phylyp sabary archebysshop brysebar well nombre vc baron knyghtes went wt florence lodgynge mayster said madame saye ye haue respyte longe ynough many thy ge may fail betwene thys mai ter ye say yght well pray el e wyl knyght betwene erm madame sayd se well ye haue yet forgoten semeth yet remembraunce good lorde sayd florence wold ryght gla ly e hym yf god pleased yt come sayd urney shal hym honor pray et hym know madam quod ye maister hal go hym shew al ter yt ye desyre yt time hat loue shew par hyualry well maister sayd ye say right well pray let e comended vnto thus de ised maister shuld go porte noyre tyl time tournay han bringe wyth florence pauilion egle gold ymage hapler pyght ye fayre medow vnd r walles cite corny e w water brought forth serued full rychely wt great sport iumphe thus kyng kepte open court v dayes euery day one fl rence wente father court thende xv dayes ye kynge dyd gyue many yche gyftes knightes b th robe hors harneys florence lyke wyse gaue hem largelye yt meruayle consyder sayd wt one voyce yt neuer b fore suche hearte woman n yther lar e gentyll cur eyse thus al hese king ke th ir l ue depa ted euery man hys owne coutre puruay good knightes agenst sayd day mayster steuen afore florence sayd madam tyme yt depart wyl go streyghte argence sure yt shall fynd arthur redy fyght agenst neuew duke bigor fayre maister said florence haue grete doubt arthur duke neuewe right fierce fell good knigh th rfore great feare madam quod haue ye dout iiii afore arthur could endure puyssant stroke tha right valyant quod florence ye maister toke loue departed toke wt brysebar syr neuelo florence mar shal toke waye argece let v leue speake th let v returne arthur phow arthur receyued yre lady margarete citie argence cap lxi ii thus ye haue herde arthur iourn good space abbey grace n mawdelayne tyde began faste approche daye foule vylayne came vnto sayd swyne nothynge eate drynke rowe ye wedded thys abbey elles thynke ye wyl become monke ye haue promysed fulfyll requeste yf ye wyll go hortely arme let v go argence helpe fayrelady margarete argenton gete agayne ryght almoost hye tyme whan arthur hearde hym smyled sayd wyth ryght good wyll soo armed hym toke leue abbot couent mounted hys horse folowed vylayne soo arthur rode forth daye daye tyll laste descended downe greate mountayne entred fayrest medowe euer sawe hys lyfe syde thys sayd medowe ranne fayre ryuer wherein manye shyppes vnder sayle redye crossed lienge anger whyche ryuer ranne thrughout parte fayre cyte argence encountred varlet came streyght fro cyte thur salute h demaunded whence came answe ed sayd howe came cyte gence wofullest cyte worlde thys tyme moost tourmente sorowe sure neuer owne sore troubled houre wherfore goo frende sayd arthur syr god helpe good cause duke bygor n uewe com nge cyte haue made cry throughout cite countre noble men al suche holdeth theyr londs heyre argent mawdelayue tyde nexte comynge theym cyte argence theyr homage syr isembarte duke neuewe wherfore praye god maye dye euil deth xv dayes sayd daye whyche tyme purposed wedde fayre lady margarete lewde barbour hys shall dysheryted fro enherytaunce noble men bourgeyses cite countre aboute ryght sore dysmayed thei wote counseyle take ase lacke capytayne lady hath noo frende vncle put pryson duke neuewe none tell become also syr isembart hath slayne murthred falsly treason father syr sorowe noble cyte argence wel good frende sayd arthur god conduyte god yet puyssaunt ynough sende h lpe lady fr nde praye thys duke hys neuewe come yet cyte syr god helpe come al redy wyth hym moche people people nobred person leest great company sayd arthur soo departed arthur rode forth vylayne began cry come shal giue light euer rode behelde euery syde great copanyes knyghtes comynge goynge towarde cyte argence arthur saw wel land argeton moost good lyest coutre euer sawe perceyued wel ful rich worldly welth sawe many noble townes oures ryght hye myghty castelles many fayre woodes medowes pleasaunt ryuers townes fayre vynes goodly pasture fieldes corne fruite saw many lady damoyselles sporting ryuers syde wt fawcons gerfawcons theyr hand perceiued wel bicause ye good comod tie country ye duke neuew would disheryte fayre ladye margaret rode long til last saw fayre citie argence shining agenst sonne enuoyred greate depe dythes ful water ye walles strogly enbatayled mo vc toures made lyme stone sciment also saw manye fayre church coue ed wt lede ful typpes pomelles gold shynyng sonne also sawe burgeses lodging closed wt hye stronge walles barred wyth great chaines yron attaining fro one house arthur praysed muche noblenesse rich countre citie sayde hym selfe might well called argence semed wel argent say syluer thus arthur entred citie vylain went euer wt leuer neck bare legged hat hanging back euer went forth great pace loking downeward earth toke hede body met alwaies cryed aloude come shal gyue lyght burgeses behelde hym well sayd howe fole woman chyldren ran wyndowes beholde hym whan one bodye spake hym woulde aunswere thyng alwayes sayd come shall gyue lyghte thus arthur rode forthe cytie sawe nothyng noo maner crafte occupacion vsed bene vpon hye f astfull day al shoppes euery craft closed wherof arthur great meruayle behelde euery strete gret companyes knightes walkyng soberly together lurkyng vnder hattes beseming though well pleased sytting owne dores croslegged leaning elbowes makyng maner ioyfull semblaunt soberly musinge behelde vylayne neuer ceased cry come shal gyue light maner arthur rode euer styll forthe tyll came myddes citie saw great companye knightes burgeyses aboute number xxxv ca kynge together counsayl semed chere great ioy heartes vylayn enforced selfe crye louder dydde come shal gyue lyghte knyghtes behelde vylayne wel saw arthur folowed whereof greate maruayle last knight company called syr emery came arthur curteysly dyd salute sayd syr myne offyce citye receyue lodge al gentilmen straungers yt resorteth nyther syr myne house therfore desyre alyght youre horse entre syr thanke sayd arthur se wel yt must nedes go ferder seke mi lodging syr sayde knyght sauyng dysplesure ye shal passe house seeke lodgyng therefore fayth yt owe vnto god ye shal abyde wt ye syr sayd vylayn trowe ye wyll abyde ye haue promysed folowe whether euer go therfore come way wyl go goyng forth euer cryed come shall gyue lyghte arthur desyred vylayue tary last agreed thereto arthur rode forthe syr eme y dore lighted knightes left theyr counseyle dyd salute arthur gayne right courteously beheld arthur wel praysed muche heartes right tayre gratious sy eme toke arthur hand led hym fayre chambre vnarme hym meane tyme vnarmynge mayster steuen syr brysebat syr neuelon sensshal wer come syr emeris house take theyr lodgyng oke theyr chaumbre whan mayste chaunged gete wente downe ha l twoo knyghtes valiaut knew ryght well sa led e name therwithal bawd win came chaumbre fro arthur soo e sawe maister brisebar anne courteously byd salute ioyfull heart ye mayster demaunded arthur ster syr sayde thys ch mbre ey entred aumbre soone arth r sawe ranne enbrased mayst brysebar sayd mine owne good companion ye roche hither ye right ely welcome also dyd salute syr neuelon sene hall herte praysed hym gr tely whan syr emery saw mayster made great chere arthur thought verelye great man knewe wel maister kinges son sate beddes syde maister recounted werke ben king emendus coutte themperour desyred haue florence maryage tyme shewed hym hys meanes dyd lette time whan thus talked good space maister called hym sir emery theyr hoost caused hym sytt downe arthur demaunded hym wherefore knyghtes cytezyns th citie sad wered sayde syr wyll better haue good cause began shewe hym house da osel doughter lord cytye londe argenton ryght ul h yre countrey duke b gore neuewe alselye mu treason lorde ath r shewed hym al hole matter ye haue herade also shewed hym howe duke neuew would mary lewd adde hys barbour dy eryted forty thousande pounde lond yerely rent hath sommoned gentylmen country round wil shall homage vnto hym behoueth theym haue false murtherer lorde reny rightful heyre therfore syr al noble men cou try citie haue bene cousa l mater conclusion cousayl thus wolde make maner resistence agenst ye duke neuew rather suffre ladie disherited banisshed owne lande howbeit right gladly would moue war lacke captayne thynke verely woma chief head warre shuld cause length lytel effect arthur sayd syr haue somwhat herde matter pray arthur mayster steuen syr phylyp sabary syr brisebar syr artaude syr olyuer syr ycect also ladi margarete ther deuysed shuld demened yt iourney tha duke bygor see sir emeryes hous comaudynge hym lady vnpuruayed good counseyle knyghtes cyte copany moo v c moost parte al comyns cyte al shewed knyght wyth wolde mayntayne quarell whan duke neuewe herde hert mounted pryde said knyght cer aynly yf medell ony thynge wyth ye mater shall hange hym necke therfore yll come counseyle howe olde proue sayeth ten tymes wanteth hys wyll folysshely thynketh fared duke neuewe nyghte greater balaunce ieopardy knyght left life pledge kyng phylyp wente palays duke hys neuewe dyd encountre broughte courte open hall sate theym downe anone came lady arthur one syde mayster syde noblesse burgeyses comyns cyte dyd enuyron soo thus great company entred palays whan kynge sawe rose soo dyd duke hys neuewe proude herte ar styl wolde ri whereof moche blamed euery parsone sawe hym whan people sylence mayster steuen sayd duke syr ye haue commaunded ladye margarete sholde come courte syr beholde know pleasure wyl duke neuewe fel full pryde rose hys fete sayd syr clarke haue thynge wyth therfore ye pea let v alone sir said maister poore clerke reputed knoweth haue sayd lady thynke wyl auowe sayenge howe saye ye madame ye pleased shal speke certaynly sayd lady wyll holde ferme stable euer ye hau sayd shall saye syr duke requyre doo ryght daye yf ye wyll open audyence put othe goodes londes handes kynge orqueney syr phylyp neuew duke sabery bothe present certaynly fayre damoysell sayd duke phylyp doubte ye nothynge ony body shall doo wronge present well madame sayd kynge receyue wyth ryght good wyll handes syth pleasure put selfe duke bygor sayd damoysell shal ryght therfore mayster speake ye shewe ye wyl ladyes behalf syr sayd mayster say ye neuewe haue sente lady margarete nowe presente therfore yf please shewe v cause duke neuewe syr isembart sayd syr clerke shall shewe ye cause fully purposed gyue maryage barbou e mine also openly straitly co maund al noble men burgeyses citie al lond argenton payne lesynge landes continen day come theyr homage chief lord gouernour wyll thus forbyd heritage holde hardy entre mayster sayd syr ceyue wel good ryght ye wold thys ladye yf knyght yt wolde answere wil spare speke accordyng right syr duke troth comentie al ond argenton well noble men burgeyses comen people haue herde seen well assured syr uicter sometime lorde al londe argenton rightfull heyre noble lady ga ete h present lawfully desc nded hym yt rightful heyre herytage goodes pertaynyng sayd father therf syr wel hye ba ons cite londe argenton knyghtes burgeses wel er meane people suche present bene bsent repureth taketh holdeth theyr natural lady yt seruauntes hys efore syr de al lady londes may delyuered agayn maye recompensed wrong hath le let hym shewe lawfull cause loose l ndes syr ele e sayde syr isembarte wyll shewe caus whye wyl kepe sabary saw arthur moued stept forth mo vc knightes enuyroned lady arthur ayd defende yf nede tydynges abrode cite arthur likely slayne ye palays wherfore thither came runing al hole coment citte brast duke toke vp batayle iudg incotinent daye syr isembarte went arme hym lady ledde arthur syr emeryes hous knyghtes dyd arme hym mayster sayd hym syr arthur bere thys daye mortall batayle whyte shelde answered sayd yf god pleased wyll bere fere one knyght yet two knowen thrughout al cyte lady armyng chapyon syr emeryes hous yt batayle iudged day al ye belle euery churche began rynge ye people cyte ye coutre besought god helpe socour arthur processyons cyte assembled togyther theyr relyke cross holy water chanons preestes clarkes cope golde sylke barefoted praying god theyr ladyes champyon processyos came mette arthur strete mouted hys ho se phylyp duke sabery vc knyghtes company whan arthur sawe processyons bysshop mytred barefoted hys herte lermed wepte pyte dyd lyght hys horse kneled downe bysshopp dyd sense hym blyssed hym wyth cross arthur dyd k sse anclyned heed downe bysshop dyd gyue hym hys blessynge sayde lorde nayled crosse ayde socoure thys daye euer knyghtes answered sayd amen processyons retourned agayne theyr church arthur company mounted agayne theyr horse soo thus brought felde hole clergy cyte theyr knee makynge theyr prayer god shoulde day helpe socoure theyr lady champyon kynge orqueney came felde comaunded neuewe syr phylyp duke sabary kepe felde soo wronge treason wrought day syr phylyp armed hym selfe toke company syr brisebar sir neuelon syr ancean syr artaude wel nombre vc knyghtes court kynge emendus tha lady came feld mo tha men wyth syr isembart armed passed people euery sayd go thy way praye god thou mai dye euyl deth whan felde arthur downe shelde kynge also dydde well beholde hym praysed hym theyr hertes aboue knyghtes euer sawe syr isembart toke oth sayd god holy sayntes myght helpe hym neuer slewe lorde argenton neuer thought wolde haue kyssed sayntes myght hys rysynge suche payne heed almoost therby hadde loste syght wherfore people sawe hym sayd knyght hath euyll countenaunce sem th wronge lepte vpon hys horse ryghte heuyly arthur redy parte felde duke bygor prayed syr isembarte hys neuewe wolde leue batayle sayde howe woulde make pea accorde wyse wolde soo sware wolde neuer make pea tyll heed hys enemy lady brente many folkes thynke many thynges whyche hurte therof lyghteth theyr owne neckes dyd hym whan duke sawe coulde make pea commaunded shulde doo theyr best bothe knyghtes let theyr horse e great ran strake eche great myghty speres bothe knyghtes great force encountred soo rudely bothe theyr speres sheuered theyr fystes russhed soo togyther theyr bodyes helmes fel downe bothe erth arthur lustyer knyght quyckely lept vpon fete drewe traunchefer good swerde hat season syr isembarte laye styll earth fete vpwarde head downewa de whan arthur sawe laye soo vnease stepte hym lyfte hym vp layde shielde vnder head withdrewe hym selfe lytell wherfore greatly praysed kyng people kyng sayde neuewe syr philip semeth wel thys knyghte hath ryghte noble gentyl hearte uerely sayd duke philyp none otherwyse must nedes extraught noble blode touch shame vylanye whan syr isembarte reuiued hys traunce start vpon fete toke shelde drew swerde came vnto arthur gaue gret stroke shelde strake away great piece hawberke stroke dyde glyde downe earth said arthur ye made righte fall slepe night shal make slepe wise ye shal neuer wake arthur answered sayde syr ye promyse muche tell whether ye shal able paye arthur strake hym helme wyth suche force bare away gret piece therof one eares might wel sene caste shielde hym arther gaue suche stroke claue shielde asunder myddes stroke dyd glent arme bloud folowed wyth stroke swearde entred earth nye foote people sawe stroke sayde saynte marye knight yonder maye sustayn stroke knight like hym truelye best knyght worlde condycyon doo hardynes hym strength whan syr isembarte felt hym selfe wounded strake arthur helme entred til came coyfe stele stroke dydde glence downe warde lyft syde strake awaye muche hawberk touched came nere hys flesshe certayne yf tha syr isembart ben true faithfull man ben right good knight neuer founde hys matche tyme abated pryde arthur strake helme claue asonder helme coyfe swerde tourned carued awaye one re head gret piece brawne sholdre part hys harneys uste vnto bare rybbes tho saw sayd iesu may suche stroke gyuen knyghte lyuynge whan syr isembarte felte selfe wounded enraged yre sayde uassayle thynketh ye haue founde sayntes paradise shall reuenge lyft vp swerd strake arthur shielde soo bare awaye great piece hys harneys whan arthur felt stroke heuy puissant stepte asyde bothe st onge hym poynted swerde towarde hys vysage sayd false recreant knight without thou wylt make open knowledge thy defaute shall put sweard thy head cryed arthur mercy sayd ree knyghte slee sende myne vncle arthur gentyl knyght ye haue delyuered londe whych lost vse nothynge therof haue agayne noble prowesse wherfore holde yt haue god wherfore wyl make faythful homage take lord whiche knowledge wyl make hys swerde gyrte aboute hym wt hys harte hande whan approched nere table king sate began crye lowde could knight called arthur brytayne yf courte let hym answere wyth wordes courte pea soo euery man might well hym whan arthur herde demauded hym answered sayd frende yf ye demaude arthur brytayne many folkes reputeth therfore beholde redye man ye demaunde saye ye wyll syr sayd squyer sente therfore ye shall shall say syr trouth mayster syr octhebon hurtebise hath hearde tydynges aduentures hath done many could hym good syr knyght seke bodye thinke verily nere deth therfore sendeth cotinent ony shoulde gyue hym helthe yll physycyon helpe hym seke ye speke syr come way shall shewe maner sekenes well sayd arthur thynketh gyue hym ony good couseyle ye syr said squyer ye hardines valure reported well frende sayd arthur suffre tyll morowe shal day take leue baron folowe syr sayd squyer brytayne yf ye wyll go come waye streyght wyll departe wyl ye know sayd mayst r appeleth hys deth name god answere kyng wolde saye ye curse mayster syr knight would haue maisters head ye wold go seke haue weyght fyne golde ye wold fain haue myght cost nothing ye neuer hardy go seke cause ye du st syr father brother remembraunce herte clo ed suche wise great space cou speke word sate wne benche whan lady could speake said fayre vncle dere frende neue sawe dere father sy departed wyth praye tel whether yo haue sene pray answere pore orphelyue bothe fath r mother whan vncle herde saye soo hym thought herte dyd breke sorowe sayd myne owne nece dere lou bothe ye haue lost hym ye disherited pouertie hath made v hath wel aduenged youre mortall enemy hath deliuered oute dolorous pryson wherefore yf euer may se hym agayne wyl become man thus talked together long ste mayster made theym night countesse wyfe cap lxvii mornynge betymes gouernar toke hys leue lady maister noble markes rode forth waye iacket hys squyer wyth hym ryght rychely beseen mounted good puyssaunte horse soo rode forthe viii dayes neuer coulde anye tydynges sought tyl laste tryued londes ynde bytwene realme soroloys empyre sawe great ryuer crosse waye encountred messenger bare scochyn hys brest also bode full letter rode great pace aboun e saynt laurence tyde gouernar dyd salute va l demaunded hym tydynges whence answered sayd syr pertaynynge erle yle perdue rydynge stronge castell knyght named syr iakes bycause lord thynketh vnpuruayed good knyghtes hath made cryed tournay mondaye next comynge thentent ye b st knightes yt cometh thider haue wyth hym sayd great ournay cornyte therfore must go sayd syr receiued hym frendly hous whan gouernar chaunged called hys hoste demauded hym maner erle maner man answered sayd syr gh valyaunt man hardy kn ght fewe may compare wyth hym dedes armes hath hys wyfe moost fayre lady worlde exc pt kyng soroloys doughter b au e hyther resorteth many strauge knyghtes duke erles many good knightes bicause dooth tournay tomorow knoweth well yt many knyghtes wyll hys house se wife therfore hath caused gate hys castel fast shette hath defended euer shal entre gate open syth none yesterday sayde gouernar name god shall assay entre yf se fayre lady called hym iacket comaunded hym brynge h hys horse sayd wolde go assay horse ayenst nexte daye olde tournay iacket brought hym horse mounted theron rode forth throughout ye stretes towne tyl came castel gate foud fast shet e bad porter open gate sayd wolde entre castell porter demau ded hym frende said gouernar wold speke good lady place eryly syr sayde port r ye may entre place lord hath def ded contrary hath comauded yt euer yt co eth hyther none shoulde entre wherfore dare lette yes pray sayd gouernar wyll gyue soo euer ye wyll demaunde porter opened lytel wyndowe sawe yt gouernar ryght goodly knyght browne vysage sawe yt rode maruayllous fayre horse thought well yt noble man sayd hym syr yf ye wyll gyue horse ye ryde wyll open gate open gate one gyue hym syr sayd porter wyll ye promyse ye true knyght shall haue hym eryly promyse ye shall haue hym trewe knyght syr sayd porter pray ary lytle whyle shal go speke wyth lorde well sayd gouernar praye ye agayne faste ye may porter went erle sayd syr youre gate maruaylous fayre knyght hath great desyre se lady yt wyll gyue hys horse rydeth wel worth lykelyhode c pounde condycyon wolde open gate let therfore syr pleaseth hewe mynde case sai erle minde none entre place howe wyl thou hould lese thy gyft tha wolde gyue therfore goo thy waye open gate take thy horse tha sayd countesse wyfe madame yonder knyghte hath gyuen ryche gyft se speake wt wherfore charge dere ye holde loue wha come ye make maner semblaunt speke worde hym euer saye yf ye doo otherwyse ye shall ryght ore dysplease syr sayd lady goddes sake axe mercy syr knowe kynght valure yf haue gyuen ryche gyfte speake shall haue small rewarde hys curtesy yf shoulde kepe speache hym ayenst loue man gentylwoman g eat power therfore greatly trespace speke im yf speake fayth vnto god said erle ye trespace agenst commaundement shall dysplease herte ro e sir sayd lady loue content yf vylany growe therby praye g maye fai porter opened gate gou rnar porter toke hor e gouernar wente forth palays fore erle uch knightes wer wi h meete gouernar dyd lute hym b helde hym maruaylouslye soo e pa ed f rth tyl came whe e cou te e wente sayd g ge fou g ue hys daye helth ioy peace blessed enowne yt run th valuce boute fresh beau ye se well trouth tha reported whan cou te e herd hym answered er worde whiche greued ryght sore herte therwith cast downe loke toward earth gouernar made countenaunce salute ladyes te downe amonge hem l st sayd countesse fayre ladye knyght passeth thrughout cou try shewed ye thys castell wherfore thought would passe without seynge therefore come offre selfe knighte may sake wherfore madame r quyre shewe youre pleasure sore desyrynge knowe countesse spake word agayne cast h r loke grounde wherwith ryghte sore greued herte whan gouernar sawe spake worde ryght sorowfull sayde madame wyll ye speake haue renowmed ye fie gentyll hearte suche courtese ye could beare none yre malice herte vylany maner persone wherfore fayre lady aunswere maner worde al spake worde agayne ther water brought forth wasshed sate downe dyner era e caused gouernar syt nexte ladye thentente doo hym anoyauce shame gouernar carued lady ryght goodly knyfe oftentymes spake woulde ueuer gyue an e e agayne gouernar sore dyspleased neyther dyd eate drynke bu ytel sawe well ho lady spake wy e would speke coutesse ight sore spleased hearte du ste speake thus e thys case tyl taken vp fro ye diner gouernar toke boldly hand sayd madam wold fay e speake lytell wyth soo lad vnto fayre wyndowe sayd swete lady none yl despite trespace haue made anye ye suche hardnes yt ye wil speke ye haue name moste free gentyllest hearte lady lynynge al bounte courtesy sayd therfore swete lady shew somewhat courtesy speakynge one woorde fayre gentyl ladye soo muche honor speke god helpe ashamed ye euer shal sayd morow folysshe knight outragyous myne outrage shal sayd haue loste herynge speche moost fayre ladye worlde madame requyre put fro reproche open lytle swete mouth wherein curtesy speke worde madame god helpe herte dyeth body fere leest ye dyspleased wyth trespace haue done yt spake worde agayne hym yet sore greued herte gouernar stode talked longe thys lady tyl laste two gentylwom n came go chambre take reste gouernar departynge layde hys arme aboute sayd madame se well must nedes departe thys tyme wyll go lodgynge ryght owful ye shall go reste slepe take lytell care greate grefe madame saye vnto wyl neuer departe fro towne tyll ye haue spoken thus talkynge brought chambre doore sawe well waye chaumbre fayre orcheya de sayd madame ye wyll speke ut promyse wyl come nyght yonder orcheyarde soo chaumbre speake thoughe dye therfore syth haue taken enterpryse mynde eyther wyl dye elles ye shal speake therwyth countesse entred chaumbre wythout spekynge ony worde hym gouernar retourned hys lodgynge towne ryghte sore dyspleased hys herte whan iacket sawe hym come fote demauded hym hys horse answered sayd fayth frend gooth wel wyth ha ha sayd iaket trowe ye haue played away horse bycause ye woulde tournay morowe knyghtes countre well shamefull knyghte morowe whan se gentyl knyghtes tournay shall shewe ye lye slepe chaumbre gouernar layde hym downe bedde replete wt yre tyll nyght sayd erle comaunded hys knyghtes departe goo theyr restes bycause shoulde trauayled next daye also sayd countesse hys wyfe madame go thys night chaumbre take rest wyll thys nyght ly alone sure shall ryghte sore trauayled morowe whan derke nyght coutesse taken leue entred chambre rose gouernar badde iacket squyer gyue hym swer e iacket demaunded hym wolde doo wyll go playe sayd gouernar fayth owe god sayd iaket trowe ye wyll go lye wayte hye way robbe marchaut newe horse wyth gouernar answered worde agayne departed fro hym euery bodye theyr thus yf loued wolde haue done nothynge thys yt done therfore madame goddes sake make hym amendes yll cruelte yt ye dyd day speke curteysly powcet sayd lady full yre hath dyspleased cominge hider flyenge aboute hym moo iii quarelles shotte oute crosbowes arthur sate shyp couered hys whyte shelde quarelles dyd lyght thycke theron thought rayned suche wyse shyppe rased wyth quarelles maner approched posterne whan came entre founde styckynge rounde aboute gate great longe sharpe speres wt heedes fyne stele toke hys good swerde hys hande layde speres faste coulde dyd cut clene asonder staye hym spe e wynd swyf eues water che payne stande vpryghte last grettrauayl dyd moche yssued straymes posterue herde thynge make great noyse castel therwt came hym one mo v hundred persones fight agaynst hym assayled rudely al partes cast speres stone dartes staues ight gret ple ty gaue agayne yght great trokes frusshed downe euer attayned vnto ye prese gre caused hym knele hys knee quickery stepte vp agayn dasht among right sore chafed str ngth began encrease grew strengthe cut asonder euer attayned vntoo clene force drew hys backe backe wall rested hym tha enemy ran crosdowes speares charged hym many gret stroke whan felte hymse fe sore oppressed sore chafed therwt habandoned elfe among gane great stroke euer touched claue sholders began flye hym folowed ight sore wety behynd hym dyd muche payne trauayle thy case thus fightyng fro thre c k tyl none thre me dryuen downe hys knee yet al euer rose agayn spyte thus fighting laste herde sowne gr horne aboue castel sone tho fought arthur herd blaste horne sodainly departed without word speakynge remayned lonely arthur wherof great maruayle arthur dressed hym toward castell entred last entred fayre halle found neyther man woman wel content yt ye fyrst ye shal dyne arthur dyned wt quene dyner toke hys leaue quene courte moche sorowe whan departed court trusted yt haue bene theyr lorde arthur mouted horse departed castel soo came hurt knight demaunded dyd whether yt well quytte couenauntes sir god helpe knyght right wel ye haue right truly nobly quytte therfore lorde yt thynge fourmed rewarde truley shall owne knyght fast toure thentent haue slayne hym nyght arthur dyd valyauntly brake toure slewe knyghte people capitulo lxxi whan arthur departed fro proserpyne rode longe tyll laste entred londe duke bygors neuewe aduenture toke hys lodgynge wyth knyghte neuewe syr isembarte receyued arthur wyth grete ioye vnarmed whan redye wente hall knight tha knyght demauded arthur hys name yt doubteth nothynge answered sayd syr called arthur squyer named bawdewyn knyght knewe wel yt yt layne vncle syr isembarte wherfore hert rose sore ayenst hym made semblaut therof knewe well arthur knyght ryght sore redoubted wy bycause ye haue slayne syr isembart men lyuynge hated hym moost dydd manye dyspleasures thus wt fayre wordes draue season wt arthur tyll souper tyme ryghte well serued souper sported tyll tyme goo theyr restes knyght caused arthur bedde made stronge tour well hanged wyth clothes sylke arres arthur could perceyue walles strengthe therof whan arthur bawdewyn entred toure incontynent knyght dyd shytte fast doore whych yren barre fast foure greate bar e escryed arthur sayd syr make mery ye ye depart chambre ye shal lese head ye maye saye ye vnhappy come hither mortall enemy wha arthur herde yt herte right sore dyspleased soo ran doore thinkinge haue opened coude barred wtout foure great barres stele tha knyght armed al copany well nobre xviii persones moone shone fayre bryghte lytle wyndowe behynde one tapperts bawdewyn ta e downe hangynges myght e e ely aboute light mou came window prisoner wont serued thur armed hym toke swerde hand beheld well wyndowe whyche stronge barred wyth yren aduenture founde chabre grete leuer yren soo e toke bothe hys handes ryght sore displeased dyd lyft vp leuer lyghtly though ben sticke layd barres yren suche strength braste barres stone made suche hole oxe myght well haue yssued therat knyght hys company wythout whan sawe dydde caste hym ryght rudely dartes quarelles shot crosbowes tha arthur toke white shelde went wyndowe receiued sheues came streyght table whereas dyd eate wyth greate staffe hande without speakyng worde lyft vp hys stuffe strake ladye great stroke betwene sholders made lene downe flatte table therewyth made greate crye therewyth toke great cuppe syluer full wyne dyd caste wyne arthur sate toke cup wyth hym therwithall returned backe agayne wythout speakyng word yssued oute hall met bawdewyn strake hym rudely wyst well arthur sayde ladye madame thus beten lese good ryght great outrage knyght answered arthur sayde syr yf thou wylte amende come crosse way besyde yonder wood shall ye fynde arthur stepte vpon hys fete called hys harneys anone bawdewyn ar hym lady sayde gentyl knyght honour hye god heauen go thither xxx horse back well armed wherfore ye endure agaynst madame sayd arthur speke wyl go loke mounted horse folowed knyght crosse way redy aby ynge arthur sone sawe arthur comyng caste cuppe toke hys sp met togither rudely knight brake sp arthur rake hym hys sper ranne oute bodye fote fell dead bawdwyn sayd right thou strak st art stryken agayne thy great pryde thou hast yll rewarde suche deserte suche payment bawdewyn drewe knyghtes owne sworde strake therwyth knightes hand wherwyth stryken ladye table dydde put hande cuppe menaunt theues departynge theyr praye wonne marchauntes espyed one theyr felowes slay e therefore contynent toke theyr ha eys nne arthur ydes soo gaue hym many great stroke euer arthur cast hys shelde hym theron receyued al theyr stroke coulde wyse payre hys shelde maner poynt whe yght greate maruayle arthur st ake one theym rudelye hys heade flewe clene felde claue another shouldres thyrde claue sholdre owne waste gaue amonge theym manye wonderous stroke manye soo ranne crosbowes artes therewyth dyde hym moche anoyaunce alwayes yghte valyauntlye detended hym selfe fyrste bronte slewe vpon ii theym w r thus fyghtynge togeth r fortuned gouernar aryue reason bront noyse hearde e sawe w al company one knyght whome sawe defende hym selfe ryght valiauntly long behelde hym tyll laste knewe well hy mayster thur reason hys e held dasht hor e came amonge wo fe doothe amonge shepe strake soo fyrste encountred ranne hym clene throughout body set hand swerde strake soo hys heade fell arthur horse necke whan arthur sawe knewe well old knight gouernar wherof great ioye rested hym selfe holde gouernar fought wt sw rd sawe gouernar yd cleue one downe gyrdell dyd arthur smyle sayde thys mayster chastiseth ryght sore scolers te heth hard lesson sayth owe vnto god shall help hym syr sayde bawdwyn whan ned frende proued goo giue grace well arthur rusht prese confounded al euer attayned vnto tha one theues fote lost hys horse ranne arthur horse wt sper strake cleue throughout bely horse fell downe dead arthur lepte fete hys sw hys hand dressed hym e slayne horse gaue suche stroke claue hym sholders whan gouernar saw arthur fete ryght sorow ul soo dasht prese encount ed knyght rudely neyther helme coyse stele could sa slayne two bound fast bawdewyn iacket dyd kepe came lady nece sawe theyr enemyes lye dead ground saw noble valute two knightes lady praysed moche theyr eattes e sawe arthur gouernar togyther making good chere e doynge theyr h me lady sayd arthur syr whence cometh knyght p traynyng ye truly madam sayd arthur frende hath ryght well ho pen thys daye sawe ether gret season lady saw fayre maruelously byg sayd syr ye happy come hither thys point sir knight ye haue acheued ente pryse theues requyre let se two slayne elles hanged yll cote spryngeth yll wyl neuer good escape whan theues herde great feare sayd r ur gentill knyght saue oure lyues shal shewe forest yghte greate treasoure sayde thur syr wyll bryng thy ther soo dye arthur answe ed sayd syrs lyfe death lyeth ladyes handes pleaseth shortly brynge v thys greate tresoure two theues wente bawdwyn toke cuppe wy h knightes hande therein dyd presente lady arthur thanked hym muche soo would haue gyuen cuppe bawdwyn wold take said ynough cariage horse harnes arthur rode longe theues forest tyll last came wyld sauage place great valley foud bowes cro bowes hawbertes helmes gownes couerynges cloth theu robbed al country also ben stolen fro church people countrey none company shall take worth one p uy therof ladye dyd arthur comaunded desyred arthur twoo theues myghte slayne incontinent urned ladyes place wente souper rychly serued arthur demaunded gouernar howe mayster steu n dydde markes answered sayd howe dyd ryght well good hel h dyd maunde vnto hym lyke wyse dooth fayre lady margarete argenton come port noyre syr thanke muche may aide socour ye haue done lady argenton cosyn germayn whan arthur sawe knele toke vp made greate ioye togeth r tyll tyme go theyr restes mornynge arthur rose toke leue lady rode fro porte noyre go tournay cornyte toke hym noble florence ryche pauylyon wherin ymage wyth chaple resembled thynge vnto lady florence moost fay e creature tha worlde capitulo lxxiiii thus arthur rode forth hys waye towarde cornyte mayster steuen porte noyre wyth markes gentyl lady margarete argenton dydde sporte playe gentyll damoysell oughte doo euery daye made chaplettes rose floures whyche gaue ioyous specially whan sawe loued arthur whome neuer sawe syr rowlandes seruauntes assayled arthur haue slayne hym valyauntlye defended hym selfe slewe many capitulo lxxv dyner archbysshop maister steuen syr rowland baron went talkyng playing togeder medowe entred forest laste came fayre grene oke whych dyd caste fayre shadowe greate cyrcuyte aboute grasse fayre soft thyck vnderneth sate wne talked together many thyng tyl last mayster demaunded syr rowlande lyked country cornyte whether fa rer country bygor sir rowland answered hym would giue answere case sayd master lytell bound well sayd syr rowland maketh matter though ye son kyng yet wyl answere matter non take ye list syr sayd mayster haue trespaced thing agenst yea yt ye haue sayd syr rowland tyght greuousely ye argente wha co n syr isembart slayne ye kepte copanye chefe couseller wt knight slew therfore bere grudge mine hert agaynst promise god yf may encountre hym dyd deede shal much hi hath done cosyn syr sayd ye aideth ight cause eu r falleth well sayd syr rowlande ye saye howe cosyn wronge none yt sayeth sayeth otherwyse trouthe wyll proue euerye ag nst ye wyll mount horse say mat r truly ega del withall syr wold suffre tyme hys request sayd wolde syr neuelon senesshall sayd syr rowlande syr content wt wordes mayster man greter dygnyte ye though stryken head ye haue soo hye frende yt durst reuenge cause noble kynge orqueney yt batayle wher ye say mater truly deite wythall ye speke vylany ayenst kynge ayenst phylyp duke sabary neuewe ayenst su whych seynge nedeth rehersed shame suffre suche wordes passe youre mouth ore dyspleased brysebar slepte forth sayd syr rowlande ye say mayster dyd truely ye mater whan cosyn slayne wherein saye ye saye truely yf ye wyl mayntayne contrary take youre hatneys shal take myn let seen trouth therwith syr brysebar rysynge haue departed bysshop helde agayn sayd loke soo euer speketh ony worde mater let hym sure shall hys frende left spekynge yt mater tyme bysshop brought talkynge deuysynge talkynge one mater arthur gouernar yssued forest soo entred medowe arthur behelde goodly tentes pauilyons pyght aboute felde also sawe sheldes helmes harneys shynynge ayenst sonne h de greate courser braye crye stampe theyr fete whych fyght noyse quyckened herte courage last gouernar espyed florence pauily wherin ymage chaplet shewed arthur whan sawe herte inwardly reioysed knewe well ladyes pauylyon tyme mayster al entred agayne fayre medowe arthur sate hys horse grete study mused hys aduenture last syr myles balefoude espyed hym knewe well yt arthur seen hym argence said knightes aboute hym lordes beholde yonder knyght al armed ryght fayre beholde onye knoweth hym wolde name bicause syr rowland wha mayster steuen sawe said know hym ryght well wherfore trust yt great wind lately blowen wyll sone layde hys comynge greate ioye herte moche forgate maner al displeasure certaynly syr sayd senesshal right fayre gracyens beholde wherfore byleue great bloude thynketh semblaunt great study whe fore euer hode brysebar knowe full well wherfore studyeth mayster senesshall brysebar rose fayre easely wente hym warde sayd eche yt wolde name hym tyme bycause syr rowlande came arthur styll study gouernar soone sawe mayster alyghted fro hys horse enbraced hym baron eche therwythal arthur lefte hys musynge soone euer sawe mayster steuen knyghtes dyd alyght hys horse salute one among made right great feast ioy syr rowlande meruayled muche knight mighte becaus sawe soo much chere ioye made knew senesshal sayd arthur syr wyl ye take rent pau n ye kep company together thi rney syr wel content quod arthur incontinent vnarmed al harnes horse sent senesshals tent wha arthur aparayled mayster sayde hym syr let v go salute ye archbysshop brother kyng emendus vncle faire lady florence whan thur herd speke florence hert trembled ioye soo wen warde bysshop whan bysshop saw rose dyd salute sir e also syr rowland bygor knew hym bi hop behe hym affectuously semed hym ye fayre knyghte world arthur dyd hys bonet dyde salute bysshop al likewise hym agayne bysshop demaunded syr said arthu knight strauger soone syr rowlande herde hym saye ran knyght slewe hys cosyn demaunded name syr sayd righte name arthur cal ye youre squyer quod syr rowland syr sayd arthur named bawdwyn syr rowlande knew wel w slew cosin soo demauded fro whens came syr quod arthur come streyght fro arg nce wel syr quod rowland saw batayl done betwen straunge knight duke bygors neuewe whan ye maister herd tho demau e right ioyous wyst well wordes yt spoken el reue knight certenli quod rowland know wel therfore saye falsely nt uly ye dyd wyl make g od incontyneut bodye agenst whan archbysshop herde blamed much syr rowland wordes desyred hym yt al matter myghte rest pea proudly answered said wold yt wold arme incontinent mayster sayd bysshop naye syr let hym alone ryght therfore hath good cause reuenged yf wha hath enemy present shal e nede go seke hym fe also lord father loueth right wel ye haue bene norisshed vp togither ye clerke sworne streyght counsayl therfore ye ought owe faith trouth wtout r son falsenes ye ought help ayde al busines certenly madam quod mayster al ye say trouth shal longe lyue shal kepe crete counsayle long lyue certenly mayster sayd haue grea affyaunce therfore wyl yt ye shal know secretes heart therfore require kepe close loue arthur wt al hert wyl loue hym aboue creature ye worlde sweare faythfully long lyue wyl neuer haue lord spouse al onely hym whan mayster e de saye ryght great ioy sayd mada surely ye haue sir myles played togyther chesse tyme kynge orqueney duke phylyp neuewe come lyghted myddes myddes medowe ne e florence tent phylyp well xiiii knyghtes wente streyght florece tent founde playenge mayster steuen whan florence sawe kyng cosin duke phylyp salute enbraced kyssed sayd welcome made eche great feest ioy sate downe fayre new grene russhes talked togither many thinges last kynge demaunded mayster tydynges arthur syr sayd mayster ferre hen senesshalles tent madame sayd kynge dyd ye se hym speake hym yet yes syr sayd florece saw hym whan dyd iust agaynst syr rowlande appeled hym falsenes bycause cosyn duke bygors neuewe pray madame sayd phylyp wente iustes bytwene syr two ribbes broken sir rowlandes syde one hys armes broken asonder hys horse fell name god said ye kyng knew arthur trowe knoweth hys stroke therfore madame spede ye knyght aqueynted wt prynce al worlde wold right glad haue noble company hym vnderstande hath offred hym selfe knyght therfore receyue hym retayne hym suche wyse escape fro ye tel nede parauenture ye shal haue hym cosyn sayd florence ye say ryghte well mayster shal go hym dyd kynge sayd duke phylyp hys neuew syr become good faythfull company ye promised thys knyght ye knowe nere yet ye make none semblaunt therwith syr phylyppe sle te forth mayster go arthur yssued theyr tente entred archebysshop kynge florence rose dyd set downe bysshop bytwene phow duke phylyp mayster wente fetche arthur kynge orqueney fayre florence capitulo lxxvi duke philyp mayster entred senesshals tent founde arthur playing wyth syr mile whan arthur saw duke philip went enbraced sayd syr ye right el welcom sir quod duke philip ye also wel foud syr sayde arthur kyng orqueney certaynly syr wyth lady florence tent desireth come name god sayde arthur praye god sende hym right good aduenture go thither duke phylyp wente hande hande talkyng together maister senesshal syr myles syr ancean brysebar went tyll came florence tent wha florence sawe arthur herte began tremble sodely blusshed none toke hede thereto euery man toke regard arthur kyng archbisshop rose went enbraced hym made right grete ioye set hym downe kyng demaunded hym howe done syth tyme sawe hym last answered said right wel thanke god kynge sayd florence madame beholde thys knyght god helpe wolde cost euery yere xii thousande pound condycyon partaynynge house companyon thys heartely requyre hym argence answered offred seruyce knyght therfore say nothinge ladyes winneth al madame ye haue wherof ryght ioyous pleseth ryght well yf sholde comaudement ye ye puyssant lady therfore good shall honour promise said florece shal make hym gret lord uissant thought herte would make gret lord ladye mada arthur thanke grace therwith stode vpon fete gentyll body fayre byg soo well proporcioned member yt ye florence beheld pleased lady wysshed bene partaininge lordes husbandes th talkyng thus togyther came florence messeger fro father king emendus shewed howe dyd hertely comaund hym desyred go bastely dyner comyng wyll lodge nighte nere tente florence made semblaunt though ben glad hys comyng content hert hasty co myng thoughte haue spoken wt arthur diner tha repented syr rowlande howe ouerthrewe hym horse earth th n king orqueney sayd syr knyght yt ye haue herde moche honour hye prowesse reputed saynt mary sayd kynge ashamed yt haue made better semblaut haue done therefore goddes sake cause hym come th n syr moraus senesshall vnto kynge v nte arthur retourned wente kynge dyde hys bonet king orqueney put arthur bytwene kynge emendus king said syr ye righte hertely welcome countre syr goddes sake myscontent thoughe haue made none semblaut tyme syr lyke grace sayd arthur none suche cause alwaies commaudement vttermost small power well arthur said kinge whythe lodgynge endured well space two leges thus king florence made together ryght great ioy myrthe kynges pauillou kynge orqueney helde forence h me ayd fayre lady nece shal sene novle chiualrye sauegarde body ye know wel yt lady doughter yong tendre hath euer swetely brought vp wherfore nede send strau ge sauage coutry ayre regyon contrary nature sauegarde body hye myghty lady owne coutre great pitie also syr ye knowe well longe season agone ther wrytynge made sealed xii peres realme sholde neuer haue none creature marriage onely hym ymage giue vnto chaplet yet neuer none assayed syr come chyualry therfore holde forth tournay let se whome pryse shall gyuen syr let themperour ye kynges noble knyghtes come pauylion ymage whome euer gyue chaplet lette enioye moche honoure kynge mormall rose ryghte auncyent wyse prynce moost preuyest kynges counseyle sayd syr trouth man holde realme therefore owe vnto fayth trouth also vnto lady doughter syr trouth wyll bere witnesse mayster hath sayd well truly syr yf ye haue put seale accorde also kynges present also xii peres youre realme syr saye ye also oughte abyde fremely seales accorde good kynges ought whan kinge emedus well reason entent yt haue stept forth ye mayster sayd syr emperour ye saye wysely call archebysshop traitour say yt seketh werke ony treason ayenst largely sayde ther neuer yet ony noble man roloys euer dyde ony treason ayenst ayenst ony liuing though accorde mariage dooth ryghte sauyng honour lorde kyng present al accord forsworne haue broke promesses couenautes dooth ayenst theyr seales log lyue shall neuer accorde therto mayster said king wyll ye accorde therto holde forsworne fayth owe vnto god yf ye wer son king make wel know ye haue spoken folishely presence thus moch say vnto charge incontinent ye auoyde pauylyon defende comynge agayne syghte dyscharge florence cou seyle well syr sayd mayster syth se must nedes leue courte comynge banysshed fro ye couseyle lady emperoure present wherefore let hym certayne yt longe liue shal neuer put ringe lady florece finger wedde power yt hath haue kynge sore dyspleased rose thought haue striken mayster king mormal kinge ismaelyte dyde holde hym therwith maister went pauylyon whan kynge valefounde sawe sone cast courte king would haue stryken hym rose vp sayde kynge syr esche wyng yll trouble tyme agreed emperour shoulde haue doughter wherin confesse yt forsworne dyde therin cotrary myn owne seale promesse consentement openly reuoke deny god helpe wil lenger forsworne therfore say emperour yt take yf let certaine ther shalbe realme va ounde king frende shall hys mortall enemy whan kyng emendus herde hym speke ye maner right sore dyspleased loued bileued hym ryght well sayd syr kynge eyther consent maryage elles forsake presece shortly auoyde pauylyon well syr wyll departe warraunt wyll noo desyre come syght say god giue grace ye well therwith went pauylyon wente hys son mayster steue king orqueney rose vp said king syr haue grete meruaile ye haue taken counseyle enstrauge self fro frendes counseyllers veryly syr ye yll mynde case al emperour shall neuer moche good fayth yt owe lady florece yf wer presence take heed fro sholdres let hym take good hede maryed cary myle place shal ther redy encoutre plesure said king ye menace threte shortly charge auoyde pauylyon beware yt se syght despyte ioy tryumphe space viii day kynges florence wente fayre chambre counsayle bishop arthur duke philyp mayster recouted florence yt departed oute court gret displesure king emendus banysshed al presence also know wel sone hath knowledge ye shall haue sharpe great war made vnto v wherfore conuenient aduise wel shal done mater ye maister rose said lordes ye thinke done shal shew mine aduyse answered said maister say ye wil shal plese right wel giue audience maister sayd madam ye propre rightfull heyre soroloys propre lady al dyscorde betwene lorde youre father v moueth propertlye reason trespasse socoure arthur encountred one kynges co mynge towarde themperoure company wel vnto nombre xviii thousande men wa e whiche kynge hector slewe people none euer escaped sauynge twoo soo fledde away hector great botye muche treasure gret haboudauc vytayle whych al brought porte noyre capi lxxxviii thus hector people entred thys greate valley perceyued came themwarde aboute nombre xviii thousande men warre hector demauded gouernar knew answered sayd syr nay good fayth doubt least oure enemyes hector made al host armed selfe gouernar armed whan armed gouernar presed forth demaunded one fro selfe gouernar drewe hys sworde strake soo knyght betwene sholders necke claue hym downe waste gouernar sayde trowe haue assured knighte parte thynke wyl abyde styll thys place tha sayd hector se wel hys sworde hys hande haue stryken head people socoured ran hector sydes hector strake among brake gret prese gouernar dashte thyckest prese without sparyng body cut armes legges hedes grete p enty syr clatembart entred prese syr othes like wise began suche fray pitie beholde kyng godyfer remounted agayne hector layde round hym went muche forward closed among hys enemis howe gaue amonge great stroke yt euer attayned vnto wente deth enemis dyd cast hym knyues dagers last therbi slewe horse vnder lept fete swerde hand enemy oppressed gretely therwith gouernar came hym gret rage also comyng beset enemy horse slayne vnder hector gouernar case yt harde escape tyll laste syr clarembalt al rou e came began sore batayle wonder beholde hector gouernar dyd valiantly eche gate hym newe horse soo spyte theyr enemyes agayne remounted dasht prese gaue myghty stroke confounded euer attayned vnto kynge godyfer came greate prese drewe clene force gouernar syr othes prese closed rounde aboute gaue many mayster yt maketh mater truste well yt shal brynge one daye place ii kynges prysoners thei yt herde began laugh al yt day sported ye maisters wordes tyl time go rest euery man wet bed toke restes tyll nexte morning morning lordes arose betymes assembled togyder middes palays tha hector sayd arthur cosyn yonder people without hath good lyfte slepe none wake ye good lord thynketh slow let v go se name god syr clemeso let deuoyrs abide log therfore let v issu dele valiautly wt name god quod arthur euery harneis euery man wet arme florece ye poyntment whan knew therof came sayde syrs mene ye mater must done wysely ye know preseisely yet cause grete assembly come aboute castell peraduenture thei come honour mariage bytwene arthur bileue king fader com harneys wherfore minde best assayle first yf assayle v tha let v defende selfe best wise syr markes ye noble goo message kynge fader wherfore pray go hym humbly comaude grace say yt requyre sende worde minde come hyder maner wyse tyme pray marke wel word haue sayd wyse man nedeth teching ye se wil nedes kepe styll hys frowarde mynde warde tha wyl ye say hys iiii kynges al chyualry sende word thei al men subiectes wherefore yf hardy drawe ony swerde ayenst ayenst ony myne tell fayth owe lady egletyne ere moder whose soule ihesu haue mercye shall cause hanged neckes though bee neuer soo noble gentil wyl ye enquyre emperour come thus realme yf ye se come yll would haue batayle shewe hym prysysely shal haue bataile right sharpe stronge morow betymes without ony longer delay name god sayde duke philyp se well haue good heed hous madam ye folow right wel noble steppe lygnage wel madame said ye markes trust shal fulfyll message yt ye shall content toke leue florence al hole barony rode forth tyll came king emendus time accompanied iiii kynges also themperour kynges duke erles baron knightes also kynge ionas kyng clamados diuerse noble men pertaining themperour gentyll markes entred place salute king al company sayd syr come fro ladye florence doughter moost noble gentyl lady liuing ryghte derely commendeth vnto grace owne dere fader syr gretely abasshed grete company harneys ye haue brought hyder thys tyme syr grete abasshement noble gentyl mayden se many helmes sheldes shyning ayenst sonne wherfore syr requyreth know pleasure mynde kinge fyerse loke said syr knight wil receyue salutacyon loue herte hope domage bothe body goodes syr said ye markes cause certainly said king hath done shame despyte hath gone awaye fro strauge knyght come hyde self castel ther folyshely kepeth company straunge knight shame euermore also hath done despyte gyuen emperour haue bene wyfe wyl folow wyl therfore bicause shame hath done dooth yet lyke false strupet shall put perpetuall prison thentente shall neuer shame shal hange ribawde knight necke caused thus despyte hathe done shal wyll neuer departe hen tyll haue brought castel downe harde earth tha noble markes answered said syr touching shame ye lay ayenst lady cominge thys castell shall answere syr lady great noblenesse honour quene called ryghte mode wherfore right yt tyme go se owne coutre take pleasure syr departed without lycence fere doubte emperour whome ye haue gyuen ayenst wil herte doubted lest wold haue ayenst wyll therefore mayster clergy made abused churche dore syr came hider simply yt ought blamed brought wt duke phylyp tharchebysshop wel v hondred knightes company syr byshop vncle youre broder wherfore wold loth ony otherwise wel selfe would nedeth fered suche wysedome ca rule selfe wel ynough ther wyser lady againe al world syr also duke phylyp hathe ben alwayes therfore suche people dayly reporte deling knoweth nothing therof yet ther none speketh ny vylany whiche thing syr thinketh ye oughte syr dede yoder good knight arthur though hath retained seruaunt thinke therin hath done wysely haue ye done lettig depart courte floure al chyualry world wysedome hath retayned whan wente courte lefte felaw behind syr haue good knyght retayned vnto suche lady suche habilite may right wel guerdon hym hys seruyce syr come castell despyte yet loue hym ye sore despyse syr bycause ye would gyue suche man neuer loued loue wyll loue longe lyueth without force syr poore lady ye wold giue neuer riche man ayenst wyl yet ye may sure neuer good lyfe longe bytwene bicause emperour would haue loueth therfore come strog castel hath careth neither hym yet yt wold dyspleasure therfore syr take hede ye ye know wel yt ye wold haue clene cotrary destenyed mout perillous natiuyte syr thynge predestynate harde broke syr shal shew ye shal doo fro hen forth leue medlyng ony ferder mater one thing make warant ther company host grete nombre best knyghtes world syr leue mater dele like true king agre promesse ye accorded vnto euer shold haue caplet ymage shoulde lykewyse reioyse lady florence doughter ye haue wryten hande set seale likewise hath done al iiii kynges preset xii peres realme syr ye ayenst owne seale couenaunt ye made lyke kyng thus sende people harneys asse ble ayenst woman fader ayenst doughter vnnatural gret shame dede kynge doo ayenst couenaut promes syr goddes sake forbere doig hurt ayenst owne child ony singuler loue yt ye haue emperour certainly sayd kynge wyll forbere minde tresour worlde shall cause ye knight shal hanged necke put perpetuall pryson wel syr sayd kes begin whan ye wil best ye peraue ture shal ye wold haue neuerthelesse iiii kinges al xii peres al knightes present saye vnto lady florence sendeth word yt meruayleth gretly yt ye come hyder harneys warre ayenst cosidering ye subiectes ryght lady mastres therfore lordes take good hede ye straitly chargeth ye none drawe swerde wepe ayenst none ye promyseth fayth oweth lady eglentine dere mother none degre euer wyl cause hanged necke lyke false traytoure wherefore syrs counsail take hede ye kynge orqueney sayd kynge emendus syr ye cause v haue grete maruayl yt ye haue somoned v come hither harneys make warre agenst natural lady agest promesses writinges seales syr troth man ought go whether eu r ye wyl haue iuste quarrell reason ryght wyl sholde make war agenst ryght ladye whose subiectes men must shal lady iust inheritaunce fayth yt owe god crowne realme orqueney neither none mine shal moue war agenst accord wer al iiii kinges xii peres eche theym sayd wolde neuer bere harneys agenst lady agest promesses made kinge emendus sayd lordes tell ye wyl promyse wyl neuer depart place tyl haue destroyed castel al knightes therin hanged neckes al aunswered said syr pleseth shal gyue lokyng wyl helpe therto none markes sayd themperour syr lady wold fayn know ye thus entred realme suche nubre men war certaynly syr sayd themperoure come hither seke mine owne giuen father denieth wil therfore come hider haue wheder wyl wyl worse wolde false traytour shal hang neck yt rybaude knight kepeth plesure duke philyp saboty also doth sustaine folysshe mynde whan kyng orquen herde themperou menase threte say n uewe duke philyp sayde ye syr emperoure fayre easely ye bringe yt ye shal haue cap hat put hed thoughe yt giue yet deliuered ye wel muse delyu raunce ensure ye get lyghtly ye wene syr knight ye menase hang necke syr gret synne nourisshing coste hym soo syr take morow appointment betwene dedes armes togider elles take part men shal ye ye ca take bind fast hang necke tha shal ye clene suspection betwene florence tha ye may sure shal trespasse syr loue hath broughte hither ye al knight nothing worth wtout ye dedes praysed sit mout horse morowe loue gouerneth lady fayre wolde gladly se giue fa stroke wt sworde loue alway good knightes getteth grace among fayre ladyes therfore syr morow wyn amourous grace wt dede chiualry good faythe ye haue well themperour get ye knyght yt sporteth hi wt ye syr marke wyl lyghtly beget syr within ye wtout rayne shadow abiding sighte thys fayre ladi gret shame therfore put castell get self syr say ye shal asseble made morowe bi faith said suche one wt lady ensure righte swete maketh oftentimes suche knightes copany goodly chaplet sir yet knowledge hath loue paramout syr think ye haue iolly wanton eye therefore syr come se morow shal walles castel shall shewe vnto ca mete wt syr ye haue sene set fete togyther assay ye lepe vp take morow enterprise perour good wil said said themperour syr require let haue batail morow well arthur company came prese b downe flewe knyghtes greate hepes arthur good sword clarece plunged amonge enemy knightes horse suche wyse al fled woulde haue fled fro death none abode hi receiued deth handes clemenson stode styl beheld gret wonder dedes stode lokig arthur encountred knight claue teth clemenson toke dedes gret hardines hym dasht thickest prese syr brisebar folowed far thei enclosed rounde theyr enemy prese great horse slaine vnder greate force taken prysoners led forth feld toward themperor fortune wold hector met sone saw sporred hors wt sporres strake fyrst claue chyn fro thanke howe shall wyl ye haue youre wife husbond ye truly said themperour syr said content therwith shal kyng father wyl sle maye haue vnder rule syr fayth yt owe vnto oure lorde body neuer defouled yonder knight arthur yet wt well fayre lady sayd themperour yf trouth ensure youre father shall hurte parte shal therein syr sayd may trust sore forthinketh yt euer dyd dysplesure ye truely said nubre xxx thousand came emperours tent comforte hym hys losse shewed themperour kyng comyng towarde shal welcome sayd themperour syr sayd proserpine vnder kepynge goddes sake let fader vilany afrayde warrant sayde themperoure king entred pauilyon soone sawe proserpyne wende verely florence doughter sayd thou strumpet art yu nowhere rybaud knight arthur hath kept thus long nowe become thy sauegard trowe thou wenest make thy peace fayth owe vnto crown sorolois thou shalt neuer escape pryson longe lyue thou shalt shame nowe haue syr said themperour goddes sake soo sore dyspleased hath done trespace haue forgyue euer syr shal ye loue mee florence requyre knele downe father cry mercy syr said wt right good wyll kneled downe fader sayd gentyl king dere fader haue mercy forgyue yl wyl kynge stylful feruent yre despyte lyfte vp hys fote strake therwith middes brest ouerthrewe wyde open erth whan themperour sawe ryght sore dyspleased sayd syr kynge ye haue done grete vilany assured shold ledde forthe tent themperour toke armes said syr kynge holde styll fayth owe myn empyre yf ye set handes ony ye shalbe enemyes togyder euermore kynge dyspleased lyft vp hande gaue grete blow two vnder cheke stode themperours armes themperour sayd stryke ye praier betwene mine armes keping faythe owe vnto god sore greueth therwith toke swerde hande gaue king puissaunt stroke kyng drew swerde gaue agayne themperour grete stroke kynge company assayled themperour themperyence ran king ther well nombre xxx thousande bothe party began amonge grete battaile fyerse yt ther many slayne aud hurt amonge occasyon batayle bytwene kynge themperour neuer trust said florence prose pyne themperours tent wene amonge remembre well sayd one arthur also wold cause moche hate stryfe amog euer loue verely madame said arthur ye say trouth wel remembred herde one say euer bataile encreased people drewe bothe party whiche tourned grete domage partyes yf iiii kynges ben moche grete payne ieopardy departed theym sodeynly proserpine vanysshed away soo none wi become soone euery man vnarmed themperour departed went waye toward owne countre people comforted hym best theyr power kynge tent trembled yre therwith came hym one emperours duke sayd syr lorde themperour quyreth gi florence youre doughter careth neyther none loues nothing ye haue shall haue defyeth biddeth ware hym nexte cestes wyll come make war shewe hym yf wil come brig self realme shall ease v moche payne duke departed kynge emendus abode styl grete malencoly king valefoude said syr begon great besynes many inconuenietes lyke folow therby therfore syr shal nedeful puruey people best knightes ye gete themperour puissaunt prince hathe many frendes gentle kynge suffre selfe cou seyled profyt honour syr goddes sake leue abusio thus lay syege doughter ayenst owne promesse agrement striue ayest doughters desteny profyte come therby many yll inconuenyentes may ensue therby hath done redy hath appered duke bigor hath receyued deth syr ye wer grete displeasure king orqueney banished v courte also syr ye grete abusyon cornyte ye chirch dore whan ye wede haue maried florence themperour ye falle wt grete mortall warre syr emperour hath lost king ii duke theyr people slayne done bicause ye obstinate ayenst florece desteny therfore syr yet best appease selfe make pea doughter wt good knyght arthur desyre hym aide ayenst emperour one syr fereth yt emperour wold doo domage therfore hath retayned hym suche hys copany bycause moost best knyght worlde lyuynge wherin syr hath done wysely ye may se poyntes thei haue displeased emperour slayne hys men syr doughter owne emperour mortall enemy syr loue ought doughter bere fyersly ayenst enemyes ayenst h r ye loue kyng sayd syr good lord preset time ouercome wyth dyspleasure receyue wordes gree shall aduyse well night morowe shall answere syr ye saye well sayd kynges xii peres kyng vnarmed al lyke wyse table spred euery man sate downe made good chere passed forth time wt kynge tyll tyme go rest phow themperour thus departed dyspleasure defyed kyng wyth mortall warre nexte nyghte folowynge subtyll arte maister steuen al kinges host brought euery man fast slepe meane tyme bytwene kynge themperour loue proserpyne ye haue herde season arthur company castell laughynge hauing good game begynning occasyon stryfe bytwene kinge emperour day thei grete feest ioye tyl time go theyr restes euery man wente therto saue mayster hys doublet bycause weder somwhat hote company duke phylyp brysebar gouernar hector clemenson perdycas played sp rted togider til ver late gouernar war shal haue shortly pea thinke veryly shall haue arthur lorde mayster swete mayster said duke phylyp pray shal al come passe veryly syr se well ye course sterres many meruayles ye planet reneth hath gouernaunce ouer kynge emendus poynt yt yf mighte haue kynge shold lightly haue peace wt hym knowe well planet layde bedde pauylyon fast slepe hys hoost know suche charme yf cast neither none shal awake tyll morowe fayre daye therfore let v go felde bring hyther kynge shall haue pea sone made ye name god said brisebar shame haue fayleth let v go streight waye sayd gouernar aparayled went castell pryuely coude desyre markes kepe gate open tyll retourned whan approched nere tentes maister blew blast ther arose grete storme thycke myste loost clene sight entes therwith euery man waking felde fell fast slepe mayster co pany w nt kynges tent founde hym hys riall bedde fast slepe grete lyghtes waxe brenning hym amonge theim toke hole bedde kyng lyenge bare fayre softely vp castell dyde set downe bedde grete hall palays set foure torch waxe brenning hym soo dyde let hym lye styll mayster sayd wyll retou ne agayn tentes awake king fader shewe hym howe haue king within castel v went faders tent vndyde enchauntement brought vnto faders beddes syde sate hym downe fayre softely abode tyll kynge fader awoke hym selfe mayster sayd syr ye slepe nay sayd kynge ye speketh thus erly syr sowdans senesshal thought veryly grea mocke wherfore al ran armure armed moo v hondred wet castel dyde knocke bete gate watchemen castell dyde crye yr harneys parte enemyes gate tha euery man castel frendes goddes sake yssue castel ye able resyste ayenst power thei ny nombre ye soo requyre yo defed castel wel ye may madame said arthur ye rest pea let v al n hardely mounted horse dyde foure companion nombre xl knightes castel rode gate caused porter set open arthur grete randon dasht ye prese white helde couered al blacke holdyng grete hatche handes laid rounde hym sarasins made hedes armes handes flye felde bet horse sarasyns suche wyse maruayle behold tor gouernar partye bette downe sarasyns grete hepes mayster brys ar syr perdycas dyde valyauntly onye good knightes ought aboue arthur dyd excellently layde rounde hym confounded al euer attayned vnto euery man fledde fro hym said deuyl hel none erthly creature auoyded stretes passed made gret hepes ead knightes florence knightes grete meruayle also florence quene orqueney ladi marga ete blissed dedes sayde lacked lytell prowesse arthur last hec beten downe horse slaine vnder soo enemyes thought haue ledde hym waye prysoner th rwith arthur came thider fury slew moo xv knyghtes remounted hector agayne horse spyte al enemyes dasht agayne prese bette downe euer attayned vnto brys bar mayster dyde ryghte well theyr partes specyally hur made place hym whan florence sawe v knightes valiauntly said vnto suche knyghtes aboute syrs goddes sake ye loue goo helpe rescowe yonder fyue knightes grete comyn bell souned euery man ranne theyr harneys nombre hondred halfe horsebacke iii hondred fote log iackes grete basenettes hedes wt good swerdes gi te aboute longe speres theyr hades entent slee theyr enemyes horse soo thei yssued castel flew many sarasyns within lytle whyle nere dyscomfyted whan sowdan sawe people ouerladen slain caused grete gr sley horne blowen euery herde ranne harneys wer nombre xxx thousand sowdan yonge lusty couragious knyght mounted horse ther none lyke al world goodnes euer mounted backe neded doubt ny man lyuynge force horse man none lykelyhode might resyst ayenst sowda dasht vnto horse sharpe sporres rushte forth though flowen ye aire lyke byrde whan arthur sawe hym co ing desyred gretely haue horse toke great myghty spere ran sowdan brake hys spere might horse horse able haue borne two men armed without payne arthur passed forth course sarasyns enclosed hym rounde aboute drewe good swerde clarence slew hys enemyes wyth nombre thei charged many stroke slew hors vnder lepte fete dyde put hys whyte shelde ore hym clarence hys good swerde cutte among enemy carpenter h hewe chyppes gre tree thei shote bowes turkey wherwyth dyde moche trouble done hys good whyte shelde hadde bene florence sayde loude coude crye saint mary sw te virgin saue defende yonder good kn ght f dauger peryl whan arthur harde voyce hardines encreased maner strength euer courage tha lyghtly lept amonge hys enemyes began deseuer sonder grete flockes sarasyns none approche nere yt receyued death mede laste hector espyed hym saw hat foote wherwith dyspleased grete rage tha haue ben tresour fraunce mounted vp rusht thickest prese th r dyde meruayles wyth handes cutte armes handes legges claue sonder helmes made hedes flye felde bette downe knyghtes horse togyder hepes ther none encoutred withal escaped deth ther came vnto hym mayster syr brisebar syr perdycas xl knightes vpon horsebacke florence company thre hondred fote al layde sarasyns bet downe lyke dogges arthur encountred sowdans broder gaue suche stroke good swerde clare ce claue hym downe sadel whan sarasyns sawe howe sowdan also broder dead slayne thei made suche roring sorow among emperour tent myght well noyse demaunded one shewed hym ye sowdan scarmusshig wyth castell therewyth ther came hym knyght hadde one armes clene striken sayd syr emperour sowda deed broder saladyne also slayne sir ther come vi thynke rather deuylles hell erthly creature haue slayne cofounded specially one among maketh waye euer cometh none hardy dare abyde stroke handes fleeth therfore syr emperour call harneis elles shal slayne emperour sore dyspleased sayd hondred deuylles hell hath brought hider vi knyghtes thus confoundeth people cryed harneis caused horne blowe hoost euery man ran harneys soo anone togyder hondred thousande men arthur hector gouernar ye maister brisebar syr perdycas wer sprent blode sarasyns th slayne quene orqueney daye well aduysed arthur dedes sayde vnto florence madame certaynly thynke yoder knight arthur deme yonder shelde whyte shelde thynke hym hector mayster gouernar syr brysebar madame sayd florence thei blacke ony ynke thus talked thei sawe emperour comyng hondred thousande folowing swete lady mary sayde florence kepe defende nowe yonder knyghtes fere shalbe slayne emperour came thiderwarde faste might grete noyse trompettes tabour horne whan mayster harde came arthur sayd syr haue lytle nombre people abyde yonder emperour tyme haue done al ready sufficient one daye therfore syr let v retourne agayne castel company ryght sore trauayled ye say wel said arthur cause retraite blowen done arthur peple entred castell closed gate drew vp brydge slayne batayle nombre xv thousande sarasyns arthur mounted vp palays florece mette wt dyd helme thanked gretly al company paine labour thei take sake day loked windowes saw themperour beholding dead body sowdan broder xv thousand sarasyns phow truse taken moneth betwene themperour arthur ca ci arthur wi eyther valure trouth ye wold thus haue done first ye sholde haue giuen warninge haue made defyaunce haue giuen certayne day batayle haue taken yf ye myght sir sholde haue bene honour thus awayte chambre thys numbre people nothing knowyng thereof well sayde themperour euer thou art thy tong fayre fyled wolde god ad ye head thine yt lokest blacke syr sayd arthur wolde ye fayne haue hed truly
