one v whan haue slayne al entred wyth castel let v set open gate let r menaunt entre wyll yf wyl come v may go wha wil loke theyr tentes moo deed fewer enemyes shal haue whan florence herde maisters cousaile pl ased ryght wel said tha would shold deuised madame sayde kynge alexander youre grate displeased shal thus ye doughter vnto hye mighty puissaunt kyng also kynge shame people take enemyes closed nette cage rather shold go seke open felde b ners dysplayed ye sa ryght wel sayd florence syr haue done ayenst vylanye trespace case thei become hyder countre hath enclosed castell withoute ny reasonable cause wherfore shame take aduauntage name god madame sayde dolphyn ye saye trouth good polyce warre spye auantage enemy treason case wh rfore let v doo thus deuysed agreed therto sayde duke britayne tyme ynoughe may issue promyse wyll porter kepe gate shall gyue fre entre many wil come without ony daunger goyng tauerne shall behoue theym paye theyr scotte suche shal entre yt shall fynde agayne theyr goyng oute euery knyght dyd laughe newe porter florence enbraced hym sayd myn owne dere lorde father appereth ryght wel ye fyernes arthur sone laste agreed thys counsayle brisebar mounted hys horse rode forth frenshe hoost without castell came syr de la lounde guydynge two togyder dyde conuay nyght al th yr hoost couertly thei coude castell none emperours people espyed theym within castel dyd rest al nyght tyl nere poynt daye lyght harde masse thei ordred al people duke brytayne al company kepte gate entred grete seller vawtes ioynynge thereto kept themselfe priuely close without noyse ket place towne dolphyn another strete erle forest erle mountbelyall corner ye erle neuers erle foys yong kyng malogres mayster steuen arthur brysebar syr de la lounde accompanyed wyth fyue hondred knightes kepte passage palays duke phylyp duke hector wer palays florence al noble men theyr company redy med closed chambres seller vawtes kept themself close noyse makynge themperour kyng ionas accompanyed wyth fyfty thousande men warre came clere toure haue made assaute therto thei founde gate open entred bothe towne castell thought verily frensshe men ben fledde deceyued frensshe men lepte theyr enbusshementes shette faste gate slewe kynge ionas fyftye thousande soo none escaped alyue one emperour taken prysoner capitulo ciiii morning wha kyng ionas saw day begyn spring lept hys bedde made cryed thrughout al host ye eueri shold harne ye entent make assaut clere toure tha king ionas assebled ther togider nobre xv thousande persones came hym knight said syr florece al frenshe men fledde away night priuely gate castel town stondeth wyde ope frensshe men hath left behynde moche bagage ther lodged wt towne whan kyng ionas hard yt neuer great ioye sayd knew well soone thei knew yt would come ayenst durst theyr lyues abyde ony lenger angry wyth nothynge florece shold thus escape v tha caused great horne sowned ther assembled hym horsebacke wel nombre xl thousande great noyse tropettes tabor horne thei rode themperours tente rysen bedde stode without tente wt great plente people aboute hym sone king ionas saw hym alyghted sayde syr ryght sore displesed florece al galautes frauce night priuely fled away sure arthur hath led countre syr please mout horse go ryde castel take possession therof shall ye haue conquest k ng emendus doth come whan come ye shal haue great auautage h shal without fayne lodge felde ye shal ease within towne castel wha themperour harde florece escaped fro nye oute mynde dyspleasure demaunded harneys armed hym dyuerse hym company king ionas thei nombre fyfty thousande themperour rode forth baners dysplayed great noyse trompettes horne tabour came fyrst gate castel emperour sawe foundation grete walles wer ryght hye thicke grete depe dytches ful water gate rychely buylde mighty stronge sharpe cuttinge porte eullesses bright stele also behelde hye mighty toures pyght full waueryng fanes praysed castel moche hys harte would giue againe al gold world said kyng ionas veryly castel pleaseth right well shal make chambre sayd trulyer ware died grete myschefe buryed castell syr sayd kynge ionas ye wyll take vp lodginges thus oftetimes people speketh thing knowe lytle conclusyon shall aduenture emperour loked windowe chefe toure blushe florece paste fyrste gate warde sayde gentil pusel make good chete verily ye haue themperour host wha florence harde say hart trembled fere said swete loue arthur nedeful day yt ye chefe floure al knyghtes swete hart deliuer day emperour yt time themperou e wyth hys l thousande passed gate wardes come chefe palays ye noble free duke britayne rusht n busshe lift vp bridge closed fast gate put sta arde ouer wall gate castel warde caused blowen grisley horne knyghtes lept horse euery syde arthur came chefe dongeo wel mouted horsebacke wel armed cried brytayne saynt malo broched horse wt greate randon dressed hym themperour strake hym rudely spere bare downe emperour horse hepe arthur thoughte haue taken hym myghte prese soo thicke whan arthur saw holde short grete nombre toke clarece good swee e hande cut therwith euer attayned vnto wha kynge alexander hys company saw noble prowesse arthur thei toke grete hardines kynge alexander ran encountred kynge ionas rudely flewe clene ouer horse crope hys legges vpwarde wyth hys fall almost ouerthrowen dolphyn layde swerde man wyt whan sawe kynge ionas make forke legges vpwarde lyfte vp hys swerde strake bitwene legges rudely ryght legge flewe clene felde sayd go thy waye thou doting fole couer thyne arse shame haue thou kynge ionas trod n wyth horse fete emperoure brused wyth hys fal nye thyne backe broken asonder soo la de vnder pyne tree shelde coude st helpe hym selfe al erles lord b auieu syr de la lounde brisebar da ht prese dyde suche valyauntnes armes thei dyde maner enemyes thei lift selfe n hande dyscomfyted bycause faute capytaynes thought haue tourned agayne gate noble duke brytayne ryght sharpely receyued brytons strake heades armes legges specially arthur lt wonder stroke bett downe euer attayned vnto euery man fled hym make shorte processe noble menne dyde moche emperyens wer clen discomfyted slayne endured moche payne labour fyrste great nombre people tune aboute none arthur hys companye vna med toke theyr dyner r tourned palays went sawe lyeng vnder pyne tree emperour hys chine sore brused almoost broken arthur caused hym sayre easely vnarmed made hym borne palays layde fayre goodly chambre appoynted vi knyghtes wayte giue attendauce hym x squye serue hym arthur caused beste surgiens countre brought hele sore hurtes arthur kept emperour honourably man ought kepe suche persone arthur sayd company lordes shall wt yonder grete hoost without thynke yf one knowe themperour taken kyng ionas slayne wyl flee awaye shal escape fro v therefore let euery man giue hys aduyse best ferder done uerely syr sayd mayster steuen counsayle heyght hyest toure thys castel ye set themperoures banner dysp ayed thentent without hoost may se wyl thinke verely ye themperour hath wonne thys place wyl abide styll thinke selfe wel assured syr soone euery man companye hath dyned l v yssue wyth baners dysplayed fighte people wtout gouernour halfe discom yted shall haue noo vertue power ayenst v let v make king alexander oua captayne gouernour king ought gouernr hoost let v soo kyng emendus whan commeth may haue litel euery man sayd howe mayster well aduysed agreed also euery man went dyner whan dyned euery man cryed harnes armed hoost ryght ioyfull whan sawe theyr lordes baner dyspl yed toppe castel kynge alexander arthur ordeyned baner britaine sholde way ward arthur sholde company fader duke britayne nexte batayle sholde erle mount belyal erle neu r therle foys therle forest nere lord beauieu th n dolphin lorde de la lounde syr brisebar laste kynge alexander theyr chefe capytayne mayster steuen company whan noble men thus good ordynaunce theyr baners dysplayed florence behelde well theyr noble hie countenauces praysed muche herte sayd gentyl cou try fraunce ryght noble art thou god kepe therein mayntayn sith thou hast nourysshed vp suche noble company knightes tyme present yssued fyrst oute baner britaine wyth thekered armes al euery good ordynaunce whan empetyens sawe come forthe knewe wel howe themperour kynge ionas bothe slaine taken w abasshed though haue fledde way kinge florypes broder themperoure kynge randalas kinge clamados cosin germayne kyng florypes mounted al theyr horse rode al theyr hoost dydde encourage thyr people kynge florypes called erle yle perdue comaunded ryde ayenst frenche hoost demau de theym people would shew yf demaund batayle haue mondaye nexte folowynge wythout fayle wyll gyue rewse meane space soo erle rode streyght duke brytayne formest bron ryght nobly dyd salute hym whan arthur saw hym made hym ryghte great ioy erle desyred hym wold cause hym speke wt theyr chefe capytayne ar hur brought hym presence kynge alexand r rle dyd hys reuerence saluted hym demaunded kyng entencyon al hys company dyd approche soo nere emperours hoost ce taynely frende sayde kyng ye company entred londe pertaynynge gentyl la florence ye haue wasted exyled al coutry subiects wrongfully wtout ani resonable cause ye haue besiege assalted castell wtout def auce made whe fore riding purpose areyse youre syege dryue oute thys cou ey yf syr therle cause hoost tary urne againe castel king floripes broder themperour desireth truse respit atayle tyl monday next coming h p omyseth deliuer bataile wythout fayle syr al oute hoost sore troubled becau e empe wo e syr se wel yt castel deliuered hym syth se al h redy batalle abiden behind al wote seke hym cer aynly syr kyng emp rour within castel pryson chine hys backe nye broke asonder king ionas dead al tho came syr respite yt ye demaud shal take counsayle behalfe gyue answere king sent al lordes shewed ye requestes kyng florypes desired giue counsaile ye behalfe han duke britaine desyred master giue fyrst aduise master sayd lordes troth yt king floripes cruell prince greatlye red ubted throughout al theperors londe p ople wyll hym themperour selfe syrs ye may wel se bylles great va ful men warre one compani e c theyrs also though themperoure dead yet people wyth captayne long haue wt hem thys kynge floripes therefore counsayle let v gine thys rulety monday syth cometh theyr desyre people ryghte trauayled payne yt haue morning theyr horse also ryghte wery sore chafed sir many knightes people sore wounded may wel take rest pa foure dayes monday euery hors shal wel refresshe syde se wel theyr hoost maner wythout ordenaunce great trouble myssynge theyr emperoure soo shol go point thynke sholde dyscomfyt al sholde haue honour lordes knightes come forth play wt v tournay syr would take great loue pray therof ryght hertely veryly syr kynge malogre shal fayle lytel thing yf please let done morow next syr bertra de name god kynge emendus wil yt shal morow morow wyll make solempnysacyon weddyng arthur doughter florence gouernar iehannet mayster lady margarete fourth day co tent yt tournay done wel kyng alexander shall pleaseth duke goubert syr bertrade copany departed fro kyng wet palays ther thei shewed knyghtes coutre yt thei taken tournay fren e men beholde fourth day ye riage wer nombre vm promised turnay togider one part ayenst frenshe men made auauntes yt thei wold bere erth al frenshe men wynne al horse daye ther greate feest ioye throughout al ye palays tyl nyght euery man went theyr restes tyl next mornynge nexte morning betimes king emedus kinges noble lordes ryse tha king caused arthur apparailed vestu e ryal lyke kyng kyrtel flamig grene like emeraude mantel scarlet furred wt ermynes stode al ye kiges wt freshe lyuely colour byg hyer head tha ony ther hold iii grete lordes rich crowne golde septer royal naked swerde sygnifyeng chefe cha pyo al realme al ye appertaineth crowne soroloys tha ye duke fader beheld hi wel ye water dasht eye ioye se sone great honour tha tharchebisshop redy potificalibus thobseruauce wt great noyse minstralsy arthur rially brought chirche florece apparailed like great quene crowned wt golde quene orqueny wet one syde quene asmaelite side somwhat behind al quenes dutch coutesses lady cam king alexander kig orqueney cosyn led chirche arthur maryed great ioye ther great f est ioy nd bruite made ye none coude scat bicause noyse instrumetes also gouernar abbay germaines apparailed lyke king duke philip dolphin hector al baros mormall ther wedded iehannet wt moche great ioye pleasure also getyl mayster fresshely apparailed lyke ye sone king alwayes free swete hert wt smylyng countenauce gracious clerke aboue al also ryght good valiaut hardy knyght ther king valefounde fader hadde ryght greate ioye whan sawe sonne gentyll gracious also hym syr neuelon syr brysebar syr morant syr rowlande bigor tha maister wedded faire lady margarete wt great ioye triumphe wha weddynge done mouted great courser mantel grene kyng fader hym knightes nobre vc suche noyse minstral befor though world haue riuen asonder wyse came court king emedus also came king gouernar courte wedded wt great ioye myrth ther made gretest ioye feest yt coude deuised ye mayster kept feest syr emery gouernar thabbey germaine arthur kept court ye palays feest endured hole moneth thus arthur laye ye nyght wt gentyll florence night engendred fayre sone kyng alexander dyde holde ouer fonte named alexander name whiche chylde afterwarde emperour ynde constantinoble ye shal playnly frensshe knightes soroloys argence orqueney mormal ismaelyte valefoude sabary dyde tournay togyder wherof arthur gouernar honour capitulo cxiii fourth daye maryage durynge feest duke goubert syr b rtrande syr clemenson syr perdycas went king alexander desyred remembre tournay yt thei enterprysed th wordes arthur came kynge alexander answered sayde fayre lordes goddes name let done morowe dyd sende erles baron knyghtes frauce shewed tournay holden next day wherof great ioye euery man comauded theyr harneys made redy ayenst next morning tidinges sprad ouer al citie ye frensshe men tournay ayenst knyghtes coutre obre x ayenst one frensshe whan arthur vnderstode yt sente gouernar whan come hym drew apart sayd frende morowe shal tourney agaynst men wherfore ought kepe defend wherfore must aduyse v shal se knightes coutry haue gret enuy th se frenche knightes x tymes many people wherfore doubt knightes haue vylany rather dye su yt therfore shal shew shall whan tourney shal morow begon shal come lodgynge pryuely ye shal abide tha wil arme v strau ge harnes thentent sholde knowen tha wil go turney helpe knightes think shal haue grete nede v hector dolphin shal fyrst front yf duke phylyp mayster brysebar shal turney agaynste knightes haue bene fraunce haue righte good chere al remenant care ou e frendes lothe displese theim kepe secrete matter yt man know therof wyl couer ly name god gouernar euery man drew rest day next mornynge betimes euery man rose went herd masse toke wine knightes ran theyr harnes euery side horne trompe began sowne euery strete ye city duke goubert al company wer redy aparailed yssued felde kynge alexander dyd arme hym al company arthur came king emendus wyth hym kyng orqueney arthur said syr knightes coutry x tymes many french knightes syr suche condicyons wyl neuer recu e back die therfo e syr know myndes th se knightes yf thin ouercome seke therfore ca none wise many shall dye quarell syr thinketh ther ore well done yt sholde cause armed v hondred knightes take kepe ye none yl sholde done name god kynge emendus departed arthur desyred toke wt hym syr brysebar syr tercelin n uew shi chambre dore said syr brisebar syr loue take pre counsayle many knightes ayenst oure frenche men se well fa ouer matched wherfore wyl go ayde wherfore wyl haue syr terceli med harneys nye bygnes yt shal take wt hym v hondred knightes w l armed go turnay kepe felde hurt shal done shal know yt ye syr brisebar wil go gouernars lodging priuely wil arm v straunge harneys thentent yt man shal know v wherfore pray dyscouer syr tercelyn armed arthur mur toke wt hi hondred yssued citie wt gr noyse trompetes abouts duke goubert sayd yonder cometh arthur kepe feld thentent shold none outerage frenche men first front duke hector dolphin lord de la ound kynges duke britaine mounted theyr horse beholde holde tourney also thyder came kyng valefound mayster steuen hys son wyth hym v hondred knightes company whan frenche men entred fyelde x part many whan mayster steuen saw said fader syr beholde yonder knightes greate hardynes seyng theyr countenaunces bee nothyng abasshed al soo farre ouermatched arthur wente pryuely thabbey saynt germaines gouernar armed strauge harnes mouted ii grete courser whan frenche men renged hector aduysed wel syr rowland bygor comynge toward hym hector rusht hors encoutred sir rowland rudely yt tombled uer hors tayle kyng emendus sayd duke brytayne syr beginnyng parte dolphyn encountred one frusshe syr de la ound syr morand ouerthrewe bothe earth turney began maruailous fiers frenche knyghtes sore ouer matched wherfore endured muche payn last arthur gouernar came towarde prese al disguysed arthur sayde gouernar syr whan ye se hector bydde hym kepe v ii company wel ware knowe good wyl syr gouernar rode forth fayre softely wha duke philip saw con yng sayd kyng syr beholde yonder comith two strauge knightes semeth theyr comyng afrayd fyrst stroke therwt aproched tournay gouernar shewed arthur syr bertrand turnay fyrst begon also duke gouberte gaue many gret stroke wt sworde wt arthur gouernar stoode styl beheld kinge emendus sayde thynke yonder ii knightes doubte greatly stroke ye syr wisely duke philip therwt gouernar ran sir ber rand b cle e sadel mary sayd kynge wene haue mocked yon er knightes wrongfully shal se sone ech knigh therwt arthur ran duke goubert encountred rudely yt sent bothe horse knight hepe toke sworde layd round confouded al yt euer attayned vnto gouernar behynd pa saynt mary kyng knoweth yonder knightes seme best knyghtes al world syr sayde kyng orqueney yt se arthur yonder withoute felde wolde aye elles playnly tyme arthur broken gret prese espyed phin hector erle mountbelial xxx co pany sore ouerladen e many time duke gouberte horsed new agayne arthur ran hym strake hym ru ely helme soo thereby trau ce hys horse bare hym yelde tyll laste came kynge emendus came selfe againe sayd al deuyl e hell take suche carpenter fyrste brought countrey arthur ore handled prease russhed forth charged swerde knightes suche wise gouernar bet downe al uer whan yt frenche knightes saw yt ii knyghtes helpe dyde nobly toke gret hardines confounded al knightes part sayd let v fle away abide de h wil folow therby fled away euery syde fro king suche copany al yt dyd behold tourney great maruaile dedes ii knightes mayster steuen perceiued play arthur knewe well yt said softely hym selfe gentyl knyght cannest fayle thy frendes ca suffre lenger ye shold endure trauayle mayster blewe suche blast yt rose sodenlye tourney suche myst yt one could scant se tha arthur gouernar departed priuelye could went thabbey germain euery man went lodgi ge sone thei wer vnarmed al french men went king alexaders lodging went ogider kinges court king emendus welcome made ryg te gret est ioye right glad gret prowes lene day king toke kinge alexander hand demaunded hi wha ii knightes nobly dyd tourney part day answered sayd syr tell becom tha kyng enquyred al could tell poynges whan kynge sawe could haue noo knowledge fell sodeynlye greate udye stode soo musyng arthur gouernar came court kynge enbraced demaunded yf knewe thyng twoo knyghtes hadde oone greate prowesse answered knewe nothynge theym wasshed wente dyner dyner sporced theym euery man lyked best kyng emendus sawe knyghtes spor ynge palays remembred two knyghtes demaunded yf body knewe mayster saw kinge ca e ame said fayre softe syr beleue certaynly woo knyghtes ye desyre sore known arthur gouernar kyng ryghte greate ioye wente theym enbraced wyth wepyng eye ioye sayd open audyence yth haue gyuen doughte arthur repente could haue bestowed hym coulde haue beleued haue seene muche noblenes one knyghte haue sene hym day kynge made greate feast oye uayle beholde thus n u feast xv dayes ladyes would returne fraunce wherof florence right sorowfull e dyd soo muche al abode v dayes departed king emendus florence al lordes lady broughte gouernar hannet theyr londe mormall receiued greate ioy honor caried viii dais phowe maryage arthur baron lady frauce returned theyr owne countryes except king alexander king emendus kept styl made vnto grete taryed soo longe tyll florence delyuered fayre son kinge alexander held fon ca cxiiii vii dayes refynysshed frenche lordes ladyes knightes toke theyr leue kyng emendus conuayed ii dayes iourney king emendus florece toke theyr leue duke brytayne al lordes knightes lady damosel florece requyred retourne ye countrey agayn shortly myght sayd wolde gladly haue gone wt sauyng kepyng companye wt kynge fader soo eche kyssed departed arthur gouernar dyd conuey theym lytel waye duke brytayne sayd arthur sonne good sonne thynke alway plese wel noble king emendus arthur promised toke leue duches moder kissed ech weping yen duke duches toke way homeward arthur gouernar returned kyng foud king alexander togyder kyng emendus entreted kynge alexander promysed hym abyde company certayne space abode long gret myrth plesure tyl last noble quene florece brought bed fayre sonne fayre day king alexander arthur gouernar sportynge ryuer syde came messenger rydynge gret pace sayd arthur syr haue brought good tidings syr kinge emendus doth send word yt noble quen florence broughte bed fayre sonne wherfore desyreth come fast ye ye king wil desire king alexander king gouernar hold e wha arthur herd yt righ ioyful said messeger giue forthy tidi ge cii lond soeuer ye louest best haue tha squier thaked hi righ hubly rode forth last came king emendus made right gret ioy wt gret solemy ti chyld brought churche cristened godfather king emendus king alexander king gouernar called alexander coming fro church made suche feast chere reuel wonder behold nothing yt could haue made king emendus ioyful al request god prayes euer florence might haue h yre body borne sucsede realme chyld fa chyld toward world wel fou med byg mighty hys sholdre fayre crosse uddy fresh rose wherof kyng emendus sayde th sygne attayne muche honour de died emperor de constantynoble co red prowes dyuers realmes phow king alexander returned country led wt hym arthur gouernar hector master steuen atye britayne long tyl florence sent arthur becaus father kyng emendus departed e wherfore made gret lamentacion capi cxv whan kynge alexander bene longe season kyng emendus toke leue hym retourned fraunce went wyth hym arthur gouernar hector mayster steuen within whyle departed king emendus grete ioye yt son suche labour toke befor fell seke laye bedde th story sayth laye vii wekes dyed kynge alexander suche went wyth hym rode longe iourneys tyll laste aryued lond brytayn messenger wente duke shewed yt wolde wyth hym monday next comynge whan duke herde neuer ioyefull duke sent al lordes lady hys coutre yt sholde wt ye receyuynge son arthur came wyth hym dyd daye arthur aryued receyued wt gret f est ioye whiche feest endured viii dayes co uayed kynge alexander owne realme nedeth demaunded wh der arthur copany good chere phow arthur set deth kig emedus nd yt crowned kyng soroloys ca cxvi arthur copany grete season wt kyng alexander hadde ryght good chere day sat table came messeger fro lady florence kneled arthur dyd arise went hym receyued letter sent hym fro florence whiche arthur incontinent breke vp therin found myghty kinge emendus dead wherof al copany made right great sorow arthur desyred kynge alexander yt wolde go wt agayne realme soroloys grau ted wt right good herte tha incontinet apparayled departing mounted theyr horse much theyr iourneys yt aryued ye realme sorolois foude florece making right great sorow death kyng fader sone saw lorde arthur herte reuiued suche wise forgat maner halfe sorowe next day corp borne chyrche great solempnite ryally buried appertayned noble prince wtin kynge alexander sayd tyme make purueyauce arthur crownacion sent al kinges duke erles baron knightes squyers al theyr kinne frendes came thyther people wythout nombre tha arthur wyth greate triumphe crowned wyth golde toke homage euery man crownacion feast endured viii dayes euery man makinge greate ioy saue florece styll great sorow death fader great feast ioye euery man made homage arthur theyr kingedomes dukedomes barony theyr landes euery man departed theyr owne countreys euer arthur gouernar hector mayster loued eche helde fast togither none theyr enemy di e neuer approche none vsed theyr lyues great honour loue pea vnion euer bytwene theyr subiectes longe liued neuer none euer moued warre agaynst thus arthur florence reygned greate prosperite rad sore doubted worlde dyd many fayre conquestes coquered died viii realmes diuerse countreys ryche seygnoryes liued longe phere deuysed longe arthur lyued buburied cap cxvii historie recounteth noble arthur lyued xxxii yere tha died quene florence whome loued well dyed sorowe bothe buryed great empnite layde bothe tombe kinge emendus whiche tombe wryte epitaphe lyeth myghty kyng eme dus arthur florence wife ledde good lyfe togyder wer neuer dyspleased eyther wyth gouernar hector mayster made grete sorowe deth arthur yonge alexnader son arthur florence guydyng kynge gouernar hector gentyll mayster steuen afterwarde emperour ynde constantinoble thus endeth hystory valya te knyght arthur son duke brytayne noble lady florence doughter mighty kynge emedus kynge realme soroloys redeth hereth history pray god sende blysse perdurable amen phere endeth hystory arthur lytell brytayne pimprynted london powles churche yeard sygne cocke roberte redborne
